Current Commentary

Recent Active "Quai d'Orsay" Diplomacy

— Lang

In the past few days, the activities of the European aggressor group have been very noteworthy. The Spanish rebels, with the active assistance of international fascist forces, have occupied the important military stronghold of Irun in the north of the country. The Regent of Hungary, Horthy, who had not stepped out of the country since the war, visited Germany and Austria under the guise of "hunting" to establish an anti-Soviet defense line. The reorganization of the Romanian cabinet has been tainted with the colors of the National Socialist Party. The extension of Germany's compulsory military service period allows it to have more than a million troops in peacetime, and there are rumors that the two giants of fascism recently met in Germany. From these facts, the activities of the aggressor group seem to be in a state of general mobilization.

In contrast to the activities of this aggressor group is the active "Quai d'Orsay" diplomacy. Since the establishment of the People's Government, France has become an important pillar of the peace front. In this Spanish civil war, the non-intervention agreement proposed by France is an important tool for maintaining international peace. As French Prime Minister Blum said at the Seine Province Socialist Party Congress on the 6th, "If countries are allowed to compete in supplying arms to both the Spanish government army and the rebels, it will cause endless disasters for the entire European situation, and the conclusion of the non-intervention agreement is to prevent this disaster." Although the non-intervention agreement on the Spanish Civil War was signed only after a long negotiation, the proof of its actual effectiveness will be seen in future facts. However, the conclusion of this agreement has deprived Germany, Italy, and other countries of the excuse to supply arms to the rebels, and at the same time, it has temporarily prevented the expansion of the war on the Iberian Peninsula into a decisive battle between the aggressor front and the peace front of the whole of Europe. The peaceful purpose of "Quai d'Orsay" diplomacy has thus achieved considerable success.

The active scope of "Quai d'Orsay" diplomacy is not limited to passively supporting peace and preventing the expansion of war, but also actively increasing the strength of supporting peace. The most obvious example is the improvement of Franco-Polish relations. A financial and military agreement was signed today, with France lending Poland 225 million francs over five years, part of which will be freely allocated by the Polish government, part of which will be used to purchase raw materials from the Soviet Union, and part of which will be used to purchase military equipment from France to modernize the Polish army and mechanize it. The conclusion of this military-financial agreement can be said to be a major success of recent Quai d'Orsay diplomacy.

The Franco-Polish military-financial agreement has profound significance for historical reasons. We know that Poland's ability to become independent after the war was largely due to French assistance. Therefore, the two countries had a military alliance treaty. However, in 1934, Poland, which was supposed to be France's peripheral force, threw itself into Germany's arms and colluded with the German-Italian group in diplomacy everywhere. Although its alliance treaty with France was not cancelled, the relationship gradually became estranged. At the same time, it adopted a hostile attitude towards France's Eastern European allies, such as Czechoslovakia and the Soviet Union. Poland's diplomatic policy certainly increased the arrogance of the aggressor front. However, recently, Poland felt that there was no good reason to collude with Germany (because even if the aggressor group wins the future war, Poland is in danger of being annexed to the Third Reich). So the relationship with France has improved again. In the middle of last month, French Army Chief of Staff Gamolin first visited Warsaw. Now, General Inspector of the Army Training of Poland, the highest authority, Riz-Smigly, returned the visit to Paris and finally concluded a military-financial agreement to make the military alliance between the two countries more consolidated. Riz-Smigly also assured France that it would abandon its hostile attitude towards Czechoslovakia. At the same time, because part of the French loan is stipulated to be used to purchase Soviet raw materials, the past hostile relations between Poland and the Soviet Union should also be considerably improved. Therefore, the conclusion of this Franco-Polish military-financial agreement not only strengthened France's military strength but also greatly increased the power of the peace front. The significance of this cannot be overstated, and this evolution of the situation is the greatest achievement of the recent active "Quai d'Orsay" diplomacy.

British Ambassador Passes Through Japan and Talks; Britain's Policy Towards the Far East Remains Unchanged; Maintains Economic Interests in China; Anglo-Japanese Alliance is a Thing of the Past; Will Leave Japan for China on the 11th

(Tokyo) The newly appointed British Ambassador to China, Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen, is on his way to China to take office and is staying temporarily at the British Embassy in Tokyo. A special correspondent from the Central News Agency in Tokyo went to the British Embassy to seek an audience and was granted an interview. According to the British Ambassador, the situation in the Far East is now changing. Britain's policy towards the Far East still follows the original system and is no different from before. Although the British Ambassador has a deep understanding of the situation in the East, he is determined to visit the Far East for the first time, so he does not want to make concrete comments on the current situation in the Far East. However, he firmly stated that Britain's greatest interests in China are economic in nature, and trade is the most important. Britain does not want to change its policy but will maintain this interest. Therefore, not only is a peaceful and friendly relationship between China and Britain necessary, but also a peaceful and friendly relationship between Britain and Japan and between China and Japan is considered necessary. The reporter asked whether the London authorities are still willing to work towards peaceful development in China with the cooperation of Japan, as envisioned by British Economic Advisor Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, and the general impression is that Leith-Ross's mission in this regard has largely failed. The British Ambassador smiled and explained to the reporter in detail his several meetings with Leith-Ross before leaving London, saying that when Leith-Ross returned to England, he expressed optimism about the reform of the Chinese currency system, at least. The success of China's currency reform has proven to be amazing, and even Leith-Ross himself, although he has contributed to this major reform, expressed surprise at its success. The Ambassador did not agree with the statement that Leith-Ross's trip was a failure, saying that if there is a possibility of improving the relationship between China, Britain, and Japan, then we should continue to work in this area. Regarding the recent movement to restore the Anglo-Japanese Alliance, the British Ambassador said that he believes that the Anglo-Japanese Alliance is a thing of the past. Britain does not want to unite with any country to oppose other countries. What Britain wants is the same as before, only to maintain friendly relations with all countries in the world. Continuing on, regarding the proposal of some British people to recognize "Manchukuo", the Ambassador firmly declared that the British government's attitude towards this has not changed. The reporter then asked whether Britain was concerned that Japan's gradual expansion of its military power in China, especially in North China, would have a negative impact on British interests. The Ambassador replied that he would have to study the situation closely in the area before he could give a concrete answer to this question but firmly stated that Britain's greatest interests in China are to maintain peace and trade, as he had already said. Therefore, Britain will consider anything that causes turmoil and unrest in any part of China to hinder British interests. Later, when discussing Japan's current policy of promoting its national policy through the "southward advance" policy, the Ambassador humorously said that he is fifty years old and remembers when he was young, someone showed him a map and told him that a certain country wanted to seize certain lands for itself, but so far he feels that this has not become a reality, and that it has caused Britain to worry about the seriousness of the Japanese threat. The British Ambassador is of medium height, with a calm and friendly attitude, polite and courteous, and has the demeanor of an Oriental. He also told the reporter that the British government is not currently planning to move the embassy but intends to move the general office of the embassy from Beiping to Nanjing. He will establish his own base in Nanjing and is willing to stay in Nanjing for half a year each year, and the other half of the year he will live in Beiping, Beidaihe, and travel to other parts of China. The British Ambassador, his wife, son, and two daughters arrived in Yokohama on the 6th and stayed in Tokyo for two hours before going to Nikko with the British Ambassador to Japan, Clive, to spend the weekend. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs hosted a banquet to welcome the British Ambassador on the 8th. Foreign Minister Arita was unable to attend due to illness. The British Ambassador will leave Kobe with his family on the British ship Chitral this Friday and will stay in Shanghai for three or four days before going to Nanjing to present his credentials. (8th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Arita held a luncheon at his official residence at noon on the 8th to welcome the British Ambassador to China, Sir Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen. However, due to Foreign Minister Arita's illness, Vice Minister Horinouchi delivered the welcoming speech. The British Ambassador delivered a speech of thanks. The guests on this day were British Ambassador to Japan Clive, Minister of the Imperial Household Matsudaira, and President of the Anglo-Japanese Association Hayashi Yōsuke. In addition, Ambassador Clive has scheduled a luncheon at his official residence on the afternoon of the 9th to welcome Ambassador Hughe Knatchbull-Hugessen, and has invited Director of the Eurasian Bureau of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Horinouchi and others to accompany them. (8th Allied News Agency Dispatch)

Suma Visits Foreign Minister Zhang; Exchanges Views on the Chengdu Incident; Wu Zexiang Arrives in Nanjing by Plane from Chongqing

(Nanjing) Japanese Consul General Suma arrived in Nanjing on the Eurasian plane on the morning of the 8th. In the afternoon, he went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to meet with Foreign Minister Zhang and talked for two hours, leaving at 6:00 PM. It is reported that they continued to exchange views on the Chengdu Incident. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) It is rumored that the content of Suma's meeting with Foreign Minister Zhang was a preliminary unofficial discussion on the Chengdu case on behalf of Ambassador Kawagoe and that he presented documents related to the matter without involving specific solutions. After returning to the consulate, he immediately telegraphed Kawagoe to report the contents of his conversation with Foreign Minister Zhang and planned to go to Shanghai to meet with him and give a detailed report. After Suma arrives in Shanghai, Kawagoe will enter Nanjing with him within the week and formally negotiate the Chengdu case with Foreign Minister Zhang. (8th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Consul General Suma returned to Nanjing from Shanghai at 7:30 this morning and plans to meet with Foreign Minister Zhang within the day to formally begin negotiations on the Chengdu Incident. Asian Affairs Director Gao Zongwu went to the Japanese Consulate General at 9:30 this morning to arrange the time for Suma's meeting with Zhang. The date for Ambassador Kawagoe's meeting with Minister Zhang will also be decided today. The Ambassador will enter Nanjing in two or three days to conduct concrete negotiations with Minister Zhang. (8th Special Dispatch)

Stimson Publishes New Book; Reveals Far East Crisis; Failure to Invoke Nine-Power Treaty Blamed on Britain; Japan's Interests Lie in Friendship with China

(New York) Former Secretary of State Stimson will publish a new book tomorrow entitled "The Far Eastern Crisis," the main point of which is that it is now difficult for the United States and Japan to reach any agreement on the Manchurian problem because any solution acceptable to Japan will be condemned by China. The book details Stimson's negotiations after the Japanese army occupied Manchuria. First, it states that before the Japanese army occupied Manchuria, the former Japanese Ambassador to the United States, Debuchi, declared to Stimson that American public opinion was "so friendly" to Japan and that he hoped to resolve the immigration issue with the US authorities before retiring. When the Japanese army invaded Manchuria, Stimson criticized Britain for not cooperating with the United States, saying that the United States suffered blows after the US government announced the non-recognition policy. He said that Britain's inability to make a strong statement to Japan at that time made the Japanese believe that Anglo-American cooperation was impossible and allowed Japan to righteously accuse China of disunity and hindering the implementation of treaties. Stimson disclosed the diplomatic process as follows: In February 1932, he intended to advise former British Foreign Secretary Simon to formally take joint action with the United States and invoke the Nine-Power Treaty to deal with Japan, but this action ultimately failed due to Britain's indifference. Finally, Stimson declared that if Japan takes military action in China, it will be enough to prevent it from doing business, and the impact will make it impossible for Japan to balance its budget. For this reason, Japan will eventually realize that its greatest national interests depend on friendship with China, but this is by no means achievable by force. Stimson praised the League of Nations for eliminating wars and preventing Japan from directly annexing Manchuria but believed that the League of Nations Charter and the Treaty of Versailles were integrated, making the League of Nations merely an institution for maintaining the status quo, which he considered a major weakness of the League of Nations. His conclusion predicts that although the relationship between the United States and Japan will inevitably experience ups and downs from time to time, there will be a day when they will restore friendship. (7th National Telegram)

The Third World Power Conference: 3,000 Delegates Gather in Washington

(Washington) The Third World Power Conference opened here today, with over three thousand delegates in attendance. American representatives will explain the development of power in the United States over the past fifty years. Various private industries, chambers of commerce, and engineering groups will hold power exhibitions. The exhibits will encompass a wide range, including detailed models, drawings, electrical light maps, photographs, etc. The Rural Electrification Administration and the Potomac Electric Power Company will exhibit electrical plowing in the vicinity of Washington. The purpose of this conference is to specifically study "National Power Economy." All power-related resources, such as coal, petroleum, gas, and hydropower, will be discussed by representatives from various countries. The organizers are the U.S. government and domestic electric companies. Secretary of State Hull delivered a welcome address to the delegates, stating that if another world war were to occur, civilization would be in danger of destruction. The current peace organizations are extremely weak, and politicians of all countries should bear the responsibility for this. Hull went on to detail the current trend of belligerence among various countries. (National Telegram, 7th)

(Washington) When welcoming the delegates to the Third World Power Conference today, Secretary of State Hull said that a general war is in danger of breaking out uncontrollably, and the civilization of the world may be utterly destroyed as a result. The only hope now lies in governments and people deeply understanding their responsibilities, truly understanding the inevitable consequences, and then being able to avert a great calamity. Dr. Muller, the German acting chairman, said in his reply that he believes the possibility of a European war is now very remote. Europeans have suffered enough from war and will not try it again. (Reuters Telegram, 7th)

Wichita, Kansas, USA. Republican presidential candidate Landon, on Labor Day, delivered a speech to the American Legion, commenting on the development of the situation in which various races in the United States are clashing with each other, and called on the veterans to work together to correct it. The gist of his speech was: "In the past, Christians, Catholics, and Jews worked together in harmony, but now this is not the case. The trend of encouraging racial struggle has gradually emerged and cannot be ignored. The reason for this is mostly that people around the world have been stimulated and lost their normality since the economic panic. Some countries have taken hostile actions against different races, and the United States has also been affected." Regarding the issue of peace, he said, "We have not advocated war, so even if we do our best to reduce the danger of being drawn into the vortex of war, the effect is minimal. Our ancestors came from Europe, so we should prepare everything to do our best to eliminate the disasters of the old continent. In short, we must have a clear head." Russian Newspaper Criticizes German Newspapers' Anti-Russian Propaganda

(Moscow) Regarding the anti-Soviet propaganda of German newspapers, the Moscow News Special Editorial writes:

"The international press has had many opportunities to be deeply convinced that this kind of anti-Soviet news propaganda is by no means a free creation of fascist journalists, but an organized and systematic propaganda of the German Propaganda Ministry. It is precisely under the orders of the German Propaganda Ministry that the German press is fully mobilized to spread inaccurate news about the number of Red Army soldiers.

"These people use the Soviet law of lowering the conscription age as an excuse, but they actually know that this law will never increase the number of Red Army soldiers. The current situation of the Red Army is the same as the news released by the Soviet government and is the same as before. This is known to the whole world. Therefore, the news about the number of Red Army soldiers published in German newspapers is all fabricated and is also deeply known to the global press. The global press can also clearly understand that this kind of anti-Soviet propaganda is used by Germany to cover up its own doubling of military strength."

Referring to the false news broadcast by the German newspapers about the famine in Ukraine, the riots of the people, the conflicts between soldiers and civilians, and the Red Army soldiers and officers disobeying orders, the newspaper said, "Although the German newspapers fabricated this kind of slander, they actually know that there has never been a conflict between the Red Army and the people. On the contrary, the workers of the whole country are extremely fond of and respect the Red Army. The Propaganda Ministry's slander of the Red Army is precisely because the Red Army is a major obstacle to the realization of the German imperialist and militarist aggressive policies.

"Journalists from various countries stationed in Moscow have repeatedly proved the falsehood of the news about the famine in Ukraine broadcast by Germany. They have jointly proved with Soviet newspapers that this year's harvest in Ukraine is by no means lower than last year's, and the harvest in the entire Soviet Union is actually better than last year's, especially in the Odessa province, which the German newspapers claimed had famine riots. Goebbels' fabrication of this lie is obviously to cover up the situation of the daily shortage of food in his own country. There is no doubt about it.

"Regarding the recent public trial of Trotskyist terrorists, the German newspapers also released a lot of rumors, saying that many government officials, Red Army officers, and diplomats were arrested. The ridiculousness of this kind of lie has already been exposed by the Soviet government's official newspaper.

"The German newspapers spread rumors and also adopted a despicable and shameless method, such as falsely claiming that the news was sent by journalists stationed in Soviet cities, but there are actually no German journalists in those cities. This method is also taught by the German Propaganda Ministry, and they sometimes even list a place that does not actually exist on top of the self-made news.

"The German state-run news agency also openly participates in this slander work, and they specifically take the path of instigating national hatred, which is proposed by Hitler in his "Mein Kampf."

"The purpose and method of instigating national animosity can be clearly seen in the current anti-Soviet propaganda and is a characteristic of Germany's consistent policy. Since it is already like this, any advice, protest, or warning to the German press or to the German government that is instigating them will be useless.

"Inaccurate news complicates international relations and increases anxiety and panic. However, the German government's organization and development of this kind of anti-Soviet propaganda is obviously intended to increase the anxiety and panic of the whole world. People who uphold peace all over the world must pay special attention to this continuous anti-Soviet propaganda and must mobilize the public opinion of all countries to fight against it to eliminate this new threat to peace from Berlin." (TASS Telegram, 8th)

Portugal Rebellion: Two Warships and Tax Collection Rebellions; Fortresses Bombard and Surrender; Government Declares Partial Martial Law

Lisbon. The warship Albuquerque and the destroyer Douro, now docked in the Tagus River, suddenly mutinied today, but surrendered after being bombarded by the Almada Fortress. It is generally believed that this is a prelude to a Portuguese rebellion, but the government authorities say that this is an accidental incident and that the country is very peaceful. (National Telegram, 7th)

Lisbon. A part of the sailors of two Portuguese warships rebelled today and seized command of the ships, firing on the Lisbon Fortress, causing a great shock in Lisbon. The land artillery at that time returned fire and hit several shells, and both ships were damaged. During the exchange of fire, several shells fell into the port of Lisbon. The rebels surrendered immediately, and both ships were towed to the Tagus Port. (Reuters Telegram, 8th)

(London) The news of the Portuguese warship rebellion was first transmitted to London by private sources. The telegram only said that two warships bombarded the Lisbon Fortress, and the Fortress also returned fire, but did not mention which country the two ships belonged to. Everyone is very concerned about this news, especially because the telephones to Lisbon cannot be connected. (Reuters Telegram, 8th)

Lisbon. The crew of the Portuguese coast guard ship "Afonso de Albuquerque" and the destroyer "Dão" suddenly mutinied. The government sent troops to suppress them, resulting in six deaths and nine injuries to the crew of the "Afonso de Albuquerque." The government also declared a state of alert afterward, and all troops were not allowed to leave their barracks and should guard all important places to prevent them. The entrances of all agencies have also been heavily guarded by the police. (Havas Telegram, 8th)

Lisbon. As a result of the rebellion of some of the sailors of two Portuguese warships, the Portuguese government has declared a partial martial law. All troops in Lisbon have been ordered not to leave their barracks without authorization, and all important locations have been stationed by troops. All public buildings are now guarded by the police. It was decided that the warships participating in the rebellion were the small gunboat "Afonso Albuquerque" and the destroyer "Douro." After the government received news of the rebellion of the two ships, it quickly took action and ordered the coastal fortresses to prepare for bombardment. Therefore, after the rebels opened the first shot, the fortresses immediately returned fire, and both ships were hit and immediately surrendered. Currently, the two ships have been towed into the Tagus Port. Passengers on the British ships "Asturias" and "Stralethmore" witnessed the thrilling situation during the bombardment. It is reported that the "Stralethmore" avoided entering the Tagus Port when the two sides began to bombard each other. The ship acted quickly, opened its engines, and entered the port from the mouth of the Tagus Sea. The whole of Portugal is now extremely peaceful. (Reuters Telegram, 8th)

(London) The International Coordinating Committee on the issue of non-intervention in the Spanish Civil War is scheduled to hold its first meeting at noon tomorrow. The responsible parties believe that if the committee seeks a compromise between the views held by the United Kingdom, France, and Italy at that time, it will inevitably encounter great difficulties. This is because Italy had previously proposed two reservations: first, to prohibit the people of all countries from providing financial assistance to the two warring parties in Spain; second, to prohibit the people of all countries from holding demonstrations or volunteering to serve in the two warring parties in Spain. In the United Kingdom and France, due to the various principles contained in the democratic system, it is difficult to adopt this radical approach. In addition, former Minister of Justice, Lémeret, Senator of Martinique, a French territory in the North Atlantic, recently sent a letter to Prime Minister Léon Blum, stating that the workers had not followed the words expressed by the Prime Minister during the demonstration held by the Seine branch of the Socialist Party at the Palais de la Mutualité. The workers announced a strike yesterday, which is using pressure on the government's foreign policy. This kind of action is "quite illegal, and can even be called a rebellion." If the striking workers, as rumored, occupy factories, exclude management, and adopt the methods of Soviet communists, freely acting, it is unknown what steps the government intends to take to maintain social tranquility. (Havas dispatch, 8th)

(London) Sir Walter Citrine, General Secretary of the British Trades Union Congress, which is participating in the Trades Union Congress here, delivered a wireless broadcast speech to American labor circles tonight, strongly arguing that the labor movements of various countries are interconnected, and vehemently criticizing dictatorial politics, stating that dictators are not satisfied with eliminating the freedom rights of their own people, and are now using force to oppress democratic countries. Therefore, the British Trades Union Congress has decided to do everything possible to maintain peace in all countries and to protect the democratic system at all costs. Anything that harms the working class of one country will inevitably harm the working class of other countries. The Spanish events are a clear example. Therefore, we should establish closer ties with American labor circles in the future, and sincerely hope that American labor circles will quickly unite with brothers from all countries, regardless of religion or ethnicity, to form an unbreakable connection. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

The Palestine Question: Important Declaration by the British Government; Deploying Troops but Also Preparing for Negotiations; Mixed Reactions from Arabs

(London) The British Colonial Office issued an important declaration today, indicating that the British government will take swift and effective action to curb the disturbances in Palestine. The declaration stated: "After careful observation of the entire situation, the British government feels that it can no longer tolerate the riots and disturbances incited by Arab leaders, attempting to change the British government's policies as a result. More rapid and effective action must be taken now to bring the disturbances to an end as soon as possible. The British government deeply regrets having to implement this decision. The conditions under which Britain accepted the mandate of Palestine stipulated that it was responsible for the welfare of all levels of the people of Palestine. Britain recognizes this responsibility as a trust, and there is no other way than to implement it." The declaration issued by the Colonial Office today is actually related to the communiqué issued by the highest military authorities in Palestine. According to the communiqué, Britain is sending another division of troops to Palestine, increasing its responsibilities. It is intended to entrust this important responsibility to Lieutenant General Dill, the former Director of Military Operations and Intelligence at the War Office. The declaration issued by the Colonial Office today first provides an introduction, briefly describing the events since the disturbances in Palestine in April, and stating that after the riots in Jaffa and other places were quickly quelled, prominent Arabs organized committees and announced a general strike of political significance. The objectives they sought were completely inconsistent with the purpose of the mandate. Furthermore, armed terrorists roamed around, and assassinations and other atrocities spread daily. In addition to British soldiers, airmen, and police officers being attacked by these mobs from time to time, even Jewish and Arab victims were too numerous to count. Attempts to disrupt traffic order were repeatedly made, resulting in significant material losses and severely impacting Palestine's economic situation. In view of the seriousness of the situation, the Palestinian administrative authorities immediately took active measures to protect the lives and property of citizens and to prevent the continuation of the disturbances. The garrison in Palestine has also been increased accordingly. The British authorities have tried their best to be tolerant, in accordance with the British government's desire to protect peace and alleviate the suffering of the people, but political strikes have continued unabated, and riots and guerrilla warfare have been heard from time to time. In short, this situation is tantamount to directly provoking the British authorities in Palestine. The declaration also stated that the Imperial Committee repeatedly issued communiqués, the content of which was published on July 29. The Colonial Secretary repeatedly assured that the Committee intends to investigate the truth of this incident after order is restored in Palestine. The declaration also cited the communiqué issued by the Permanent Mandates Commission of 1930, in which the mandate obligations regarding the two peoples of Palestine, Jewish and Arab, were extremely equal and could not be more in agreement. The declaration continued: "The British government greatly agrees with the meaning of the communiqué of the International Permanent Mandates Commission and is willing to implement an impartial policy towards both the Jewish and Arab peoples, seeking peace and progress for the country they deeply love. British policy is to maintain friendly relations with the Muslim people and gain their trust. Therefore, the actions currently taken are taken out of necessity and are not what we desire. It must be understood that a government, even one responsible for a mandate, cannot change its original policy due to riots and disturbances. However, the British government still hopes that those who are currently disturbing the peace of Palestine will eventually repent, realize that their actions are hindering the real interests of the people at all levels and the welfare of the country, and understand the impartiality of the mandated government, so that the Imperial Committee can come to Palestine to carry out its investigation mission. Finally, it is hoped that the Imperial Committee will make suggestions afterwards, so that this situation of mutual suspicion can be brought to an end, and the tragedies of misunderstanding and turmoil of the past five months can be finally resolved. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

(London) The War Office has recently announced that Lieutenant General Dill will be the commander of the British forces stationed in Palestine. Lieutenant General Dill was the Director of Military Operations and Intelligence at the War Office and is an outstanding talent in the British Army. When the chiefs of staff of England, France, and Belgium held talks on the Locarno Pact issue in April of this year, Britain appointed Lieutenant General Dill as its chief representative. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

(London) Lieutenant General Dill departed this morning for Palestine to take supreme military control of the area. Furthermore, the First Division, which has been ordered to go to Palestine to reinforce the military strength of the area, will depart under the command of Major General Armitage. It is reported that the majority of the division, except for the artillery unit, will be dispatched, with the advance party scheduled to depart on Friday. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

Jerusalem: The British Colonial Office's declaration that Britain will implement coercive measures in Palestine has aroused various reactions among the people here. The Arab Higher Committee has convened an emergency meeting to discuss the current situation. Security is very strict, and the situation is impossible to ascertain, but the general mood here seems to be unstable. On the one hand, there is hope that the Arabs will understand that their situation has attracted worldwide attention and decide to cancel their strike without losing face. On the other hand, there is fear that die-hard elements among the Arabs will engage in incitement and forceful resistance. At the same time, Fuqi, a well-known Arab rebel leader who recently arrived in Palestine from Syria, has been vigorously engaged in propaganda. The most noteworthy of these is Fuqi's mention of the participation of Iraqi and Syrian troops. However, according to reports in the Arab press, Iraqi Foreign Minister General Nuri does not seem to intend to return here to continue mediation. (Reuters dispatch, 8th)

Iraq's Proposal on the Question of Amending the League of Nations Covenant

(Geneva) The Secretariat of the League of Nations, in accordance with the resolution of the League of Nations General Assembly in July of this year, has solicited suggestions from its member states regarding the amendment of the League of Nations Covenant. To date, multiple suggestions from various countries have been received. The Secretariat of the League of Nations has recently received proposals from Iraq and Peru. The Iraqi government's proposal advocates separating the League of Nations Covenant from the various peace treaties concluded in 1919, and argues that the collective security system stipulated in the Covenant should be strengthened through regional agreements. As for the Peruvian government's proposal, it expresses opinions on each article of the League of Nations Covenant, and puts forward multiple amendments on the conditions for joining member states, the reorganization of the Executive Council, and the reform of its election system. In addition, it also advocates abolishing the distinction between permanent treaties and non-permanent treaties. The proposal indicates that the Peruvian government supports strengthening the provisions of Article 10 of the Covenant regarding the protection of territorial integrity, but the actions and implementation of sanctions stipulated in Article 16 should be restricted. Finally, the Peruvian government requests that the method of amending treaties stipulated in Article 19 of the Covenant should be effective if passed by a two-thirds majority of the League of Nations General Assembly. (Havas dispatch, 7th)

Ministry of Finance Orders All Customs Offices to Pay Attention to Civilian Ships and Automobiles Transporting Smuggled Goods

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance instructed the finance departments of various provinces and all customs offices to the effect that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Anti-Smuggling Committee proposed that the government should vigorously suppress smuggling. Although smuggled goods have gradually disappeared from ships on the Yangtze and roads, unscrupulous people are avoiding inspection by transporting smuggled goods inland for sale by small launches or long-distance automobiles. Anti-smuggling agencies in various places have not yet paid universal attention. In addition, current anti-smuggling work often causes difficulties for the transport and sale of legitimate goods to various places, with unwarranted detentions by inspectors. Please find a way to provide relief. Please issue a general order to all anti-smuggling agencies to pay attention to civilian ships, small launches, and highways, and strictly guard against smuggled goods transported by automobiles. At the same time, please ask the inspectors not to arbitrarily cause difficulties for the transport and sale of legitimate goods. The regulations for the inspection of imported goods are very clear on the inspection methods for goods loaded on inland river steamers, civilian ships, automobiles, and trains. These should be earnestly enforced. Inspectors should not arbitrarily cause difficulties for the transport and sale of legitimate goods, causing disturbances. This order is issued. (Special dispatch, 8th)

British King Departs for Austria, Meets Bulgarian King and Yugoslav Regent

Sofia – The British King passed through here today, heading to Vienna. King Boris of Bulgaria warmly welcomed him and personally escorted him to the border before returning. (7th National Telegram)

Sofia – King Edward VIII of Britain, on his way back home, arrived here by train today and was warmly welcomed by the locals. King Boris and Prince Cyril greeted him cordially 50 miles outside the capital. The people who lined the railway tracks cheered enthusiastically. When the train arrived at the Philippopolis station, welcomers presented the King with a bouquet of flowers. After the King alighted, he immediately joined King Boris in a car and drove to Novoselci, twelve miles from the Bulgarian capital, for a luncheon at the Vrana Palace, attended by Queen Anna of Bulgaria. After the banquet, they briefly toured the capital, then took a special train to the Dragoman station on the Bulgarian border. Bulgarian cabinet members and British expatriates enthusiastically bid farewell to the King. (7th Reuters)

Sofia – King Edward VIII of Britain arrived in Bulgaria yesterday by train from Turkey. King Boris personally went to Novoselci on the border to greet him, boarded the train there, and traveled with the British King to Gariche station, where they disembarked and went to the Vrana Palace for a short rest. They then switched to cars and traveled together to the capital, where the British King transferred to a train bound for the capital of Yugoslavia. King Boris, accompanied by Foreign Minister Kálmánov, personally escorted him to the Yugoslav border before returning. (8th Havas)

(London) On July 16th this year, King Edward VIII was traveling near Hyde Park when a man named McMahon suddenly drew a pistol with the intention of assassination. Fortunately, a woman noticed him and knocked the gun to the ground, and the King was not alarmed. McMahon was immediately arrested and imprisoned. He has now been indicted by the court on three charges: (1) carrying a pistol with the intention of endangering the lives of others; (2) drawing a pistol with the intention of disturbing public order; (3) drawing a pistol next to the King with the intention of intimidating the royal carriage. It is now known that the court is scheduled to begin hearing the case tomorrow. (7th Havas)

American Espionage Expert Suggests Implementing a Prevention System to Prevent the Leakage of Military Secrets

(New York) Mason, an international espionage expert and author, delivered a speech here today, urging the United States to adopt an espionage prevention system to counter the countless spies from other countries who come here to probe America’s most important national defense secrets. Mason, who studied espionage during the European War, stated tonight that the naval and land secrets on which American security depends have become public knowledge for the intelligence agencies of various countries due to the lack of an espionage prevention system. The United States spends millions of dollars on national defense, but spends not a penny to protect its most valuable secrets. Therefore, all new inventions related to warships, aircraft, guns, cannons, and poison gas are known to other countries due to carelessness. The world’s major powers all have well-trained espionage prevention systems that can be easily implemented. (7th National Press)

Over Ninety Counties in Guangdong Submit This Year’s Budget to the Ministry of Finance

(Nanjing) The local budget of Guangdong Province has not been prepared and submitted to the central government in accordance with the law. Person in Charge of the Ministry of Civil Service States That the Salary Schedule Does Not Need to Be Revised

(Nanjing) It was previously reported that the outside world believed that the temporary salary schedule for civil and military officials was too divided and the treatment was inconsistent, and hoped to revise it. According to the person in charge of the Ministry of Civil Service, although the official salary schedule is divided into 36 levels for simple recommendation and appointment, appointed officials are divided into three grades. New appointees may start from the lowest level of each grade. Simple recommendations also have the lowest level of each official grade. Those with outstanding performance may be awarded two levels of salary at once. The regulations on performance evaluation, rewards, and punishments also provide for the possibility of advancing two levels. Although the official salary schedule stipulates a large number of levels, there is still room for flexibility in promotion. The original schedule was revised and approved based on the opinions of various central agencies. Now, the salary schedule for police officers has also been changed to be consistent with that of civil officials. If it is revised again, not only will the procedures be complicated and involve many things, but since the original schedule has great flexibility, if one is indeed a talented person, it will take only ten years or so to be promoted from an appointed position to a recommended position, and one can rise level by level. There is no need for thirty or forty years. It seems that there is no need to revise it. The grade differences between the official positions of the National Government, the Five Yuan, and the military officers in the ministries and commissions as stipulated in the original schedule are actually due to the fact that the original schedule was formulated based on the established facts at the time of revision. If the National Government’s column is lowered, it is not allowed by the facts. Raising the column for the Five Yuan and the ministries and commissions is not possible for the country’s finances. The National Government is the highest administrative agency in the country, and it is not excessive to slightly increase the official grades of its civil servants in terms of system. It seems that the current situation can be maintained. Furthermore, according to the Civil Service Performance Evaluation Law and the Performance Evaluation Reward and Punishment Regulations, those who are evaluated as first-class should be promoted. The current official salary schedule has more levels and the grade differences are not large, which allows the majority of civil servants in various agencies to be promoted and receive salary increases. The combined increase is also limited, and it will not affect the budget of each agency. If the number of levels is reduced, then the level salaries will increase accordingly. If no promotions are given every year during the performance evaluation, it will lose the meaning of rewards. If many promotions are given, then the salary increase will be huge. The country is currently facing national difficulties, and there are doubts about whether the country’s financial resources can afford it. Therefore, the implementation of the current official salary schedule does not have any obstacles. (8th Special Telegram)

Chairman Lin Returns to Nanjing, Welcomed by Officials at the Dock

(Nanjing) Chairman Lin, accompanied by Wei Huai, Lü Chao, Chen Xunyong, and others, descended from Jiuhua Mountain to Datong on the morning of the 7th and boarded the Yongsuo warship to return to Nanjing. Because it was late, they stopped overnight in Tong, and set sail at 7:00 AM on the 8th. They arrived at the Xiaguan naval dock at 3:30 PM. In addition to the Metropolitan police and military agencies increasing security along the river, the National Government’s Counselor’s Office sent a band to wait at the dock. The Navy also sent a band and a guard platoon to stand at attention on the gangway. Central government officials who came to the dock to welcome him included Deng Jiayan, Chen Shaokuan, Wang Yongbin, Chen Qicai, and other senior officials from the National Government’s Civil Affairs Office, Military Affairs Office, and Accounting Office, as well as representatives from various agencies, totaling over one hundred people. When the warship approached the center of the river at 3:10 PM, the Ninghai, Haiqi, Haichou, and Haichen warships anchored in the river raised flags and fired 21 guns in salute. At the same time, foreign warships also raised the national flag of China to express their respect. At 3:20 PM, the Yongsuo warship slowly approached the dock, where Chen Haichang personally directed everything. After docking properly at 3:30 PM, the welcoming officials boarded the warship in succession and went to the lounge to pay their respects to the Chairman and offer their greetings. The Chairman shook hands with each of them. At 3:40 PM, the Chairman disembarked, and the officials also left the warship. After disembarking, the Chairman took a car directly back to his private residence to rest. According to what Chairman Lin told reporters before leaving the warship, he was greatly pleased to see that the agricultural harvests along the way were good and the farmers were full of joy. With the peaceful resolution of the situation in Guangxi and the completion of national unification, the Chinese people should now work together with sincerity and unity towards the task of national salvation and survival. Then the future of the country can be celebrated. (8th Central News Agency)

Hunan-Guangdong Economic Cooperation

(Guangzhou) Yu Jichuan, the Director of the Department of Construction of Hunan Province, came to Guangdong and negotiated with the provincial authorities. The results of the economic cooperation between the two provinces are as follows: (1) Exchange product exhibitions will be held in Guangzhou and Changsha. The methods are: A. Investigate export types and prepare venues. B. Reduce or exempt taxes and reduce freight rates to guide production. C. Provincial products will be displayed at the same time. D. Promote sales at low prices. E. The Ministry of Industry will send personnel to Hunan for inspection. F. The Guangdong Provincial Government and the Guangdong Chamber of Commerce will handle the publicity and solicitation of merchants in Guangzhou. G. Hunan and Guangdong should implement the new system of weights and measures within a time limit to unify transactions. (2) After the exhibition, the two provincial governments will discuss exchange promotion and mutual benefit methods for exchangeable products. (3) Promote the sale of Hunan rice. A. All taxes in Hunan and Guangdong will be exempted. B. Railway freight will be reduced by half. C. Encourage merchants to undertake transportation and provide low-interest loans from banks. Yu Jichuan has presented this cooperation plan to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek for review. Also, Yu has completed his mission and is scheduled to take the Yuehan train back to Hunan on the evening of the 8th. (8th Central News Agency)

Legislative Yuan Financial Committee Reviews Two Public Bond Regulations

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan Financial Committee held a meeting on the morning of the 8th to review two public bond proposals. The committee members present were Chen Changheng, Wei Tingsheng, Shi Weihuan, etc. Ma Yinchu chaired the meeting. Tao Changshan, Director of the Public Bond Department of the Ministry of Finance, and others attended the meeting to express their opinions. The results are as follows: (1) The draft regulation on the reorganization of the Guangdong financial public bonds of the 25th year of the Republic of China was resolved to be submitted to Zheng Hongnian, Shi Weihuan, and Xiao Shuyu for preliminary review and to be convened by Zheng Hongnian. (2) The draft regulation on the land reorganization public bonds of Jiangxi Province in the 25th year of the Republic of China was resolved to be revised and passed, and immediately submitted to the Yuan Committee for review. The fixed amount of the public bonds is 3 million yuan, the interest rate is 6%, and the issuance date is set for October 1 this year. It is specifically used to offset the debts guaranteed by Shang Qin. The denomination is divided into three types: 100 yuan, 1,000 yuan, and 10,000 yuan. The actual income is 98%. The principal will be repaid in six years, with the land registration certificate fee collected from the entire province and the land tax increased due to the land reorganization as the fund. The collection agencies in each county will collect and remit the funds to the Fund Management Committee on schedule to pay the principal and interest. The public bonds can also be used to mortgage all taxes in each county. (8th Central News Agency)

Wu Dingchang Talks About the Four-Province Cooperation Projects, Which Must Start From Simple and Clear Steps

(Anqing) Liu Yiyan, the Director of the Construction Department, accompanied Wu Dingchang, the Minister of Industry, to inspect the cooperative undertakings of various counties to Wuhu. Wu returned to Nanjing by turning. He returned to the province from Jiangxin transporting on the morning of the 8th. (8th Special Telegram)

(Nanjing) The reporter recently visited the Minister of Industry, Wu Dingchang, and asked about his recent inspection of the cooperative undertakings in the four provinces and the future improvement plan. According to him, this inspection took a total of seventeen days and covered the four provinces of Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei. In addition to visiting local authorities and visiting industrial and commercial enterprises and the special products of each province, most of the time was spent on on-site inspections in rural areas. However, due to the short time, only a general impression was obtained. The major points are as follows: (1) The cooperative laws and regulations must be unified, and the undertakings should be handled carefully by the local authorities according to local conditions. The central government should provide guidance and necessary assistance. (2) There are seven categories of cooperative business, but the type of business to be handled should be determined according to the needs of the members. According to the inspection, one type must be handled well before the second type is handled. It is not appropriate to force more to be handled. At present, farmers are very eager for credit lending to be used for production purposes. Therefore, how to develop credit lending is indeed a question that the people of the country should study today. (3) The joint organization of cooperatives should be based on its constituent members. Only when the organization of individual cooperatives is sound can it be effective. (4) Cooperative undertakings are organizations to improve the economic life of the people. Therefore, when promoting cooperation, one should always consider the economic life of the people themselves and should not include other meanings in between. (5) Whether the cooperative undertaking is pure and promising depends on whether the cadres who handle the cooperative undertaking in each locality are appropriate. Those who understand things well often lack the moral character to be role models, and those who are generally old and virtuous lack the ability to handle affairs. Therefore, when promoting cooperation, it is hoped that appropriate personnel will be trained. (6) Cooperation is a permanent undertaking. Being eager for success can easily damage the foundation, and once it fails, it will be more difficult to proceed. Now, cooperative undertakings have attracted the attention of people all over the country. According to the inspection, my country’s cooperative undertakings are still in their infancy. It is impossible to talk about this with the general knowledge of farmers. Even finding simple cooperative talents is not easy, let alone involving complexity. Therefore, although we cannot but have this great expectation, we must never make this great expectation want to be realized immediately. We still need to be down-to-earth and start from the four words “simple and clear” and gradually expand. We can naturally achieve success. Therefore, in the future, we still plan to stick to the stable and progressive principle and consult with local authorities to proceed. (8th Central News Agency)

The Yongding River Continues to Fall and the Breaches in the Beida Section Have Been Blocked

(Beiping) The water level of the Yongding River fell to sixteen feet on the 7th and did not change that night. It continued to fall one foot at 9:00 AM on the 8th. As of 8:00 PM in the evening, the water level was measured at fifteen feet. On the morning of the 8th, two breaches suddenly occurred in the Beida section, which quickly became huge holes. The employees and laborers of the section quickly blocked them with burlap sacks, preventing a major disaster. The north and south sections are still being reinforced and repaired as they are filled. The River Affairs Bureau originally scheduled to hold a stabilization ceremony on the 22nd of this month. If the river water falls another four feet within a few days, the ceremony can be held as scheduled. (8th Special Telegram)

Waste Land Reclamation: Key Points for Supervision Measures

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan passed the following key points for supervision measures regarding the implementation of waste land reclamation in various inland provinces and cities at its morning meeting on the 8th: (1) All reclaimable waste land in inland provinces and cities should be implemented in two phases. The first phase covers the twelve provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, Hunan, Sichuan, Guizhou, Henan, Gansu, and Shaanxi, as well as the two cities of Beijing and Shanghai. The second phase covers the six provinces of Shandong, Shanxi, Hebei, Guangdong, Guangxi, and Yunnan, as well as the three cities of Qingdao, Peiping, and Tianjin. (2) For the first-phase provinces and cities, if the survey and reporting of waste land have not been carried out in accordance with the Interim Measures for Clearing Waste Land, or if the information is incomplete, the deadline for reporting is still the end of this year, and reclamation will be implemented from the 26th year onwards. (3) For the second-phase provinces and cities, the deadline for completing the survey and reporting is the end of the 27th year, and reclamation will be implemented from the 28th year onwards. (4) When implementing reclamation, public and private waste land should be handled separately. If the public waste land covers an area of more than 5,000 mu, the county government should report to the provincial government for handling. If it is less than 5,000 mu, the county and city governments are responsible for soliciting reclamation. In cities directly under the Executive Yuan, the city government will handle it. For private waste land, the owners will be urged to reclaim or solicit reclamation. (5) When soliciting reclamation, county and city governments should formulate implementation plans in accordance with the Regulations for Contracting State-Owned Waste Land and its Implementing Rules, as well as the principles of supervising reclamation under the Interim Measures for Clearing Waste Land, and the principles of encouraging and assisting migration for reclamation. These plans should be submitted to the provincial government for review and then forwarded to the Ministries of Interior, Finance, and Industry for record. If reclamation is handled by the provincial government or a city directly under the Executive Yuan, the implementation plan should be sent to the Ministries of Interior, Finance, and Industry for record. (6) If the reclamation of waste land requires the construction of water conservancy and transportation projects, and the expenses are large and there are indeed difficulties, the county and city governments should submit a budget each year, stating the reasons and proposing an engineering plan, and request subsidies from the provincial government. If it is handled by the province or a city directly under the Executive Yuan, it should be submitted to the central government for consideration of subsidies. (7) County and city governments are responsible for urging the owners of private waste land to implement reclamation in accordance with the following regulations. In cities directly under the Executive Yuan, the city government is responsible for urging them. (8) County and city governments should prepare an annual report on the reclamation of waste land each year and submit it to the provincial government for forwarding to the Ministries of Interior, Finance, and Industry for record. If it is handled by the province or a city directly under the Executive Yuan, it should be directly sent to the Ministries of Interior, Finance, and Industry for record. (9) After the county and city governments report on the reclamation of waste land, the provincial government will conduct a preliminary inspection, and the Ministries of Interior, Finance, and Industry will jointly send personnel for a re-inspection. If it is handled by the province or a city directly under the Executive Yuan, the Ministries of Interior, Finance, and Industry will directly send personnel for inspection. (10) The number of mu of public and private waste land reclaimed by each county and city each year should not be less than one-fifth of the total. Those who can increase reclamation by more than two times this limit will be rewarded separately. Those who do not meet the minimum limit will be deemed as neglecting their duties and will be subject to disciplinary action in accordance with the law. (11) In accordance with the provisions of these measures, the reward and punishment matters carried out by each province or city directly under the Executive Yuan should be compiled and sent to the Ministries of Interior, Finance, and Industry for record at the end of each year. The reward and punishment matters carried out by each county and city should be compiled and submitted to the provincial government for review and then forwarded to the Ministries of Interior, Finance, and Industry for record at the end of each year. (12) These measures will be implemented from the date of promulgation. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 8th)

Election Disputes: British Subject Files Suit in Court

(Nanjing) Since the start of the preliminary elections for representatives of the National Assembly, there have been many disputes arising from elections in various places. Voters in various places often file complaints with the National Election Headquarters. In fact, the headquarters does not have the authority to hear lawsuits. According to the provisions of Chapter 7 of the Election Law, in the event of election fraud or other violations of laws and regulations, electors or unsuccessful candidates may file a civil lawsuit with the Higher Court in the locality. For election-related crimes, criminal proceedings may be instituted with the Local Court in the locality in accordance with the Code of Criminal Procedure. However, such lawsuits must be filed within ten days from the date of the election. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 8th)

Yellow River in Shaanzhou Continues to Rise; Flood Prevention on the Yellow River in Shandong is Critical; The Head of the Flood Has Passed Lishengtun and is Approaching Luokou; River Bureau Director Wang Kairu Goes Upstream to Supervise Prevention

Jinan Correspondence: The Yellow River in Shaanzhou, upstream, suddenly rose sharply on the 5th of this month. The water level and flow rate were almost the same as when the Chongzhuang breach occurred last year. On the 6th, the head of the flood had passed Zhongmou. This morning (7th), its highest level had passed Lishengtun, upstream of the Shandong border. It will reach Luokou in the middle reaches tonight. In this environment of a large flood entering the border, according to the water reports from various reaches received by the River Affairs Bureau today (7th), the water level at Lishengtun suddenly rose by more than 1.3 chi from the night of the 6th to 10:00 a.m. on the 7th. Guanzhuang and Luokou in the middle reaches have also seen increases under the high pressure of the upstream water. There have been no significant changes in the water level at Xiezhiwan and Damajia downstream. However, today (7th), the River Affairs Bureau continued to receive a telegram from Kong Xiangrong, Chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, stating that he had just received a telegram from Longmen, stating that the water level at Longmen reached 91.23 meters on the 4th of this month, and the flow rate in Shaanzhou below increased to 17,700 cubic meters per second. On the 6th, the water level at Longmen continued to rise to 92.01 meters. It is expected that today (7th) the flow rate in Shaanzhou and below will inevitably be higher than before. The telegram ordered all on-site personnel along the river to continue their efforts, guard day and night, and not slacken in the slightest. Wang Kairu, Director of the Shandong Provincial River Affairs Bureau, went upstream to supervise prevention early on the 6th after the water rose in Shaanzhou. Today (7th), he had driven to Dongzhuang. After receiving the telegram from the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, he reported to Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government. In view of the continuous rise of water in the Longmen and Shaanzhou areas upstream of the Yellow River, which will soon reach Shandong, and that the flood prevention along the river has reached a critical stage, for the sake of caution, and to decide on flood prevention at Dongzhuang, he telegraphed Han to urge the magistrates of the counties along the river to quickly mobilize laborers to the dikes to guard day and night, hoping to ensure safety. At the same time, he telegraphed the two general section chiefs, the ten section chiefs, the five dike chiefs of the Dike Works Bureau, and the flood prevention personnel along the river upstream to supervise their subordinates and strictly guard against the situation to get through this critical juncture.

Water Levels in Various Reaches of the Yellow River in Shandong Province

At 6:00 p.m. today (7th), Pan Jianfen, Chief of the Engineering Section of the River Affairs Bureau (who set off at the same time as Wang Kairu), said in a telephone call that the water in the Longmen and Shaanzhou areas had stopped rising. Kong Xiangrong has returned to Kaifeng and is scheduled to come to Jinan on the 9th to attend the sixth anniversary commemoration and encouragement meeting of the Provincial Government. As of 6:00 p.m. on the 7th, the water levels in various reaches of this province were as follows: Lishengtun upstream rose a total of 1.3 chi for the whole day, with a water level of 58.7 meters; Guanzhuang in the middle reaches rose 3 cun, with a water level of 35.76 meters; Luokou rose 1.8 cun, with a water level of 30.07 meters; Xiezhiwan downstream had a normal water level of 18.93 meters; Damajia fell 1 cun, with a water level of 14.55 meters. Attached below are the texts of various cables and documents.

Total River Alert as Head of Flood Enters Shandong

To: All County Magistrates, General and Subdivision Chiefs, Flood Prevention Personnel, and Dike Chiefs of the Five Dike Works Bureau Upstream. Comply with the telegram from the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, which stated that the water level at Longmen increased to 92.01 meters at 6:00 a.m. today. The water level at Longmen on the 4th was 91.23 meters. The flow rate in Shaan County on the day of the decision reached 17,700 cubic meters per second. Now that the water level at Longmen is higher than before, Shaan County will inevitably continue to rise. Order all to comply, supervise the soldiers and laborers to strictly guard and prevent danger, and ensure safety. Director Wang Kairu, seal.

Head of Rising Water Approaching Luokou

To: All County Magistrates, General and Subdivision Chiefs, Flood Prevention Personnel, and Dike Chiefs of the Five Dike Works Bureau Upstream. It has been found that the water from the rise in Shaanzhou is now reported to be approaching Luokou. The water level at Lishengtun has reached 58.6 meters. Tonight and early tomorrow morning will be a critical moment. Order all to comply, supervise the soldiers and laborers to intensify patrols, carefully protect, and not be negligent. Director Wang Kairu, seal.

Dongzhuang Reports Rise and Day and Night Defense

To: All County Magistrates, General and Subdivision Chiefs, Flood Prevention Personnel, and Civil Dike Chiefs. It has just been reported that the river water at Dongzhuang has risen continuously. From 12:00 p.m. yesterday to 5:00 a.m. today, it rose a total of 9.5 cun, and the water level has reached 58.35 meters. It is still rising sharply. Flood prevention is very tense. Order all to supervise employees, regardless of day and night, to strictly guard and prevent danger, and not be negligent. This is of utmost importance. Director Wang Kairu, seal.

County Magistrates of Various Counties Go to the Dike for Joint Defense

To: Han Jun, Chairman of the Jinan Provincial Government. The Yu You telegram. I hope you are aware. It has just been reported that the river water at Dongzhuang has risen continuously, reaching 58.35 meters by 5:00 a.m. today, and is still rising sharply. Flood prevention in various works is suddenly tense. In addition to telegraphing the counties and sections along the river to strictly guard, I beg you to urgently urge the county magistrates to quickly mobilize laborers to the dikes for flood prevention to avoid negligence. With all sincerity, Wang Kairu, seal.

Wang Kairu Telegram to Han Reporting on Engineering Situation

To: Han Jun, Chairman of the Jinan Provincial Government. The Yang Mao telegram. I hope you are aware. I arrived at Dongzhuang at 10:00 a.m. today to observe that the river water is still rising. From 5:00 a.m. to 10:00 a.m., it rose another 2.5 cun, with a water level of 58.6 meters. The engineering situation is still stable. In addition to supervising the employees to work hard to prevent danger and not be negligent in the slightest, I respectfully report this. Wang Kairu, seal at Dongzhuang's flood prevention works.

Shaanxi Water Continues to Rise, Flood Prevention is Very Tight

To: Director Wang of the Shandong River Affairs Bureau. It has just been reported that the water level at Longmen at 6:00 a.m. today was 92.01 meters. The water level at Longmen on the 4th was 91.23 meters. The flow rate in Shaan County on the day of the decision reached 17,700. Now that the water level at Longmen is higher than before, Shaan County will inevitably continue to rise.
