Kong Xiangrong, Chairman of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, seal.

Bandits Rampant in Various Counties in Southern Jiangxi; Forts Are Often Captured; Many Innocent People Are Killed

Nanchang Correspondence: In the past, the scourge of bandits in Jiangxi spread throughout the province. The Central Government devoted its full efforts and several years of effort to suppress the Red Bandits, who threatened the nation and the people. However, since Zhu and Mao fled westward, although the large forces have been pacified, there are still sporadic small groups everywhere. The most rampant are the remnants of Fang Shao and the Huang Ligui gang, who harass the border areas of Wuyuan, Dechang, and Fuliang, and spread to Xiuning and Kaihua. The remnants of Xu Yangang and Gao Yongsheng are hiding in the mountains around Xiuwu and Tongyi. A few days ago, 400-500 people disturbed the Jiangxi-Hunan Road and captured the station personnel at Shinao Weir on the Gaoshang section. Another group attempted to enter Fengxin City. Fortunately, the county had early warnings, and the city gates were tightly closed, so the bandits did not succeed. The counties of Fengjing and Gao are now holding a joint meeting for suppression in Yifeng. As for the southern Jiangxi area, scattered bandits in Chongyi, Shangyou, Xinfeng, Yudu, and Xunwu are hiding in the mountains and appearing and disappearing unpredictably. Previously, because the 1st Army of Guangdong, led by Yu Hanmou, suppressed them with a large army, the remnants of the bandits began to retreat slightly. Now that the Guangdong army has returned to Guangdong, the scattered bandits in Chongyou and Xinyu counties have become active again. At the end of last month, when Li Dezhao, a member of the provincial government, patrolled from Ganzhou to Dayu, the bandits in Chijiang fought fiercely with the police, and traffic was cut off, so he turned back halfway. The forts guarded by the Xinfeng four-village militia are often attacked and captured by bandits, and many innocent people are brutally killed. If this continues, it is feared that it will spread like wildfire. The provincial government has now sent Deputy Security Director Liao Shiqiao, Security Team Leader Lai Weiying, and his Chief of Staff Xiong Bin to various places in southern and western Jiangxi to supervise the suppression. (9, 5)

Epidemic Spreading in Anhui Province; Ministry of Health Sends Personnel for Prevention and Control

Wuhu Correspondence: This year, Anhui Province has had a full harvest of various agricultural products, and the recovery of farmers is celebrated, and the commercial market is active. Unexpectedly, an epidemic broke out in the inner counties after autumn, and deaths followed one after another. Recently, due to the improper weather, the epidemic has become even more rampant. The places where it has occurred include the counties of Chaoxian, Dangtu, Nanling, and Guichi in the central and southern regions, with Chaoxian having the widest and fastest spread. In various villages and towns in the fourth district of the county, more than 200 people have died from the epidemic in the past ten days. The symptoms are headache, inability to speak, followed by vomiting and diarrhea, and death within two or three days. In the jurisdiction of the third district, not only have human disasters not ended, but also six animals such as pigs and cattle have suffered from yellow diarrhea, causing plague. The place where the epidemic has occurred in Guichi is in Guanqian Town in the second district. Every household in the town is suffering from diseases such as malaria, cholera, and typhoid fever, and deaths from the epidemic are heard every day. Although the local government has established epidemic prevention and medicine distribution centers, and hired medical professionals to specialize in diagnosis, the area is too large, and assistance is difficult to provide, so the infection is still severe. There are more deaths among children. According to reports, all these places are remote areas, and medical facilities are extremely lacking, and the villagers are confused by superstition, which has delayed treatment. In view of this, the Ministry of Health has specially sent doctors Feng Rulin and technical student Ying Xihong, etc., to Anhui with a large number of medicines. Since the infection in the countryside of Chaoxian is rapid, they have crossed the river from here and taken the Huainan train to provide relief, and then transferred to other places for prevention and control.

Yongding River Water Level Rises Sharply; Water Level Exceeds Historical High; Leaks Have Been Found in Dikes and Embankments on Both Banks; Danger is Inevitable During the Autumn Flood Season

Peiping Correspondence: The water level of the Yongding River this year has risen sharply due to the impact of the typhoon's northward attack. According to a survey report by the Huiximiao Measurement Institute on the 6th, the water mark has risen to 1 zhang and 9 hua chi, breaking historical records. Many dams have collapsed, and the water is turbulent and dangerous. After hearing the news, all parties paid great attention to it. Although the water receded slightly to 1 zhang and 6 chi by the evening of the 7th, it has not yet escaped the danger period. The reporter made a special trip to the Lugouqiao, an important point of the river, in the afternoon of the 7th to inspect it, and visited Liu Yuful, Director of the River Affairs Bureau, to inquire about everything. The details are recorded as follows:

The western part of Wanping County is Lugouqiao, which is only a mile away, but the sound of the turbulent river water has long entered the ears. The Yongding River is usually only a chi deep, but recently, due to the impact of typhoons and heavy rain, it has suddenly risen to 1 zhang and 9 chi, and the water is mixed with a large amount of yellow sand, small stones, branches, and other debris. The villagers are all extremely frightened and flock to the riverbank to watch. Lugouqiao, which is usually deserted, has become lively due to this. A group of children is using this natural swimming pool to swim and collect branches and other debris from the river. According to the farmers there, when the water was fierce on the 6th, the bridge holes were blocked, and the water surface was about to reach the railway, and the Pinghan traffic was almost interrupted. Fortunately, the water has receded, and the farmers are all celebrating, hoping that the water will not rise again. Liu Yuful said that this year's water level is unprecedented. Because precautions were taken in advance, although leaks were found in various sections, no villages and towns along the coast suffered disasters. Now the water has reached the Sanjiadian area, because the river surface is widened there, so the water is very stable. However, it is still the autumn flood season and has not yet escaped the danger period. It will be safe after another ten days or so if there is no major flow. The reason for the sudden rise in the river water is that the terrain of the San'an River upstream is extremely high, and the flow is very rapid when there is a large amount of water. The provincial government has allocated 20,000 yuan for emergency rescue, and the county magistrates along the coast are supervising the laborers, security teams, and garrison troops to rush to carry out flood prevention work. Liu also said that the Yongding River and the Yellow River are the two major harms in North China, and their treatment is quite difficult. The water flow is sometimes small and sometimes large. When it is small, it is almost dry, and when it is large, it is dangerous. It cannot help with transportation and often causes disasters. The water also contains a large amount of yellow sand and silt. After the water has passed, the silt is deposited on the river bed. In recent years, the river bed has been blocked by silt, resulting in a very shallow river bed, which is also the source of flooding. If you want to dredge the river, it is not only difficult to do, but even if you spend a lot of manpower, money, and time to dredge the river well, it will be blocked by silt again after a large amount of water passes through in the future. It has now been decided to implement a diversion method after the autumn flood this year, opening several branches from the river to allow the silt to enter the branch channels and reduce the amount of silt in the river. This method is being planned. In addition, in order to facilitate management, the River Affairs Bureau has specially divided the north and south banks into eight sections each, and sent personnel to guard them separately. Now that dangerous situations have occurred in the river, each section is reporting dangerous situations by telegram. In the afternoon, it has been forwarded by telegram to the Department of Construction. The original telegram said, "Continuous rain and mountain torrents have broken out. Since the 4th of this month, the river has gradually risen, reaching 64.31 meters yesterday afternoon, breaking recent records. Yesterday evening, we received a phone call from Guanting, stating that the water level at that station had decreased by another 6 chi and 4 cun, which is the same as the water level in the telegram from the North China Water Conservancy Commission. We have reported to you by telegram one after another. Immediately, we telegraphed various counties and contacted the Wanping County Government and the garrison troops nearby to prepare for special emergency rescue. The report from the first section on the south bank stated that the water in the 4th, 5th, 6th, 7th, and 8th numbers of this section has reached the top of the embankment, and there is flooding in many low-lying areas. The report from the sixth section stated that the 54th and 58th dangerous works in this section are all local lateral water hazards, causing the 7th, 8th, 9th, and 10th section dams of the 54th number and the 3rd to 9th section side dams of the 58th number to be flooded, and the soil on the dams has been washed away. A large seepage hole and two small seepage holes have also been found in the 64th number, and water has penetrated outside the dike. The report from the seventh section stated that there are three drilled holes in the middle of the 69th number and one drilled hole at the end of the 74th number. The 13th to 19th and a half sections of the 74th number side dams are uneven, ranging from two or three chi to three or four chi. The report from the first section on this bank stated that the water surface at the place where the dam is located near the Wanping Normal School has increased, and it is only a few inches away from the west wall of the school, which is extremely dangerous. The report from the sixth section stated that six leaks have appeared in the 76th number, two leaks have appeared in the 75th number, and one leak has appeared in the 78th number. The report from the eighth section stated that two drilled holes have appeared in the 92nd number and three drilled holes have appeared in the 98th number. According to the reports from these 5th, 6th, 7th, and 8th sections, the low-lying parts of the dike are mostly level with the water, and they are about to overflow. We have telegraphed each section to lead the officers and soldiers and laborers to add compartments to fill the leaks, chase and compress the sack bags, and rush to pick up the son-in-law embankments, regardless of day and night, to protect the embankments as they see fit, and do their best to defend them."

Songjiang: Investigation of Theft of Military Arms

The sixth squad of the second platoon of the first company of the twelfth Security Brigade of this province was stationed independently in Huan'an Town in Punan, led by its squad leader. Among the soldiers in this squad was a man named Wang Yushi. Recently, a fellow villager, Ding Wenyu, came to borrow travel expenses and was allowed to stay overnight. The next morning, it was discovered that Wang Wangbao's weapon (a Mauser pistol) and Ding Wenyu had both disappeared. The matter was reported to Wu Zongjun, the commander of the second platoon of the brigade, who immediately hired a car and rushed to Punan. In Jinshanwei Town, he spotted Ding Wenyu, the gun thief. He ordered him to stop and searched him, finding a Mauser pistol on his person. The gun's serial number matched that of the one missing from the first company. Ding Wenyu was immediately taken back to headquarters. Under interrogation, he confessed that he was from Heze County, Shandong Province, and was twenty-nine years old. He intended to use the gun to borrow travel expenses from a Mr. Zhang, a wealthy man with a horse shed, to help him return to his hometown. He begged for leniency. After interrogation, Brigade Adjutant Yang, considering that the criminal dared to steal military arms, a truly heinous crime, ordered the relevant department to prepare a formal report and send it to the Third District Headquarters for strict interrogation and legal action.

Wu Boyang Experiences an Unpleasant Taste

The dispute over the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Monument at the Xiyuecheng base in Songjiang, following a ruling by the Supreme Court that the property rights belonged to Wu Boyang, led Wu to obtain permission from the District Court to hire workers to dismantle it on the 25th of last month. Afterwards, Gu Wenshi and Gao Rongqing, the main figures in the construction of the monument pavilion, believing that Wu had defiled the Father of the Nation, immediately requested Lin You堂 to write a complaint and sued Wu in court, asking for him to be punished to the full extent of the law and ordered to rebuild the monument to leave a lasting memorial. It is now known that Wu Boyang believes that Gu and Gao have damaged his reputation and has filed a lawsuit with the District Prosecutor's Office for investigation. The Prosecutor's Office, based on the lawsuit, issued summons yesterday morning at ten o'clock, ordering both the plaintiff and defendant to appear in court for questioning. As a result, Gu Wenbao was released on bail, and the plaintiff was ordered to return home to await further questioning. However, at around ten o'clock in the morning, when Wu Boyang and an elder from his village arrived at the District Prosecutor's Office for questioning, as they passed the courthouse entrance, Gu Wenbao took his own excrement, wrapped it in paper, and taking Wu by surprise, told Wu Guang生 that he wanted to treat him with a snack, and then immediately smeared the excrement on Wu's face, covering him completely, with the stench permeating the air. His family was immediately called by phone and came to help him clean up, but he had already enjoyed a mouthful of osmanthus flavor.

Wuxi: Gold Bar Unearthed in Wood Pulp

In Qian Jinbao's carpentry shop in the Jiantou Longchuanbang area outside the West Gate, a partner named Li Hesheng, while having breakfast outside the back door at seven o'clock yesterday morning, suddenly saw a corner of a golden-yellow object protruding from the soil. Hesheng, seeing this, became suspicious and believed it was a gold bar. He immediately took scissors, dug away the soil, and took it out for inspection. The words "Xin Bao Cheng Yin" were engraved on it. Hesheng weighed it on a scale and found it to be over five taels. It is said that when Hesheng unearthed it, he promised to split it among three or four partners in the shop, but unexpectedly, they left without saying goodbye at noon. The partners are now searching for them separately to negotiate.

Adulterer Kills Paramour with a Knife

Xu Zhian, from Taizhou, made a living as a barge operator, traveling between Wuxi and Shanghai. His wife, Song, was thirty-three years old and from Benniu, Changzhou. She had three daughters. Unfortunately, Zhian died of illness in March of this year. Through an introduction, a peddler named Luo Youcheng became a boat partner. Luo was in his thirties, lived behind the Xifeng Depot near Huangbudun in this county, and had no wife. Soon, he and Xu Song lived together day and night. Before long, a relationship developed, and their feelings deepened, becoming like husband and wife. The matter was discovered by Xu's aunt, Xu Zhu, who scolded them. The other day, Xu Song's barge was loading soybeans from Benniu to Wuxi, stopping at the entrance of the Xinchangyuan Rice Shop in Beitang. Luo Youcheng went to the boat and asked Song to meet him at his home for a tryst. Song did not agree at the time. At around five o'clock in the afternoon, Luo came to the boat again, claiming that he had important matters to discuss and that she had to go. Song had no choice but to take her daughter, Jidi, and go with Luo. When they reached a remote area behind Ronghu Village, Luo suddenly pushed Song to the ground, took out a small knife, and stabbed Song three times in the neck. Blood flowed profusely, and she lost consciousness. The murderer, seeing that his goal had been achieved, fled the scene. Afterwards, the head of the neighborhood, Dong Xiuhua, carried the injured person to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. Due to excessive blood loss, her life is feared to be in danger. Upon hearing this, the Fourth and Fifth Precincts of the Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched officers to investigate and pursue the murderer to bring him to justice.

Changzhou: Drug Offender Investigation Bribery Case

Police officer Zhang Bin of the Third Police Station of the First Branch of the Wu County Public Security Bureau previously arrested three drug offenders, Wan Binyi, etc., and seized a small package of drugs. After handing them over to the county, Wan Binyi was sent to the County Hospital for examination. On the sixth day, Zhang Jiaoru, who runs a special training school, visited Wu Huigong, the hospital director, asking for help with Wan Binyi's case, offering 60 yuan in legal tender as a gift. At the time, a note for 30 yuan in silver dollars was written and given to Director Wu. He also asked Yu Zhijian, an affairs clerk in the county government, to ask Xu Chunsheng and Zhang Zirong to intercede once, asking that the case be handled according to precedent, etc. Director Wu immediately reported this to County Magistrate Hou by telephone. County Magistrate sent Wang Yao, the head of the Fourth Section, to investigate, and Zhang Jiaoru and Yu Zhijian were taken into custody. On the seventh day, Xu Chunsheng and others were summoned for questioning. Zhang Jiaoru and Yu Zhijian were ordered to be sent to the hospital for examination. Zhang Zirong and Xu Chunsheng were detained. Wan Binyi was sent back for drug rehabilitation in another case.

Jiangyin: Tragic Collision with Merchant Ship

Fan Zhengqi, a resident of Dongtai County, made a living by operating a boat. The other day, he took 280 yuan in legal tender to Wuxi to buy wheat. While passing through Jiangyin, at around seven o'clock in the afternoon of the sixth day, the boat was sailing near Huangtiangang when it was suddenly struck by a black foreign merchant ship, causing the boat to sink. All six people on board fell into the river. Two of Fan's daughters drowned. The remaining six were rescued by the Jiangyin Sub-Customs Office and were able to survive.

Nantong: Organizing the Northern Jiangsu Cotton Association

More than seventy representatives of cotton merchants from various counties in northern Jiangsu Province met in Nantong. Under the chairmanship of Wu Xucheng, they resolved to organize the Northern Jiangsu Cotton Industry Association. Representatives from each county elected Wu Xuxian, Zhang Tongwu, Li Yinong, and fifteen others as executive committee members. They discussed important issues: (1) Regarding the collection of commissions, they agreed to act in unison and resolved to hand the matter over to the executive committee. (2) Regarding the Cotton Improvement Office's levy of improvement fees, one dime per stone of cotton, they expressed extreme support for the improvement, but resolved that the government should find other ways to raise the improvement fees and decided to send representatives to visit Commissioner Ge, who also heads the Cotton Improvement Office, to petition.

Zhenjiang: County Land Administration Bureau Illegally Collects Land Price Tax

Citizens Wu Dilou and others submitted a petition to the Provincial Land Administration Bureau requesting correction and cessation of the County Land Administration Bureau's illegal collection of land price tax. The original petition stated: "Petition regarding the Zhenjiang County Land Administration Bureau's illegal collection of land tax, requesting investigation and determination according to Article 3 of the Land Law Implementation Act. It is observed that the Land Law Implementation Act was implemented on March 1, 1936. Article 3 states: 'In areas where the Land Law is implemented, land administration matters that have been carried out before the implementation shall be submitted to the Central Land Administration Authority for determination according to law. Those that are deemed non-compliant shall be ordered to be corrected or stopped.' This means that if there are non-compliant matters in the land administration bureau, the higher-level authority shall determine according to the law. Now, when the Land Law Implementation Act is implemented, your bureau seems to have determined the land administration matters of the said bureau according to the law, and ordered those deemed non-compliant to be corrected or stopped, in order to demonstrate the spirit of the rule of law. Please bring to your bureau the various illegal acts of the said bureau for your review: (1) Illegal zoning; (2) Illegal valuation; (3) Illegal increases; (4) Illegal double taxation; (5) Illegal collection period; (6) Illegal surcharge," etc.

Jiaxing: Public Security Bureau to Change Name

The Jiaxing County Government, upon order from the Executive Yuan, will change the County Government's Public Security Section to the Police Bureau and the Public Security Bureaus in each district will become police stations. The county government is proceeding with the plan. The directors of the joint township construction offices are currently concurrently held by the heads of the public security bureaus in each district. This reorganization may lead to separate appointments, and it is understood that they may be renamed district offices, but this has not yet been determined.

Belgian Minister Ji Youmu Returned to Shanghai Yesterday Morning, Visited Mayor Wu in the Morning to Say Goodbye, Consul-General Hosted a Luncheon, and the Mayor Hosted a Dinner in the Evening

Belgian Minister to China Ji Youmu paid farewell visits to Foreign Minister Zhang and other authorities, staying in Nanjing for one day. After being hosted by Foreign Minister Zhang for dinner the previous night, he took the 11:00 PM express train back to Shanghai with the Counselor of the Embassy and Consul-General to Shanghai Tan Erfu. He arrived in Shanghai at around 7:00 AM yesterday. After getting off at the North Station, he returned to the Huamao Apartment on Baishi Road to rest. Then, at 11:00 AM, he and Tan Erfu drove to the Municipal Government to visit Mayor Wu to say goodbye. The mayor and Secretary Tang Shixuan met him and sent a guard of honor to pay tribute. They talked for 20 minutes before he left. At 12:00 noon, Tan Erfu hosted a luncheon for Ji Youmu at his official residence in the Consulate-General on Lafayet Road, inviting the President of the Belgian Chamber of Commerce, Hailshi, the Director of the Sino-Belgian Bank, Lan Bote, and all members of the consulate to attend. Mayor Wu and his wife also hosted a farewell dinner for Minister Ji and his wife at their private residence on Haige Road at 8:30 PM last night, inviting the Belgian Consul-General, the Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, Zhu Changnian, Yan Nanzhang, and Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun and Secretaries Geng Jiaji and Tang Shixuan and their wives to attend. The party ended at around 10:00 PM. Minister Ji also paid farewell visits to the envoys of various countries in Shanghai these past two days. This afternoon at 5:00 PM, the Sino-Belgian Friendship Association will hold a tea party at the Clement Hotel on Lafayet Road to welcome him. From 6:00 PM to 7:00 PM, Minister Ji himself will host a tea party at the Consul-General's residence to entertain the Belgian community (previously mistakenly reported as entertaining people from all walks of life in China and abroad). Then, at 10:00 AM tomorrow morning, he, his wife, and children will depart on the Zhijiade ship of the Zhaohua Company, departing from China to inspect the Dutch East Indies and the situation of the consulates and overseas Chinese businesses in the Dutch East Indies, and then return home. Minister Ji, believing that the envoys of major countries in China have been promoted, suggested to his government that China and Belgium also promote their ministers to ambassadors to strengthen diplomatic relations. The two governments are currently considering and waiting for the opportunity to realize this. However, it is understood that according to the Belgian diplomatic personnel appointment regulations, all ambassadors must be over 50 years old. Since Minister Ji is not yet 50 years old, he is bound to be restricted by this. After returning home this time, he will no longer return to China to resume his post. Once the promotion is realized, the Belgian government will naturally send another ambassador. Before the new ambassador arrives, the embassy's duties will be temporarily handled by Tan Erfu.

National Assembly Election News from All Circles

Railway Union Begins Nominations

The National Assembly Representative Election Implementation Law stipulates that the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Unions should have one representative. The union had previously been ordered by the Third District Representative Election Office of Jiangsu Province to submit a roster of all members and resumes of officers for review by the Zhenjiang General Office. The union worked overnight to prepare and submit the documents. It also received instructions from the Third District Election Office of Jiangsu Province that the railway union should nominate candidates through the executive staff of each branch. Subsequently, it received instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Election General Office that the election general office had decided to adopt the method of voting by correspondence for the method of nominating candidates by the vocational group of railway employees regarding the officials of their vocational group organization, using the example of the free vocational group nomination, and attached 36 ballots, ordering them to be distributed immediately for nomination, limited to the 10th of September, and the union council will directly send them to the Zhenjiang Election General Office. The railway union is now proceeding in accordance with this order and has begun the election. It is expected that the list of candidates will be submitted to the Zhenjiang Election General Office before the 10th of this month.

Joint Suggestions from Various University Associations

More than twenty presidents of public and private universities in Shanghai held a discussion and dinner the other day, and they all expressed regret that vocational schools nationwide were not allowed to participate in the election of candidates for representatives to the National Assembly, and that it was also inappropriate to mix the teachers' associations of universities with the members of the National Education Association for elections. They specifically suggested that the Ministry of Education revise the National Assembly Representative Election Law. The public document submitted by the association to the Ministry of Education is as follows: "It has recently been seen in the newspapers that, according to the interpretation of the General Office for the Election of National Assembly Representatives, vocational schools are not included in the list of free vocational groups in the professional election. Upon hearing this, everyone was suspicious, and they all believed that vocational schools also belong to higher education, and the term "schools above vocational level" has been commonly used, and they are classified as the same stage as independent colleges and universities. There are dozens of public and private vocational schools across the country, and they should enjoy the same treatment as independent colleges and universities. Furthermore, according to the provisions of Article 18 of the professional election on the number of representatives, according to the attached Table 4, the number of representatives from the educational associations, national universities, independent colleges, and teachers' associations of universities and independent colleges registered by the Ministry of Education is 18. The number of members of the educational associations is in the tens of thousands, which is quite different from the number of teachers in public and private universities and independent colleges. Mixed elections are inappropriate. Teachers from schools above vocational level should elect a certain number of representatives to the National Assembly themselves. We have always looked up to your department for its concern for higher education and teachers' rights. All the reasons for which we request that the National Assembly Representative Election Law be amended have been duly prepared and are hereby submitted to your department for review, and we would be grateful if you would promptly forward it to the General Office for the Election of National Assembly Representatives for their consideration. We are extremely eager to await your response. Respectfully submitted to the Ministry of Education, Shanghai each."

Chamber of Commerce Cables Ministry of Finance, Legal Tender Should Be Accepted Universally, Without Restrictions Based on Place Name on the Bill

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce cabled the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing yesterday, stating: "To the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, It is hereby observed that since the currency reform, the banknotes issued by the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Agricultural Bank of China, and the Farmers Bank of China have been designated as legal tender, regardless of the place name printed on the banknote, as long as it is not a counterfeit, it should be accepted universally in order to achieve the effect of currency unification. According to reports from merchants and citizens in this city, recently, banknotes of the Central Bank of China in Shanghai with the words "Chongqing" printed on them have been rejected by small merchants and tobacco shops in an attempt to gain small profits, which hinders the credibility of legal tender and inconveniences citizens. We hereby cable to you to request that your ministry investigate and promptly instruct the municipal authorities of this city and the provinces and cities to issue a bulletin stating that the legal tender of the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Agricultural Bank of China, and the Farmers Bank of China should be accepted universally regardless of the place name printed on them, in order to emphasize currency unification, which is the common sentiment. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce bows in reverence."

Guangdong Finance Office Successfully Borrows Two Million Yuan from the Bank of Communications and Other Banks, Using Provincial Tobacco and Alcohol Stamp Tax Revenue as Collateral, Each Shanghai Head Office Has Approved the Guangdong Branch to Transfer the Funds

The Xinsheng She reported that Song Ziliang, Special Commissioner of Guangdong and Director of the Finance Office, to reorganize the finances of Guangdong Province, continued to discuss borrowing two million yuan from the Bank of Communications and eight other banks, using the tobacco and alcohol stamp tax revenue as collateral, and has been successful and signed a contract. The details are as follows:

Previous Loan Already Released in Three Installments

At the end of July, the Guangdong Finance Office, to reorganize its finances, borrowed six million yuan from the Central, Bank of Communications, and Three Banks, using the provincial consolidated tax revenue as collateral. After the agreement was reached, the funds were released in four installments. Three installments have already been released, totaling 4.5 million yuan. The fourth installment of 1.5 million yuan is scheduled to be released on September 15th, all directly released by the Guangzhou branches of the above three banks. Before the establishment of the Central Bank branch in Guangzhou, it was entrusted to the Bank of China.

Another Loan of Two Million Yuan Successful

The Guangdong Finance Office is now borrowing another two million yuan from eight banks: the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Shanghai Bank, the Zhongnan Bank, the Jincheng Bank, the Yanye Bank, the China National Products Bank, and the Guohua Bank. After Special Commissioner Song negotiated with the managers of the Guangzhou branches of the above banks, it was agreed that the loan would be secured by the provincial tobacco and alcohol stamp tax revenue, with a monthly interest rate of 0.9% and a term of one year. The branches have applied to their Shanghai head offices for approval and will sign the loan contract immediately.

Each Bank Individually Acknowledges the Loan to be Released by Guangzhou

Each bank acknowledges the amount of the loan: the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications each acknowledge 275,000 yuan, the China National Products Bank 600,000 yuan, the Guohua Bank 200,000 yuan, the Shanghai Bank 250,000 yuan, the Zhongnan Bank 150,000 yuan, and the Yanye Bank and the Jincheng Bank each acknowledge 125,000 yuan, totaling two million yuan. As for the method of releasing the funds, the Guangzhou branches of the above banks will directly release them to the Guangdong Finance Office, University Federation, August 31st.

Before the Implementation of the Transportation and Marketing Regulations, Goods Can Be Purchased

Exemption from Adoption, But Those Suspected of Smuggling Shall Still Be Dealt With in Accordance With Regulations

The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau issued an instruction to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce: "It is hereby decided that in the instruction No. 19891 of the Municipal Government, it is stated that in the consultation No. 46541 of the Ministry of Industry, it is stated that in the consultation No. 28659 of the Ministry of Finance, it is observed that the Ministry has previously distributed the Temporary Regulations on Punishing Smuggling and Tax Evasion and the Temporary Regulations on Inspecting the Transportation and Marketing of Imported Goods to various provinces for reference in order to strictly combat smuggling. Miniature Chinese Family Exhibition to Open, from the 11th to the 30th

The Miniature Chinese Family Exhibition is scheduled to open on the fourth floor of the Daxin Company at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Xizang Road, starting on the 11th of this month. The exhibition features various exquisite models collected by Mr. Zhou of Wuxian County for decades. Everything from halls and pavilions a hundred years ago to chairs and other indoor furnishings are made of rosewood and porcelain. The exquisite carving and high level of skill are rarely seen today, and each is explained and open to the public for viewing until the 30th. It is expected that there will be many visitors at that time. To limit the number of visitors, tickets will be sold for four cents.

Municipal Party and Government Jointly Proclaim to Labor and Management That They Must Not Suspend Business or Strike Without Authorization, and If There Are Any Disputes, They Should Apply for Mediation, and If They Continue to Violate, They Will Be Investigated in Accordance with the Law

The Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters Executive Committee and the Municipal Social Bureau jointly issued Proclamation No. 1105 yesterday, stating: "It is hereby observed that the industry of our country is backward and needs to catch up quickly. Although there are countless ways to revitalize it, the coordination of labor and management is a necessary condition. Therefore, the bureau and the society have repeatedly emphasized the importance of mutual understanding and cooperation to overcome difficulties together. If both labor and management have disagreements due to minor matters and do not apply for mediation or arbitration in accordance with the provisions of the Labor Dispute Handling Law, and suddenly suspend business or strike, such direct actions will not only destroy the industry and hinder livelihoods, but also affect social order and disrupt law and discipline. The bureau and the society have repeatedly declared this to be strictly prohibited. However, this has been ignored for a long time, and recent disputes have gradually increased. A joint proclamation is hereby urgently issued to reiterate the prohibition. The labor and management in this city shall abide by this proclamation. If there are any disputes, they shall first send representatives to directly and peacefully negotiate. If the matter cannot be resolved, they shall apply to the bureau for mediation in accordance with the law. If the factory shuts down or goes out of business without going through the mediation or arbitration process, or if the workers go on strike or work slowly without authorization, once it is verified, they will be investigated in accordance with the law without any leniency. Be careful and do not neglect this important matter. Signed on September 8, 1936, by Executive Director Bai, Pan Gongzhan, and Acting Director Pan Gongzhan."

Du Chongyuan Regained Freedom Yesterday

Mr. Du Chongyuan, the person in charge of the Xinsheng Weekly, was sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment by the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court on July 9 of last year for the crime of obstructing foreign relations. He was sent to prison to serve his sentence. He was detained in Caohejing Prison. Later, due to illness, he requested bail and was transferred to Hongqiao Sanatorium by the Second Branch of the High Court, where he was guarded by police officers from the Public Security Bureau. He was released from prison yesterday upon the expiration of his term. A large number of people went to the hospital to welcome him at 11:00 AM yesterday, but he politely declined. The following is a transcript of his announcement: "Chongyuan's prison term has expired, and he has regained his freedom on September 8. I have been in prison for more than a year, and I am very grateful for the concern of all circles. Due to a slight indisposition, I must go to the countryside for recuperation immediately after my release from prison, and I will not be able to thank you in person. I hereby report this to you and ask for your forgiveness."

This Month's Third Day Hurricane Invasion - Multiple Breaches in the Gaoqiao East Embankment - Zhao Shiqi and Others Request Planning for Prevention - Existing Breaches to be Repaired Imminently

Due to the hurricane invasion on the third day of this month, the Gaoqiao East Embankment suffered multiple breaches and is extremely dangerous. Residents of the area, including Zhao Shiren, are appealing to the Municipal Bureau of Public Works to organize immediate repairs. The appeal states that on the third day of this month, a hurricane swept through Shanghai, and the tide surged violently, causing extensive damage to the East Embankment. The embankment faces in Lier and other sections are almost entirely broken, with successive breaches and water flowing in. Fortunately, the wind direction changed immediately, averting a major disaster. Otherwise, it would have been dire. In light of unpredictable autumn floods and tides, the East Embankment is always at risk of danger. Previously, when under the jurisdiction of Baoshan County, the Gaoqiao Township Office was responsible for hiring laborers to pile up mud bags to address emergencies. Since coming under the administration of the Bureau, a special Embankment Works Management Office was established. If emergency repairs were needed, the Management Office would handle them accordingly. However, the Management Office has now been abolished. With the autumn flood season just beginning, if another hurricane strikes and high tides rage, the existing breaches will not have been repaired. If the already weakened embankment collapses further, how can emergency protection be carried out? Furthermore, the Bureau is far away across the Huangpu River, and transportation will inevitably be disrupted, making it impossible to provide assistance. The degree of danger is such that it may become unmanageable. Citizens, considering this, feel deeply uneasy. They implore the Bureau to promptly plan for prevention, so that there is no panic in emergencies, and the danger can be prevented from escalating. They also request that the existing breaches be repaired imminently to protect the embankment and safeguard the lives of the people.

The Hujia and Sujia Roads are Open to Traffic - Opening Ceremony Scheduled for October 1st - Supplementary Opening Ceremony to be Held

Long-distance buses traveling directly from Huzhou to Suzhou and Jiaxing have been in operation for half a month. There are as many as ten train trips between Shanghai and Suzhou every day. From Shanghai to Suzhou, passengers can transfer to long-distance buses on the Sujia Road to Wujiang, Beita, Pingwang, Zhenze, Nanxun, Huzhou, and from Pingwang to Shengze, Wangjiangjing, Shuangqiao, Jiaxing, etc., all of which can be reached in a short time. The entire route is flat, and the company has thoroughly repaired it. The vehicles are newly built, so they can arrive on time, making them faster than other vehicles. The station staff at each station provides attentive service, and it is very convenient to carry luggage. It is truly the most important route connecting Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. There are eight local buses with sixteen round trips, and more than forty regular buses. Small chartered cars for everyday use and more than twenty large and small stations are all available for telephone calls. In the future, the joint transportation of goods will be actively pursued, which will prove the completeness of the paper weaving of the two roads. We must also invite all transportation bureaus to change the Shanghai-Suzhou long-distance service to a short-distance passenger service. If there are even large towns connected on both sides of the road, there are more than twenty towns such as Shuanglin Wuzhen, Lianshi, Xinshi, Shanzhen, Zhili, Yigao, Linghu, Dibao, Yuanjiahui, Xia'ang, and Luohe. Furthermore, to reach small towns and villages and the Seventy-Two Tower Ports, there are no less than two hundred places. There are also more than one hundred towns in Wuxing West Township, Pi Su Wan Zhe six or seven counties, and the name of the bridge is Shaoxiang Town, and the original towns in the mountains are also available. They can all gather in Huzhou and reach Sujia Hangzhou Shanghai. It is now heard that the two roads are scheduled to hold a supplementary opening ceremony on October 1st, inviting the county governments, public security bureaus, and local business and academic circles of Jiangsu and Zhejiang to participate. The directors of the company, Chen Qinshi, Shen Lianfang, Zhang Xuanchu, Jin Runquan, Zhang Boqi, Zhang Kongxiu, Wang Miaoda, Shen Tianxin, Xu Ziwei, Pang Zanchen, Zhou Jianchu, Zhang Gengchu, Qi Baosheng, Chen Yizhi, Mao Haozhen, Supervisors Zhang Weiru, Chen Shuchen, Chen Zhian, Manager Jin Tanghou, Deputy Manager Zhao Longshan, Jiang Dingzi, Secretary Ling Songru, Section Chief Zheng Shouguang, and Lu Juehou, will be in attendance.

British and American Three Factories - Workers Decide to Resume Work This Morning - Demands Waiting to be Resolved According to Law - Party and Government Agencies Hold Second Mediation

The Dagong News Agency reports that all 2,200 workers of the Third Factory of the British American Tobacco Company (i.e., Yizhong Tobacco Company) on Shutaopeng Road in Shanghai, due to opposing the oppression of workers by Manager Wei Ziqian, triggered a general strike on August 18. In the past ten days, the attitudes of both sides have become increasingly antagonistic. Although the Social Bureau has mediated according to the law, the capitalists have refused to attend, resulting in no resolution. In order to consider the livelihood of the workers and maintain local safety, the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions specially dispatched Standing Committee members Zhou Xuexiang, Zhang Kechang, Ye Xianggao, Lu Muqin, and Hu Menglin, together with the Fourth District Cigarette Industry Union, to Yangshupu at 2:00 p.m. yesterday to convene representatives of workers from various departments of the factory. After giving earnest advice on the current situation, the representatives listened to the advice of the Federation of Trade Unions and expressed their acceptance. They notified all workers in groups overnight and decided to resume work in the factory this morning.

Order to Resume Work

The Municipal Federation of Trade Unions immediately issued Instruction No. 31, stating: "For the purpose of following orders, in the case of the Yizhong Tobacco Factory (i.e., British American Tobacco Company) dismissing workers without reason, causing a strike, the workers have repeatedly presented requests for assistance to the Federation. The Federation feels that the workers have suffered unreasonable oppression, which is truly pitiful. However, at this time of great difficulty and deepening national crisis, the order in the rear should be maintained. In addition to dispatching personnel to give earnest advice, it is urgently ordered that the workers resume work in the near future and wait for the Party and government to resolve the matter. The Federation has high hopes." This order is issued by Chairman Zhu Xuefan, Standing Committee members Zhou Xuexiang, Ye Xiangfu, Zhang Kechang, Li Mengnan, Shao Xubai, and Long Peiyun.

Second Mediation

It is now known that the Party and government agencies of this city, in order to resolve the British and American labor dispute as soon as possible, have specifically scheduled to convene the labor and capital sides for a second mediation at 9:00 a.m. today. If the mediation fails to establish, it will be submitted to the Municipal Government Arbitration Committee for arbitration according to the law.

Suggestions from the Commercial Commissioner to the Dutch East Indies - Key Points for Improving Export Products - Trade Values Were Equal in the Past - Hope that We Can Develop Technically

The economic structures of our country and the Dutch East Indies are almost the same in nature. Therefore, although the possibility of trade development between the two is not great in terms of value, it is also not much in terms of variety. If our country can make considerable progress in technical industry, the industrial manufactured products it can supply to the Dutch East Indies will be more than what it can supply today. The following is a report on Sino-Dutch commercial conditions from Xu Tinglie, our country's Commercial Commissioner to the Dutch East Indies:

Import and Export Comparison The types and amounts of imports and exports of goods between our country and the Dutch East Indies are compared as follows. In 1935, China's important export commodities included: (1) animals and animal products (excluding raw hides, finished hides, leather goods, and fish, shellfish, and marine products), totaling 37,021 tons; (2) raw hides, finished hides, and leather goods, totaling 2.67 holes tons; grains and products, totaling 6,107 tons; (3) oil, none; (4) seeds and kernels, totaling 8,126 tons; (5) tea, totaling 20,392 tons; tobacco, totaling 272,112 tons. The Dutch East Indies' important export commodities included: (1) rubber, totaling 134,000 tons; (2) tea, 14,000 tons; (3) sugar, 18,845,000 tons; (4) tobacco, none; (5) coffee, totaling 26,000 tons; (6) camphor, totaling 161,000 tons; (7) copper skin and copper ore, none; (8) oil and main products, totaling 5,500,000 tons. From the above observations, some of our country's main products exported to the Dutch East Indies may have a monopoly in the Dutch East Indies market, and some have already been introduced to the Dutch East Indies and are expected to successfully monopolize in the future.

Export Improvement The goods that should be improved for our country's exports to the Dutch East Indies include: (1) matches, the quality is inferior to that of Sweden, but better than those made in Japan, and the price is cheaper than European matches, not far from Japanese matches; (2) tea, the quality of our country's non-smoked tea is quite excellent in quality, but the market is extremely limited, our country's smoked flower tea is better than the well-known Taiwanese counterpart, the price of Chinese smoked flower tea competes with Taiwanese smoked flower tea, but is higher than Taiwanese and Dutch East Indies mixed smoked flower tea; (3) unbleached cotton goods, the quality is generally very good, comparable to the better products in Japan, the price is too expensive compared with Japanese goods; (4) colored cotton fabrics, the quality of some is good or just passable, some are too poor, the price is still relatively high compared with Japanese products; (5) silk, the quality is good, but often fades, the price is higher compared with the price of Japanese rayon fabrics and mixed rayon and natural silk fabrics, or rayon and cotton interweaving fabrics; (6) cotton yarn, the quality is good, at least equal to that made by Japan, the value is too high; (7) cement, the quality is good, the value must be competitive under the current limited system; (8) carpets, the quality is good, the price is higher than the average of European machine-made carpets, but lower than the products of Persia and Turkey; (9) ink, the quality of some brands is very good, some are not satisfactory, the price must be competitive; (10) paint, the quality is good, the price must be competitive; (11) flashlight batteries, the quality is good, the price is too high; (12) Shandong manchu silk, the quality is good, the price is still cheap, quite popular.

When Transshipping Taxed Goods - A Permit is Still Required

The New Medicine Association sent a letter to its members yesterday, stating: "Dear Sir/Madam, we have recently received a letter from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, which in turn received a proclamation No. 1541 from the Jianghai Customs, stating: 'The interim regulations for inspecting the transportation and sales of imported goods were announced in proclamation No. 1521 on June 23 of this year. Now, according to the order of the Ministry of Finance, the provisions of Articles 2, 3, and 6 of the aforementioned transportation and sales regulations should be interpreted as follows: For taxed goods (i.e., goods that should apply for a transportation and sales license) that are transported by sea or river from the original port of entry to another port, if they have not obtained a transportation and sales license, they should apply to the Customs (i.e., the Customs of the other port) for a transportation and sales license in accordance with Article 2 of the transportation and sales regulations if they need to be transported to other places for distribution from that other port. If they are transported from the original port of entry to various places by train, inland river vessels, civilian ships, or automobiles and have already obtained a transportation and sales license, they should still be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 6 of the transportation and sales regulations if they need to be transported to other places for distribution. Merchants should be informed accordingly.' Therefore, we have sent a letter to inform you and hope you will take note accordingly."

Dr. Pang Jingzhou Returns Home

Dr. Pang Jingzhou has been serving in the medical education field in Shanghai for many years. Last autumn, he was ordered by the Ministry of Education to go to Europe and the United States for inspection. He returned to China from the United States on the 7th of the previous day. In an interview, he stated: "I took an Italian mail ship abroad on this day last year and traveled to a total of fifteen countries, including Germany, France, Russia, Austria, England, and the United States, for exactly one year. The main task was to investigate the equipment and new trends in modern medical education. I stayed in Germany for a relatively long time, because I had lived in Hamburg to do private research, and I also helped the University of Frankfurt run the folklore museum of the Chinese Academy. During the trip in Europe, except for taking a plane to Moscow, I traveled by car, covering more than 12,000 miles of highway. Therefore, I was able to get a glimpse of the rural facilities of various countries. I arrived in the United States in early July and stayed in New York and Washington. Soon after, I chose to travel east and stopped along the way for sightseeing. In the middle of last month, I finally took the route to the West Xian De Wharf and returned home. I once drafted a book on medical education and travel notes, which are stored in my luggage and will be sorted out and published later."

He repeatedly fought fiercely until his strength was exhausted and aid was cut off. He was captured but unyielding. On May 12 of this year, he sacrificed himself for the country at the age of 73. The government has issued a decree to commend him and ordered the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission and this office to prepare for a memorial service. Gan Yuan, Ding Monong, He Mingzhai, Ma Gongyu, Xiang Peiliang, Liu Haisu, Wang Jiyuan, Zheng Kechang, Xie Haiyan, Ni Yide, Shi Zhongpeng, and Xie Gongzhan attended, with Liu Haisu as the chairman.

Preparatory Committee Members

Liu Haitang, Wang Jiyuan, Ma Gongyu, Xie Gongzhan, Yan Kechang, Jiang Jianbai, Pan Yuliang, Xie Haiyan, Ni Yide, Wu Gonghu, Li Jian, Shi Chongpeng, Xiang Peiliang, Xu Zexiang, Song Banggan, He Mingzhai, Zheng Wuchang, Chen Dabei, Wang Xianyan, Gan Yuan, Liu Yazi, Chen Hecheng, Gu Shusen, Li Haoran, Ding Monong, Zhang Xiaozhou, Lu Fengzi, Zhao Junhao, Hu Shuyi, Ma Chonggan, Jiang Xiangqing, Gao Jianfu, Liu Shi, Chen Shuren, Xia Jiancheng, Wang Yiting, Huang Binhong, Wu Zhongxiong. The outline of the organization and the detailed rules for soliciting products are recorded as follows:

Organization Outline

Article 1: The purpose of this association is to collect fine arts products, hold public exhibitions, promote national culture, cultivate the national spirit, and promote the development of the sanitary undertaking. Article 2: This association is sponsored by the China Fine Arts Association. Article 3: The scope of the exhibition of this association is limited to the following categories: Chinese painting, oil painting, and sculpture. Article 4: The products are divided into special and solicited. Fine arts artists nationwide are welcome to participate (the detailed rules will be set separately). Article 5: The association's affairs are organized by the preparatory committee. The organization is as follows: the preparatory committee has one director, who manages all the association's affairs. It is divided into: 1. General Affairs Group, 2. Solicitation Group, 3. Review Group, 4. Venue Group, 5. Publicity Group. Each group has several group directors, who are appointed by the members of the preparatory committee. When necessary, several staff members may be appointed. Article 6: This association may request the government to assist in the process. Article 7: The association's product review matters are handled by a review committee composed of experts. Article 8: The association's exhibition period is from September 24 to September 30 of this year. Article 9: The association's expenses are covered by members' special donations, product handling fees, and various income from the exhibition. Article 10: The association's exhibition location is set in the painting hall on the fourth floor of the Daxin Company on Nanjing Road, Shanghai. Article 11: The address of the association's preparatory committee is located at the China Fine Arts Association, 45 Aimeiyu Road, Shanghai.

Wuzhou Pharmacy New Building on Fuzhou Road Nearing Completion: Magnificent and Solemn Exterior, Perfect Interior Facilities, Now Moved into Office, Grand Opening Next Month

The new building of Wuzhou Pharmacy Co., Ltd.'s Fuzhou Road main store has been under active construction since its inception and is now nearing completion. The grand opening is scheduled for October 10th, at which time an opening ceremony will be held. The building occupies an area of 13,000 square feet and was designed by Shanghai Tonghe Company. The entire project was contracted by Xin Jin Ji Kang Company. The electrical engineering was contracted by Xingtai Electrical Appliance Company. The elevator engineering was installed by Otis Company. The hot and cold air equipment engineering was installed by the Beiji Company. All sanitary equipment was contracted by Xin Shen Company. Shanghai-based engineer Ji Tai was hired as a consultant. The building has ten floors with a height of more than 130 feet. The exterior is made of powdered talc stone, making it magnificent and solemn. The main entrance is located between Fuzhou Road and Henan Road. Inside the central door is the main hall, which belongs to the business department. It is equipped with air conditioning for both hot and cold temperatures, making it warm in winter and cool in summer. There are two pillars in the hall, both made of a special kind of mica stone, extending directly to the top of the mezzanine floor. The floor is paved with extremely light pink mica stone and inlaid with new-style patterns made of gold copper strips, with well-matched colors, making it extremely artistic. In the hall are stone stairs, leading to the mezzanine. Next to the hall are two doors: the right door leads to the elevator to the upper floors, and the left door leads to the business department, manager's office, and dispatch office, etc. Ascending the steps also leads to various office areas. In the rear is another two-story building, specially prepared for the storage and preparation of goods, with a bridge connecting the various offices on the mezzanine floor, which is very convenient. In the center of the third floor is built the Mr. Song Mao Memorial Hall, built by famous craftsmen from Beiping, making it extremely solemn and luxurious. The purpose of each floor has also been properly allocated. The mezzanine and third floors are used as offices, the second floor as a warehouse, and the fourth floor as clinics for doctors in various departments. The internal facilities are extremely scientific, and the whole house is divided into ten floors, with a total height of more than one hundred and thirty feet. The exterior is made of powder talc stone, magnificent and solemn. The corner of the main entrance is located between Fuzhou Road and Henan Road. The central door leads to the hall, which belongs to the business department, equipped with air conditioning and heating facilities, making it warm in winter and cool in summer. There are two columns in the hall, both made of a different kind of mica stone, extending directly to the mezzanine floor. The ground is paved with extremely light pink mica stone and inlaid with new-style patterns made of gold copper strips, with balanced colors and extremely artistic design. In the hall is a stone staircase leading to the mezzanine. The fifth floor is rented out as offices, and it is said that there have been several requests for rental every day, precisely because of the convenient location and the extremely beautiful equipment. The sixth floor is a dining hall that can accommodate twenty to thirty tables, and all kinds of banquets can be held on that floor. The seventh, eighth, and ninth floors are staff dormitories. The rooftop garden offers a panoramic view of everything and provides a place for staff to rest in the morning and evening. The entire building has ample light and ventilation, which is a distinctive feature. It is reported that the company's head office has now moved in to conduct business.

Ceylon Xuefa Delegation Receives Bhikkhu Ordination: Ordination Platform Set Up in the River, More Than Five Thousand Visitors

The members of the Ceylon Xuefa (Study Dharma) Delegation organized by the Shanghai Chinese Buddhist Association, Hui Song, Xiu Lu, Wei Huan, Wei Zhi, Fa Zhou, and others, set sail in April of this year.

Ceylon Xuefa Delegation

Goes Directly to Ceylon

To study Southern Buddhism and other matters, as reported in the newspapers. After the delegation arrived in Ceylon, they were warmly welcomed by the local people. On the Buddha's Birthday in May of this year, they first received the novice monk ordination. Thousands of people attended the ceremony, a rare event in history. Their teacher specially bestowed upon them Dharma names, the same as the Dharma names of the five monks first converted by the Buddha, expressing deep expectations. In the past few months, they have been studying Sanskrit, Pali, English, and Sangha precepts with Master Naluoda, making rapid progress. Yesterday, the Shanghai Buddhist Pure Land Karma Society received

A Report From The Delegation

Stating that they had already received the Bhikkhu ordination on July 29 in Kelaniya. The ordaining preceptor was the foremost elder of Ceylon, Faqi Luona, over ninety years old, with noble precepts. A special ordination platform was set up in the river to symbolize purity. After they were ordained, they sat upright and received the reverence and offerings of thousands of spectators. The people of that country all know how to make offerings of clothing and food to the Sangha according to the Dharma, so the monks can abstain from holding silver and money, strictly abide by the precepts, and the atmosphere of the forest and graveyard is no different from when the Buddha was alive. The first Chinese monk to go to Ceylon

Was In The Six Dynasties

The great master Faxian. The people of that country have the utmost respect for Master Xian. There is a rock, said to be the place where Faxian practiced meditation, named Faxian Rock. Specialists Zhong Xian Song and Wei Huan, two bhikkhus, have recently sent back works of translation to China, which will be published in Buddhist magazines soon.

Strange Insects in the River at North Gaoqiao, Pudong: About an Inch Long, All Colors Available, Health Bureau is Eliminating Them

The river at North Gaoqiao in Pudong (also known as Jiebang) is the largest river in the area, with constant boat traffic. However, the residents there usually do not know about sanitation and arbitrarily throw garbage, feces, and dead cats and dogs into the river. Although the Health Bureau has previously posted signs strictly prohibiting this, it has not been effective. Therefore, a strange insect has recently been found in the river, about an inch long, everywhere. Red, yellow, blue, white, and black colors are all available, and they are as numerous as tadpoles in spring. A few days ago, a worker named Jia got thirsty and took water from the river to quench his thirst. Unexpectedly, he immediately vomited and diarrhea, and the above-mentioned strange insects were also found in the diarrhea. It was then known to be poisonous. Fortunately, he was immediately treated by a doctor and escaped the danger of death. At present, the residents there are quite frightened by this. Therefore, the Health Bureau has come forward to inspect and find ways to eliminate it, while strictly prohibiting the throwing of garbage and other filth into the river.

Soon, she gave birth to a daughter, named Amao (now an adult, also listed as the second petitioner), who was taken back by Zhu for upbringing. Afterwards, Zhu changed his attitude. Zhu Ziyun devised a plan to send Amao to his in-laws, the Ma family, for upbringing. This was entirely a matter of morality. Even Amao's marriage to the Zhang family was presided over by the Ma family, with gift lists and other evidence to prove it. Therefore, the petitioner's allegations were entirely castles in the air, etc. The court inquired whether there was any possibility of settlement. Lawyer Lu immediately stated that it was absolutely impossible, etc. Judge Wang then declared the mediation unsuccessful and instructed the petitioner to file a formal lawsuit separately. Poor Daughter-in-Law Painfully Abandons Her Sick Child: Municipal Council and Court Have No Relief Measures

The Continental News reports: Last Thursday night, a Chinese woman abandoned her nine-year-old paralyzed son on the steps in front of Renji Hospital on Shandong Road. This incident has left the police authorities of the Municipal Council and officials of the First Special District Court in a quandary, with no precedent to follow. In other words, there is no precedent to follow. The court cannot now send the child to a hospital or charitable organization in the Public Concession or the Greater Shanghai Municipality for treatment, because the major charitable organizations in the Concession are not under the jurisdiction of the First Special District Court. Therefore, taking in the sick child is not a matter that the court can decide, but should be decided by the hospital or other similar organizations, or by the Municipal Council. Although this matter has been reported to the court, it has not been judged. The sick child is currently temporarily taken in by the police, but the police authorities are eager to determine a solution so that they can be relieved of the burden of caring for the child. The child cannot move from the waist down and needs constant medical treatment. The police believe that the child's future life will depend on the public. The whereabouts of the mother are currently unknown. Although the child can speak, he cannot tell the police where his mother is or her usual residence. The child's clothes are tattered. When he was found that day, there was a note on his clothes that read: the child's father is dead, and the mother is destitute, so she cannot afford the child's medical expenses. Now she is abandoning him on the steps of your hospital, hoping that the doctors will do good deeds and treat him properly. If he can be cured, she will do her best to save the wages she earns to repay their labor, etc. The note was not signed. The hospital staff took the child in and reported it to the police. The police immediately formally applied to the court for disposal, which ordered the child to be sent to a certain nursery in the Xinzha district. The nursery refused, saying that it was currently repairing the building and could not take him in. The child was then cared for by the police and the court again. Major foreign charitable hospitals in the Concession are unwilling to take in the child, setting a precedent, and wish to have the matter resolved by the judicial authorities. Logically speaking, if the mother is found to reside in the Public Concession, then the responsibility may be borne by the Municipal Council. If she is a resident of Zhabei or Nanshi, then the Chinese authorities should bear the responsibility. However, it is heard that the Municipal Council is unwilling to assume this obligation, believing that if this precedent is set, other disabled people will flock to it. The Municipal Council has not prepared the funds to support such people.

A notorious gangster, Ding Xiaodi from Changshu, nicknamed Xiao Zifan (Little Rice Cake), is quite powerful in the Xinzha area and has many disciples. Last month, Chen Zhengguang, residing at No. 373, Lane 568, Xinzha Road, introduced his tenant, Wang Xiaosan, to Ding Xiaodi as a disciple (commonly known as "Old Man"). Biscuit and Candy Association Submits Document to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Requesting the Cessation of Increased Taxes in Vietnam

The Biscuit and Candy Industry Association submitted a document to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, stating (previous content omitted): “Since recent years, domestic goods manufacturers in our country have suffered from the global economic downturn externally, and have been affected by rural bankruptcy internally. They struggle arduously and try to survive with difficulty, and are already in a precarious situation. Since the September 18th Incident, the sales routes in North China for our biscuit, candy, and canned goods industries have been completely cut off. The situations in Central and South China are also far from what they used to be. The vitality of various factories is hanging by a thread. Fortunately, in the Nanyang region, due to overseas Chinese not forgetting their homeland and loving domestic goods, and particularly because the overseas Chinese in Vietnam have a deep understanding of domestic goods, exports to Vietnam are still substantial and the future prospects are limitless. However, recently, the Vietnamese government suddenly became envious and implemented a scorched-earth policy, excessively increasing import taxes on goods imported from our country. Such measures are clearly erecting high tariff barriers to block the sales routes of our country's goods and cut off our trade with Vietnam. Upon investigation, the ink is barely dry on the Sino-French Vietnamese commercial agreement, but the authorities are suddenly going against it, disregarding the agreement and arbitrarily increasing taxes, which is truly infuriating. We earnestly request that your ministry promptly raise a serious protest, ensuring that diplomatic relations are considered and the tax increase is urgently cancelled, in accordance with the principle of mutual benefit and equality. The diplomatic front, the national economy, and the people's livelihood will all deeply benefit from this, not only will the future of domestic goods be bright." (remainder omitted)

Forging Land Deed Mortgage Guarantor Sues for Fraud

Deng Jieqing, a Cantonese native and the owner of Ruichang Hardware Store at No. 667 Jing'an Temple Road, aged 64, retained lawyer Jiang Hechun to file a complaint with the Criminal Division of the Special No. 2 Court, accusing Chen Huibin, a local resident living upstairs at the Yalu Bookstore at No. 48 Glock Road, of colluding with Ding Huiting, a land guarantor from Map 1, District 1 of the 29th Bao, to forge documents in a fraud case, and filed a civil suit requesting the recovery of the $2,250 compensation paid on his behalf. According to the complaint, in the 23rd year of the Republic (1934), Chen Huibin mortgaged a land deed for farmland to the Tongyuan Bank for $4,000, with the plaintiff acting as guarantor and Ding Huiting providing land guarantee certification. At the deadline, Chen first repaid half of the amount, leaving $2,000 outstanding, and replaced the original mortgaged land deed with another land deed (measuring 5 mu, 4 fen, 7 li, 9 hao) from the Jiang character No. 1454 in Map 3, District 1 of the 29th Bao, still with the plaintiff as guarantor. When the deadline arrived, Chen Huibin did not redeem the deed. The creditor, Tongyuan Bank, filed a lawsuit in the Special No. 1 Court to enforce the mortgage. Because the land was located in the Chinese area, the case was entrusted to the Shanghai Local Court for assistance in enforcement. Unexpectedly, when the land deed was checked with the Land Bureau, it was found to be owned by Chen Hanzhou and had another land ownership certificate, rendering the enforcement impossible. The plaintiff had no choice but to pay $2,250 to compensate the debt. However, Chen Huibin and Ding Huiting completely ignored the matter. It is clear that the later land deed was forged by the defendants for fraud. He requests that they be punished according to Articles 211 and 339 of the Criminal Law. Upon receiving the complaint, Judge Chen Shuoying from the Criminal Division No. 2 summoned the defendants yesterday. The defendants did not appear. Because the plaintiff had language difficulties, his lawyer explained the main points of the prosecution on his behalf. Witness Chen Songtao, the head of the business department of Tongyuan Bank, testified that the defendant mortgaged the land deed until the deadline, repaid half of the amount, and still owed half. He also described the circumstances of the replacement of the mortgaged land deed. After reviewing the evidence, the court instructed that the hearing be adjourned to the 15th to summon the defendants for further questioning.

Lawyer Loses Over 700 Gold Coins Gambling Check Bounces Holder Hu Tiegen Files Suit Yesterday's Trial Concluded, Judgment Scheduled

Wang Zongpu, courtesy name Yangsu, from Hangxian, Zhejiang, 26 years old, joined the Shanghai Bar Association as a member in July of the 24th year of the Republic (1935) and practiced law in Shanghai, with an office at No. 423 Continental Market and residing at No. 15 Jingu Village, Father Jin Road, French Concession. At 10:00 PM on March 8th of this year, Wang received a phone call at his residence from his friend Hu Jinchang from room 215 of the Datong Hotel, stating that there were business matters to discuss and urging him to go there immediately. Wang complied and went to room 215 of the Datong Hotel, where he chatted with Hu Jinchang and several others. On a whim, they played mahjong with a base of one thousand yuan. After entering the game and playing two rounds, Wang lost over 700 yuan. Wang immediately stopped the game and settled the debt of 749 yuan, issuing a check on the Shanghai Bank branch on Jing'an Temple Road, dated March 9th, with the number C390786 for 749 yuan, to the winner, and they all dispersed. The next day, the check holder and winner, Hu Tiegen (age 36), a native of the right place, went to the Shanghai Bank branch on Jing'an Temple Road to cash the check, but it was returned due to insufficient funds. Hu also sent a letter to Wang, asking for a delay in repayment, but Wang has not paid a penny to this day. The check holder, Hu Tiegen, retained lawyer Ye Changyi to file a complaint with the Criminal Division of the Special No. 2 Court, accusing Wang Zongpu of fraud, and filed a civil suit requesting the recovery of the check amount. Upon receiving the complaint, Judge Qiu Xiying presided over a hearing in the Criminal Division No. 2 yesterday morning. The plaintiff, Hu Tiegen, arrived with his lawyer to explain the situation and present the check as evidence. The defendant, Wang Zongpu, stated that Hu Jinchang, a former classmate from Minli Middle School, called him and invited him to room 215 of the Datong Hotel to discuss business matters. Unexpectedly, there was no business to discuss, and he was urged to play two rounds of mahjong, resulting in him losing over 700 yuan. Fearing that they were setting him up, he immediately stopped. They demanded cash on the spot, otherwise they would not let him leave. Being forced and helpless, he issued the check, deliberately writing the date as August 9th of the 24th year of the Republic, to indicate that he would not honor this gambling debt. The judge reprimanded the defendant, saying, "As a lawyer, you went to play mahjong with a base of one thousand yuan. If you were cheated and lost money, you could have filed a lawsuit and reported it at the time. Why did you only claim it was a gambling game after the plaintiff sued you? You are too absurd." He then ordered the debate to begin, declared it concluded, and scheduled the judgment for the morning of the 11th.

Another Depositor of Meihua Bank Accuses Gu Yubo and Others Of the Eight Defendants, Only Sun Wenkui Appeared Attorney Wu Peng Presents Important Evidence to the Court

The Meihua Bank, founded by Gu Yubo and others, closed down after only two weeks of operation, making it arguably the shortest-lived bank. However, Gu and others disappeared after the bank failed, ignoring repeated accusations from creditors. Now, Wang Tingfang, Chen Peidong, Wu Youji, Lin Boyuan, Li Qiuyang, Zhu Meifang, Zhou Guanqun, Zhang Yushu, Chuan Fengguo, Li Songsheng, He Hongfang, Ma Buqing, Qian Zhixiang, and fourteen other depositors of the bank, retained attorney Wu Peng to file

criminal self-accusation of fraud and embezzlement

against Gu Yubo and others in the First Special District Local Court, stating that Gu Yubo, Zhang Xusheng, Li Yichou, Bao Ziwu, and Chen Xuanzai were initially co-founders of the former Daxin Bank with Lin Kanghou, Jiang Baili, Shen Jingzhong, Chen Jinnan, and others. However, because the shares could not be concentrated and no record was filed, Li Yichou introduced a merger with the Meihua Bank on January 16th of this year and signed a merger agreement. Gu Yubo subscribed to 150,000 yuan of shares, serving as a director and manager of Meihua Bank. Zhang Xusheng, Li Yichou, Bao Ziwu, Chen Yizhai, etc. each

subscribed to 50,000 shares

Zhang served as deputy manager, Li and Bao as executive directors, and Chen also served as deputy manager. Liu Tongfu, Sun Wenkui, and Wang Zhonglin each served as assistant managers. Whether the subscribed shares were fully paid is unknown. However, without legally registering, the bank opened on April 8th of this year at No. 230 Jiujiang Road. Unexpectedly, it closed down on the 30th of the same month. The plaintiffs were collectively owed 9,945.89 yuan, which is obviously a case of setting up a bank to

fraudulently obtain deposits

and should be punished under Article 339 of the Criminal Law. In addition, the private prosecution requested that, since the bank was not registered, all defendants be held jointly liable for repayment and legal interest. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng opened a court hearing to summon the defendants. Only Sun Wenkui appeared with his defense attorney, Lin Hanqing. The other seven defendants, Gu Yubo, Zhang Xusheng, Li Yichou, Bao Ziwu, Chen Yizhai, Liu Tongfu, and Wang Zhonglin, were all in hiding. Judge Huang decided to combine the case with

the self-accusation of breach of trust

filed by the Westerners Yale, Menglei, Malaysia, and others against Gu and others, as the circumstances were similar. The Westerners' attorney briefly stated the case, saying that Meihua's closure was due to Gu Yubo, Bao Ziwu, and Chen Yaozai embezzling the collected shares, making it impossible to maintain the bank. He requested that Gu be wanted and that Bao and Chen be arrested and investigated. Then, attorney Wu Peng, representing the other plaintiffs, presented ten photographs, all taken at the bank's opening, and photographs of

various congratulatory telegrams

and the agreement signed with Dajia, stating that this evidence was sufficient to prove that Gu and the other eight defendants were all important figures in the bank and could not deny it. Attorney Lin Hanqing defended Sun Wenkui, saying that Sun was only an employee of the bank. The court then ordered the plaintiffs to present deposit slips to prove the amount of the deposits and adjourned the hearing for further questioning at a later date.
