Privately Pledging Deposited Silk Accusations of Business Embezzlement Fuxingheng Suffers Losses of 140,000 to 150,000 Yuan Xu Ziming and Zhu Xingzhai Ordered to Appear, but Cannot Be Found

Tongfeng Silk Shop, located at No. 20 Jingxing Lane, Tianjin Road, is an extremely large organization managed by Xu Ziming (also known as Minggao) and Zhu Xingzhai (also known as Shikui). Fuxingheng Money Shop, originally located in Chongqing, engages not only in the money industry but also in the silk and cotton business. It appointed deputy manager Li Xiangchi to handle the buying and selling of silk and cotton in Shanghai. Because Tongfeng Silk Shop is very familiar with various foreign firms, Fuxingheng stores all the silk shipped from Sichuan to Shanghai in the shop and entrusts it for sale. In the 20th year of the Republic (1931), Fuxingheng stored over 400 dan of Sichuan silk in the shop. Tongfeng sold over 100 dan, leaving 292 dan still in storage, which was worth over 200,000 yuan at the time. Li Xiangchi repeatedly urged the shop to sell the silk, but Xu and Zhu made excuses, claiming that the silk was of poor quality and the market price was not suitable. Until last year, there was still no news of the sale. Li then demanded that the goods be returned, but Tongfeng kept delaying. Li then filed a civil lawsuit in the First Special District Court against Xu and others, demanding the return of the stored silk. Xu and others hired a lawyer to appear in court. The plaintiff, Li Xiangchi, requested that the defendant disclose the identities of the shareholders, but they were unable to do so. Only later did it become known that Tongfeng had mortgaged the stored silk to Xinfu Foreign Firm at No. 9 Aiduya Road in the 21st year of the Republic (1932) for a price of 500 to 600 gold coins per bale. The term was six months, and because it was not redeemed, it was auctioned off by the foreign firm. Tongfeng seemed to have ceased operations last year, with only a few junior employees left to handle matters. Li believed that Xu and Zhu should not have privately mortgaged the deposited goods. Based on the current market price, Fuxingheng suffered a loss of 140,000 to 150,000 yuan, which clearly constituted business embezzlement. Therefore, he retained attorney Wen Dairong to file a complaint with the Criminal Division of the Special No. 1 Court against Xu and Zhu. The court ordered them to appear, but they could not be found. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng opened a hearing in the Criminal Division No. 8. Because the defendants did not appear, the hearing was adjourned for further questioning at a later date.

Squatter Wang Baoliang Died of Illness Yesterday Morning

The Squatter Association Requests the Municipal Council to Provide Compensation for a Victim of the Chaoyang Road Demolition The New Voice Society reported that two households at No. 448 Chaoyang Road, Shanghai East, were forcibly demolished because the houses were old and dilapidated, and the owner, Wang Baoliang, repaired them. The Municipal Council deemed this an illegal construction and forcibly demolished them, which was the cause of this tragic incident. On September 2nd, a large number of detectives and laborers forcibly carried out the demolition. Wang Baoliang, being old, suffered too much shock from this incident and became ill immediately. He died around 2:00 AM yesterday morning. His wife, Liu, is also seriously ill and unlikely to survive. Wang Baoliang was a native of Funing, Jiangsu, 58 years old. He used to run a small pharmacy on Chaoyang Road, but business was poor and he had to close down. He was then forced into this squatter's life. He had four sons. The eldest son is an adult and works as a laborer, but the other sons are not yet established. The orphans and the old woman are now destitute, which is unbearable to hear. Wang's body cannot be put into a coffin due to lack of funds, and the situation is extremely tragic. The Squatter Association has requested the Municipal Council to provide compensation. Sincerely, Wang Baoliang, a member of our association and a squatter at No. 448 Chaoyang Road, is 58 years old and a native of Funing, Jiangsu. Since his squatter house was forcibly demolished and all his daily necessities were destroyed, he became depressed and ill from the severe shock. He suffered for several days and could not afford to see a doctor or take medicine. Unfortunately, he passed away at 2:00 AM on the 8th. We are ashamed that we cannot console the deceased. However, we believe that Wang Baoliang was an innocent victim of your council's extraordinary measures and should be given generous compensation to comfort his aggrieved soul. We are endlessly pleading.

Central Bank Inspection Report

The two hundred and nineteenth inspection report on the issuance reserve of the Central Bank exchange notes states: This council, in accordance with the provisions of Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, is responsible for inspecting the issuance amount and reserve funds of exchange notes of this bank. We held the two hundred and fifteenth inspection at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on September 5, 1936, and the results of the inspection are reported as follows: (A) Exchange note issuance amount: 30,681,232 yuan in silver dollars, including 27,435,895 yuan in silver dollar notes and 3,245,4227 yuan in fractional currency notes. The total amount of exchange note reserve funds is 30,681,232 yuan in silver dollars, including 20,513,822 yuan in cash reserve in silver dollars. The cash reserve includes 10,956,089.79 yuan deposited in the head office and branches of this bank, and 9,557,732.21 yuan deposited with other banks. The guarantee reserve is converted to 10,167,410 yuan in silver dollars. (B) Total issuance of Customs Gold Unit exchange notes: 400,963.07 yuan. Total amount of Customs Gold Unit exchange note reserve funds: 400,963.07 yuan. The reserve funds include 7,926.290 ounces of pure gold, valued at 51.68, totaling 400,963.07 yuan in Customs Gold Units. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve should be at least 60%, and the remainder should be a guarantee reserve in the form of legal guarantees. The inspection results show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the guarantee reserve is within 40%, which complies with the regulations. This report is hereby made. September 7, 1936, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fuson, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilun.

Letter

Dear Editor, I have received a statement from the person concerned, Wang Liu Shi, stating that her late husband, Wang Jiasheng, was seriously injured by his colleague, Zhang Pinfu, in the factory's toilet on the 3rd of this month and died on the afternoon of the 4th. The sudden death has caused unbearable pain. Fortunately, the murderer, Zhang Pinfu, has been arrested by the police. The widow will wait quietly for the court to make a judgment according to the law regarding the prosecution. However, the newspaper reports have stated that the deceased, Wang Jiasheng, had an affair with Zhang Pinfu's wife, A Feng, which is untrue. Leaving aside the fact that the deceased and A Feng are more than twenty years apart in age and usually address each other as "Uncle," how could an affair occur? Even when the deceased was alive, he was silent and taciturn. If he were not a good person, he would not have worked in the electric light factory for fourteen years. Colleagues in the factory and neighbors can all testify. Justice is in the hearts of the people and will be clear after investigation. Now, Zhang Pinfu killed the deceased for no reason and is trying to defend himself with fabricated words, which is utterly heartless. The widow believes that her husband's death was sudden and unexpected, a calamity from the sky, and that he is already suffering in the depths of injustice. Yet after his death, he is being tarnished with an impure reputation, adding injustice to injustice. How can she bear it? Therefore, she has entrusted your lawyer to send a letter to various newspapers for correction. Please publish it to correct the record. Yours sincerely, Lawyer Jia Yi, September 8th, to the Shen Bao Newspaper.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 pm yesterday stated: The Shandong area and the Yellow Sea are overcast with showers and whirlwinds due to a small low-pressure system moving northeastward. The Yellow River basin and the upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River are clear and sunny with variable winds. Zhang Bofang Appeals Against Fraud Conviction; Hearing Concluded Yesterday; Verdict Scheduled for the 15th

Zheng Chengqing, a former executive committee member of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce who has been expelled, alleged that the national flags manufactured by Zhang Rongchu's National Flag Manufacturing and Sales Bureau used inferior materials. He forged an official document from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce stating that it had sent personnel to investigate and forged the signature of the former chairman, Yu Zuoting, to instigate his brother-in-law, Zhang Bofang, manager of the Zhonghe Soap Factory, to visit Zhang with the document and attempt to extort 50,000 yuan. Zhang reported this matter, and the Chamber of Commerce resolved to revoke Zheng's executive committee membership and Yu filed a criminal lawsuit against Zheng and Zhang. After hearing the case, the court sentenced Zhang to two and a half years of imprisonment, a fine of 900 yuan, and deprivation of civil rights for five years. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yu specially convened a collegiate panel for a joint hearing. Zhang admitted that Zheng Chengqing had instructed him to take the official document to Zhang's place, but claimed that he was unaware that the document was forged by Zheng and that what he was seeking from Zhang was the outstanding shares of the Zhonghe Soap Factory, and absolutely not extorting money. Zhang Zilian has committed many crimes in recent years, and his character is imaginable, so his testimony is difficult to believe. The original judgment should be revoked, and the appellant should be declared innocent. Yuan Hanyun, the lawyer for the appellant Yu Zuoting, argued that Zheng and Zhang were brothers-in-law, and Zhang could not claim ignorance of the fact that the document was forged by Zheng, and asked the court to impose punishment according to the law. Judge Yu then announced that the verdict would be rendered at 15:00 on September 15.

Shen Bao National Products Supplement

A Visit to the Taizhou National Products Sales Office

— Qiao Yunxun

Last summer, I wrote an article based on my limited knowledge, suggesting that national product sales agencies should be established in county towns, creating smaller-scale national product markets so that the general public in the interior could know where to go to promote national products. Mr. Pan Yangyao, the editor of this publication, added a note expressing enthusiastic support. Before a year has passed, a market exclusively selling national products has actually been discovered in a county town. Overjoyed, I made a special visit. Taizhou is the current Taixian, which originally included Taidong County. Dongtai does not have a city wall and once belonged to Taizhou. Now, Taixian and Dongtai are adjacent to each other. It's called "Taizhou National Products Sales Office" rather than "County." It seems that the natives of the Lixiahe region, and even the eight prefectures of Yangzhou, know Taizhou more deeply than they know Taixian. This is similar to Suzhou and Wuxian. It's also a business strategy. The office is located on Pozi Street outside the North Gate. This street is as lively and prosperous as Guanqian Street in Suzhou and Duozi Street in Yangzhou. The manager, Mr. Xue Pingfan, is in his prime and is a talented and promising young man. He is amiable and willing to be a bulwark for the national products industry. During our conversation, he mentioned that his ancestral home is Jingjiang and that the office originated in Liangxi, the industrial area south of the Yangtze River, as a branch of the Wuxi General Management Office. After the "May 30th Massacre," the Chinese and foreign merchants deeply felt the loss of profits and worried about it. They organized the Datong National Products Management Office, a united front of Chinese and foreign grocery businesses. Now the banner is even clearer, renamed the National Products Market, consigning purely domestic products from major Shanghai factories, such as cotton weaving and printing, steelware, cosmetics, rubber, enamelware, and batteries, as well as household daily necessities. Qiming Cotton Weaving Factory, Family Industrial Cooperative, China Chemical Industrial Cooperative, Liangxinji Toothbrush Factory, Da Dong Rubber Factory, Central Battery Factory, Lixing Thermos Factory, and Wuhe Weaving Factory are all the targets of his promotion. The Taizhou National Products Sales Office follows the business policy of the head office, with minor differences in details. Taixian's retail market is not broad, so it focuses on wholesale. There are full-time representatives who promote to department stores. Mr. Xue believes that by doing so, imported goods will have no place to stand! Although the office does not occupy a large area, the furnishings are in line with modern business rules, and there are printed materials for promotion. The price list has these introductory words: "Entrusted by major national product factories in Shanghai, this office has been specially established in Taizhou to facilitate the procurement of department stores in Taixian, Dongtai, Xinghua, Yancheng, Funing, and other counties. Since its opening, it has been pursuing the aim of faithful service and vigorous promotion of national products!..." After reading these words, one knows its ambition. Finally, I believe that while attention should be paid to wholesale, retail should also be promoted. Mr. Xue nodded in agreement, and we said goodbye with mutual respect.

Shen Bao National Products Supplement Department

Words of Contribution

The Fruits of Promoting National Products in Recent Years

— Yang'an

People love to eat fruit, and they say it is sweet and delicious. But little do they know that at the time of planting the seeds, cultivating the soil, applying fertilizer, and removing weeds, how many years, how much spirit, how much strength, and how much cost have been spent before they can taste the sweetness and sigh in admiration. Perhaps at the time when the fruit ripens, the one who planted the seeds is no longer in this world. "The predecessors plant trees for the descendants to enjoy the shade," "Success does not have to be my own." The mentality of the tree planter is like this, but those who eat its benefits should not forget its favor.

Yesterday at the meeting of the Citizens' National Products Promotion Association, the attendees praised the promotion of national products in recent years, saying that it can be described as vigorous and unstoppable. From government offices to families, wherever there is talk, it is about national products; wherever there is a question, it is about national products; what children sing is about national products; what literati write is about national products; what radio stations broadcast is about national products. Recently, the key point of the New Life Movement is to use national products, and the outline of the National Economic Construction Movement is to promote national products. All government circulars and newspaper and magazine articles are full of national products. How magnificent! The splendor of national products has reached its peak today. If Chinese people living today do not use national products, they are truly deranged and not of the Chinese nation. What is gratifying is that waiters in bars and restaurants mostly use domestic products to serve guests, and children do not want to wear clothes that are not made of domestic fabrics. China's opportunity for revival is within sight. At the same time, Mr. Gan Jie'an, who has been promoting national products for decades, sighed: "Twenty years ago, when we promoted national products, people laughed secretly, either considering it impractical or criticizing it as meddling. Some even regarded it as foolish. At that time, Chinese people lacked patriotic ideas, and national products were also crude and inferior. Modern people regarded imported goods as fashionable and imported goods as glorious. When you talk about national products, they cover their ears and run away. How much effect could it have? And the song was too high for the few to sing along. Who would agree? Who would echo? Who would obey? I never thought that twenty years later, there would be such a glorious and sensational day at home and abroad." As he spoke, tears welled up in his eyes, and everyone present was moved. We dare to comfort you by saying: Without the past, there would be no present. Only by planting seeds in the past can we have the fruits of today. Nothing in the world can be accomplished without hardship. Moreover, the situation of national products today is not optimistic, and it cannot be said that the time has come to eat the fruit. Pests are everywhere, and weeds are everywhere. We still need our association to struggle, cultivate, work hard, and continue the movement to promote national products. Then the sweet fruit can always be delicious. What do the patriotic people of our country think?

New Developments in National Product Medicine Water, Electric Essence, and Lamps

— Qiulang

The latest invention among national products, the "Medicine Water Electric Essence Lamp," although previously briefly reported, has not had any follow-up news for a long time. It turns out that the original inventor of this lamp was the Hua Yi Industrial Cooperative, but it only produced samples. In June of this year, it submitted it to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for patent application. Due to a shortage of capital and waiting for the ministry's approval, it temporarily stopped. Recently, however, Mr. Wang and Mr. Wu have also researched and manufactured this lamp, and have succeeded. They are now actively rushing to produce a large number of products. It seems to be a case of "the latecomer surpasses the former." It is heard that they have set a date in mid-September to begin connecting lines for installation. According to reports, the most difficult point of this lamp is the coordination of the medicine water procedure (the medicine water is also a national product). It will use medicine water to conduct electricity. Its wiring situation is similar to ordinary electric lamps, but the bulbs are specially made, and each lamp must have a medicine water bottle box. More lamps will require more boxes. The medicine water can be used for 150 hours, and the electricity cost is two-thirds less than ordinary electric lamps. Therefore, many households have already ordered installations. This is truly a new contribution to the national product industry!

Education News

More Than 800 People Have Registered for the Municipal General Examination; Registration Closes on the 20th

The municipal education bureau is holding a general examination. Since registration began on September 1st, participation has been very enthusiastic. More than 800 people have already registered, and it is expected that more than 2,000 people will participate in the examination. The bureau has specially assigned staff to handle the matter, and the work is quite intense. A temporary qualification review office has also been set up to handle review matters. The registration is scheduled to close on the 20th. To facilitate candidates' registration, the following procedures have been specially formulated for candidates to register: (1) Obtain a physical examination certificate, two registration application forms, a guarantee form, and a selection examination subject card. (2) Fill out in ink in regular script, without alterations, and fill out truthfully. (3) Submit the physical examination certificate, proof of qualification for the examination or a temporary application for review, and academic and experience certificates, seven recent 4-inch front-facing, hatless half-length photos without cardboard, with the name and address written on the back of each photo, the completed registration application form, guarantee form, and selection examination subject card, and a registration fee of one yuan, and obtain a receipt. Those who temporarily apply for review and registration should first pay a temporary receipt for the application for review and registration documents and registration fee, etc. After receiving the notice of passing the review, they should separately obtain formal document receipts and registration fee receipts. (4) Obtain the examination admission ticket, which can be obtained with the registration fee receipt.

Recent Four Years of National Central University (3)

— Luo Jialun

(10) New Xueshi School Xuechi Building, 23,100 yuan. (11) Two new student dormitories, 103,289 yuan. In order to concentrate management, the school returned the rented dormitories and built two new student dormitories on the original site of the old fifth dormitory, which can accommodate hundreds of people. They were designed and supervised by professors from the school's architecture department. Currently, most of the school's students live here. (12) New special mechanical research class factory and wind tunnel room, 11,810 yuan. (13) New telecommunications experimental room, 4,800 yuan. (14) New plant research room and heating system for the Department of Biology, 1,895 yuan. (15) New hydraulic laboratory, 6,200 yuan. (16) New chemical laboratory for the Department of Forestry, 1,100 yuan. (17) New medical school, 42,000 yuan. (18) New refrigerated room for the Department of Animal Husbandry, 5,000 yuan. (19) New National Building of the Experimental School, 12,000 yuan, of which 4,500 yuan was saved from the school's regular expenses. (20) New piano practice room, 1,000 yuan. (21) New dormitory storage room, 3,000 yuan. (22) Additional ball field, 1,200 yuan. (23) Renovation of the Biology Museum, 13,700 yuan. The original Biology Museum was in very poor condition and severely damaged. The groundwater accumulated two or three feet underground, so it had to be completely renovated. (24) Additional new classrooms, factories, and soap factories for the School of Engineering, 6,790 yuan. (25) Renovation and addition of classrooms and laboratories for the School of Education (Nanjing Higher Normal School), 14,530 yuan. This is the oldest building in the school and must be completely renovated. However, the bell tower was not repaired because it might involve other departments. (26) Renovation of the School of Law (Southeast Academy), 7,700 yuan. (27) Renovation of the faculty housing, 5,785 yuan. This is also the earliest building in the school, dilapidated and must be repaired. (28) Renovation of student dormitories, 4,739 yuan. Although this house was built in 1929, the foundation and materials are very poor, so it had to be repaired. (29) Renovation of the South House of the student dormitory, 10,230 yuan. (30) Renovation of the old first dormitory into a female dormitory, 7,000 yuan. The female dormitory was originally rented from private houses. The old first dormitory is now renovated into a female dormitory, so that all female students can live on campus for easy management. The above are only the larger and more expensive ones. In total, from September 1932 to June 1934, the amount has reached 368,160 yuan. There are also smaller buildings and construction projects that cannot be listed one by one, totaling more than 66,849 yuan. From July 1934 to the present, the total construction cost has reached 211,624 yuan. There are also smaller buildings and repairs, such as the addition of chemical laboratories, which are not included here, totaling more than 7,900 yuan. As for the amount not yet paid after the completion of the auditorium and the amount for the installation of seats, 14,455 yuan has also been paid. Therefore, within these four years, the total amount actually paid for construction is 668,988 yuan. For all major constructions, professors are hired to form a construction committee to preside over it, so as to make a joint decision and achieve perfection.

4. Extensive Expansion of Library and Scientific Instruments

Besides academic buildings, school facilities primarily consist of libraries and scientific instruments. The current policy focuses on minimizing administrative expenses to expand the aforementioned facilities. This is the wellspring of academic subjects, textbooks, and research, and should not be neglected for even a moment. Examination of the past reveals that while the budget for these facilities was considerable, the actual expenditure on libraries and scientific instruments in a single year amounted to only 36,582 yuan. Since Chancellor Zhu Jiahua's arrival, great efforts have been made to enrich these facilities. From September of the 21st year to June of the 23rd year of the Republic (a period of 22 months), the total expenditure on library resources was 165,342 yuan. Furthermore, from July of the 23rd year to the end of June of the 25th year, the actual expenditure on library resources was 205,303 yuan. Thus, within four years, the total actual expenditure was 370,645 yuan, with the addition of 48,265 volumes of Chinese and Japanese books, 19,570 volumes of Western books, 266 types of Chinese magazines, and 186 types of Western magazines. The number of individual issues is countless. Among the Chinese books, there are many rare and fine editions, and among the Western books, many are considered quite valuable. Examples include P. Gelisdidot's La Peinture decorative en france du 16th au 18th Siecle (French painting from the 16th to 18th centuries, bound from individual pages), Paul Pelliot's Les grottes de toue Houang Peintures et Sculpturesbou dhigues epoques des Wei des Tang et des Long (Buddhist statues and sutras from the Wei, Tang, and Song dynasties in the Dunhuang grottoes, published between 1914 and 1924, in six massive volumes, bound from individual pages), and Arthuur Pugin's Gothic architecture (over a hundred drawings illustrating ancient British architecture, reproduced from originals dating from 1821 to 1838). The number of Western magazine titles is significant. The most gratifying aspect is that a large portion of the Western magazines that were missing from the 20th year of the Republic have been acquired, alleviating the perceived financial burden. It is also noteworthy that a complete collection of over thirty Western magazines has been acquired within a short period. These include Journal fur die reine unp angenandte Mathematik, dating from 1826 to the present (111 years), Justus liebig'S Annaleender Chemie, dating from 1832 to the present (105 years), Petermanns Mittilungen, dating from 1855 to the present (82 years), "Mittilungen"Annaien"B-I-II2, dating from 1869 to the present (68 years), Geographisches Tahrbuch, dating from 1866 to 1931 (66 years), "Berichte der DeutschenBotanischen Gesnllscafi," dating from 1883 to the present (54 years), Acta Mathematica Vol I-66, dating from 1882 to the present (55 years), Berichte der Deutschen Chemischen Gesellschaft Vol I-69, dating from 1873 to the present (64 years), "American Journal of Mathematics" Vol. I-58, dating from 1878 to the present (59 years), "Transaction of the American Mathematical Society" Vol. I-39, dating from 1900 to the present (37 years), and "Harvard Law Review" Vol. I-49, dating from 1887 to the present (50 years). All of these have been completely purchased. Some of the more expensive sets cost six or seven thousand yuan, but for the sake of research, no expense has been spared to acquire them. (To be continued)

Ministry of Education Announces Regulations for the Printing of Textbooks for Private Schools

The Ministry of Education recently issued a decree promulgating nine regulations regarding the printing of textbooks for public schools, as follows:

(Article 1) Textbooks for public schools compiled by the Ministry of Education may be printed and distributed by publishing houses that issue educational books and newspapers, but they must comply with these regulations. (Article 2) Publishing houses seeking to print such textbooks must submit a request, along with two copies of the sample, to the Ministry of Education for approval before they can be published. (Article 3) The request must include the following information: 1. The number of editions to be printed and the number of copies per edition; 2. The selling price; 3. The name of the organization applying for permission to print; 4. The name, address, and brief history of the publisher. (Article 4) Publishing houses printing Ministry-compiled public school textbooks may not add, delete, or alter the text, illustrations, format, or content. In addition, domestically produced paper should be used as a matter of principle. (Article 5) Publishing houses printing textbooks must include the full text of the Ministry of Education's approval for printing on the cover and bottom page of the printed textbook. (Article 6) The cover of the printed textbook may only include the title, a note indicating "Compiled by the Ministry of Education," and the name of the publishing house. No other wording may be included, and no advertisements or other text may be printed on the bottom cover. (Article 7) The selling price of the textbook must be approved by the Ministry of Education. (Article 8) Those who print textbooks privately in violation of these regulations will, after investigation by the county or municipal government, be reported by the higher-level authorities to the Ministry of Education, which will prohibit their distribution. (Article 9) These regulations shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Mr. Wang Liansong, A Scholar of New Year, What He Studies

Wang, styled Baiquan, is from Yingcheng, Hubei. He graduated from National Beiping Industrial University in the 15th year of the Republic and subsequently worked for the Jidun Railway Engineering Bureau in Jilin Province. In the 18th year of the Republic, he served as a technician and senior technician in the municipal utility and public works bureaus of Hankou, and as the director of the Wubo Wireless Radio Station in Wuchang. In the 20th year of the Republic, he served as an electrical engineer for the Pinghan Railway Bureau. He is currently employed by this publication. Mr. Wang has been researching the three great problems of geometry for a total of fourteen years, from the 11th year of the Republic to the present. He has finally completely solved these geometrical puzzles, which have eluded the world's mathematicians for over two thousand years. When he began researching these problems, he first used the triple angle function to create a proportional mean formula to graphically solve the trisection of an angle, finding Nicomedes' conchoid method to be simple. At the same time, he also used this new curve to solve the problem of duplicating the cube, finding it more convenient than Diocles' cissoid method. However, since this curve was still a curved solution and could not be constructed with a ruler and compass, he abandoned this method and switched to using the method of bisecting the angle of eccentrically arranged arcs, spending eight years proving that this bisector was a straight line. At the same time, he also sought the limit of this new bisecting line, using it as a boundary for dividing infinitesimal arcs. Due to the convenience of this new straight line, the problem of trisecting an angle was suddenly solved. After another four years, the problem of duplicating the cube was also solved, still using the same consistent principle. He then continued to solve the problem of squaring the circle. Thus, the three great problems of geometry were thoroughly solved. Immediately following this, he generalized and solved the problems of dividing an angle into any number of equal parts, dividing a circle into any number of equal parts, straightening the circumference of a circle, squaring the surface of a sphere, and cubing the volume of a sphere, all based on the above principles. Mr. Wang is currently editing his research findings into a book, which he will submit to the Academia Sinica, the Ministry of Education, and other organizations for review. He is also translating it into English to be sent to the World Educational Association for research. Below is a recent photo of Liansong (taken by International News Service).

Zhejiang Normal Elementary Education Correspondence Course Eighth Session Enrollment

The elementary education correspondence course affiliated with the Zhejiang Provincial Hangzhou Normal School has been established for seven sessions. The rich and engaging content of the course materials and the simple and convenient correspondence procedures have resulted in each session attracting over a thousand students. This semester marks the continuation of the eighth session. The correspondence course includes a total of sixteen subjects. To better meet practical needs, subjects with similar characteristics have been merged, and two new courses, "Rural Construction and Education" and "Scout Training," have been added. The qualification for graduating from the correspondence course after completing the required coursework was previously approved by the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education and submitted to the Ministry of Education, and is considered "equivalent to completing two summer semesters of make-up education." Therefore, those holding a diploma from this course can use it as one of the qualifications for the Ministry-issued elementary school teacher certification, without examination or verification. It is reported that enrollment for the course has now begun and is scheduled to close in mid-October. Brochures with detailed information will be sent upon receipt of one cent in postage stamps.

Sports News

Today's Annual Meeting of the Shanghai Western Football Association Will Discuss Reforming the League Scheme; The Western Association Plans a Scheme to Respond to Attackers; A League Committee of Three Will Be Established to Handle the League; Last Year's Revenue Was Over 17,900 Yuan

The Shanghai Western Football Association is scheduled to hold its annual meeting at 5:15 PM on the 10th of this month (tomorrow) at the Western Children's Public School at 219 Jiujiang Road. The motions to be discussed at the annual meeting have attracted attention from all walks of life. It is generally agreed that the reform of the league organization scheme will become the focus of debate. The reform of the organization scheme has been included as the fourth item on the agenda for this year's annual meeting, but it is noted that this refers to the measures announced by the association on August 17. The sixth item is proposals from various teams, which are still being compiled and have not yet been listed in detail. The association's accounts for the past season will also be reported at the annual meeting. The following is a breakdown:

Annual Meeting Agenda

(1) Report on the past year's progress and overview (i.e., the implementation plan resolved at the annual meeting on September 12, 1935); (2) Report on the results and accounts of the previous competition (up to July 31); (3) Election of this year's officers, including: (A) One president; (B) Four vice presidents; (C) Four team representatives attending the meeting; (D) Other officers; (4) Reform of this year's Western League organization scheme (i.e., the notice to all member teams issued on August 17 of this year); (5) Organization committee responsible for drafting the association's new constitution and new rules; (6) Cases proposed by various teams (cases proposed by each team must be submitted to the registrar's office two days before the annual meeting, but in addition to the proposer's signature, there must be a countersignature from one team). Notice: Those attending the meeting are Western League officers, committee members, representatives from each team (two people), and referees. Seating: Members and those with voting rights are on the right side of the podium, and observers are on the left side. Newspaper reporters are in the front row near the podium.

Restructuring Plan

The Western League Football Association issued a draft reform plan to its member teams on the 17th of last month, which will be submitted at this year's annual meeting. The plan includes a total of nine articles, which are listed below. If the plan is adopted, it will be implemented this season and will be valid until 1937-38.

(1) This year's Shanghai Western Football Association will be divided into three groups (Groups A, B, and C).

(2) There will also be a reserve group, specifically for the inclusion of reserve teams from Group A. Players in the reserve group will not be restricted from competing in Group A.

(3) Member teams joining Group A must join one reserve group team.

(4) The bottom team in Group A will be relegated to Group B, and the champion of Group B can be promoted to Group A (but must join one reserve group team). The bottom team in Group B will be relegated to Group C, and the champion of Group C can be promoted to Group B.

(5) There will be a Sunday morning league to replace the previous Group E, with a limit of twelve teams.

(6) All member teams can join the league or the Sunday morning league.

(7) Each member team can join at most one team in the league or the Sunday morning league.

(8) In each match, the winner will receive two points, the loser will receive zero points, and a draw will result in each team receiving one point. If the scores are the same at the end, the average number of winning goals will be used.

(9) This season's League Committee will consist of five members, three of whom will be selected from the executive committee, and the remaining two will be selected from the member teams. This committee has no administrative power but can report to the executive committee for handling.

(Note) This reform plan is very similar to Davidson's plan, and is a modified version of Davidson's plan. The biggest difference is that the league will still be subordinate to the Western Association and will not be independent. However, a committee of three will be established. This is clearly a response to Davidson's attacks.

On the expenditure side, last year's total was 16,583.69 yuan, which is a decrease of 3,884.19 yuan compared to the previous year's 20,467.88 yuan. The net surplus for the last year was 1,346.76 yuan, while the previous year was 4,856.41 yuan, representing a decrease of 3,509.65 yuan. The details are listed below:

Interest on investments: 3,033.61 yuan. Total revenue: 17,930.45 yuan.

Cantonese Football Star Defender Li Jin Dies

Guangzhou News Police soccer player Li Jin, rising football star, served as defender for the police team since 1931, his skills improving daily. Selected for the Guangdong football team for the National Games in 1935, Li Jin made great contributions when the Hong Kong Nanhua won a special silver medal last year. It turns out, Mr. Li fell ill due to overwork, and after several months of treatment, he did not recover and passed away yesterday morning. It turns out Mr. Li's affairs are bare, and his burial was the responsibility of Public Security Bureau colleagues. The burial takes place today at 4pm at the Police cemetery. Li Jin was from Dapu, Guangdong, age 27 with one younger brother studying in the Nanyang region, with his parents both merchants in Sandakan. His mother returned from Nanyang after receiving the news, fortunate to see him one last time.

Youth Association Swimming Competition to be Held on the 16th of This Month

The Sports Department of the China Youth Association has scheduled a swimming competition for its members to be held at 7:00 PM on the evening of the 16th of this month (Wednesday) at the association's swimming pool on Sichuan Road. All members of the association are welcome to register and participate. The competition will be divided into four groups: (1) Children (under 90 pounds), (2) Juniors, (3) Adults, and (4) Men over 25 years old. Registration starts from today and will close on the evening of the 15th of this month at the association's office. Mixing between groups is not allowed. Each person can only join one group, and the competition consists of a total of eleven events. However, each person can participate in a maximum of four events. If any event has less than four participants, it will be canceled. The events specified at the time of registration cannot be changed. For each event, prizes will be awarded to the top three finishers, but if there are fewer than five participants, only the top two finishers will be awarded. Each person is limited to receiving three prize plaques. There will be no overall championship. The events are as follows:

(1) 20-yard freestyle (Children), (2) 40-yard freestyle (Men over 35 years old), (3) 50-yard freestyle, (4) 100-yard freestyle, (5) 100-yard breaststroke, (6) 100-yard backstroke, (7) 200-yard freestyle, (8) 200-yard breaststroke, (9) 400-yard freestyle, (10) Fancy diving, (11) Underwater object retrieval (Open to all groups)

Central Ministry of Civic Training Promotes Mountain Climbing Competition

A letter requesting that party departments in each province and city initiate a mountain climbing competition. The Central Ministry of Public Training sent a letter to the party departments in each province and city, stating that, in order to implement national physical education and training, it is appropriate to maximize the public's interest and encourage them to participate enthusiastically, so that the results can be achieved with half the effort. Now, when the autumn is high and the air is crisp, the custom of climbing mountains on the Double Ninth Festival in each province is a beneficial folk sport for both body and mind. It should be advocated or initiated to hold mountain climbing competitions to encourage the public to participate in order to achieve practical results. Accordingly, the Ministry hereby requests your department to consider the local situation, formulate competition methods, and issue orders to your subordinates to comply with them. Furthermore, it is hoped that the handling situation will be compiled and reported as a burden. Sincerely,

Finance - Selling Pressure Suddenly Increases - Premium Falls by Ninety Cents - Stagnant Sales of Spot Goods: Lack of Support in the Market

The gold market fell yesterday due to some parties settling their positions, resulting in selling pressure. There was some support when prices were low, but the final situation was uncertain. In the morning, overseas silver markets were stable in London and New York, with traders claiming that after the market closed, buyers were hanging bids and sellers were offering above 0.0625. Montreux forward silver prices were also stable, exchange rates opened higher but closed stable, and London spot gold was unchanged. The Central Bank's fixing announcement showed that both the pound and the dollar were flat, and the customs gold unit was unchanged. The standard premium fixing price remained at 1123.2 yuan. The market opened slightly lower in the morning. After the opening, large players offered their positions, and there was a lack of support. Although the exchange rates of the HSBC Bank for both the pound and the dollar, as well as the silver equalization tax, remained unchanged, they were still downstream. Although there was a period of struggle in the middle, the buying interest was only temporary, and the trend remained weak at noon. The afternoon market was still weak. Later, large players took advantage of the low prices to buy, and the market was slightly pulled up. The initial decision to raise the Indian silver was one anna, but it was not changed the second time. Finally, the overall trend hovered. The daily market conditions are recorded below:

The morning opening was 1125.9 yuan, down 0.2 yuan from the previous closing. Qingfa, Yongyuanmao, Yongheng, and Yu Futai sold their positions. The HSBC Bank's fixing announcement showed that both the pound and the dollar were flat, and the silver equalization tax was also unchanged. The price gradually retreated to 5.2 yuan. Yuanmao and Yongcheng took large positions, raising the price to 5.4 yuan. Chunyuan and Yongzhen took short positions. The noon closing price fell to 1125.1 yuan.

The afternoon market opened at 1125.1 yuan. Dadecheng and Dingkang sold their positions down to 5 yuan. Tongfu, Futaiyong, Tongfengh, Hengfu, and Yu took positions, gradually rising to 5.4 yuan. Chunyuan and Yongqiafeng sold their positions. The closing price was 1125.2 yuan.

The settlement price, based on the Central Bank's standard premium fixing price, remained at 1123.2 yuan. In terms of the closing price, it was about 2 yuan higher. The registration price for this month was 1122 yuan, and for October it was 1125 yuan. The morning water price was 1122 yuan, and the pure gold price was 8 yuan higher, at 1133.9 yuan. The spot market conditions were stable, and the premium for futures was downstream. The water price was slightly higher, but there were no transactions. The Tianjin goods were priced at 13.75 yuan higher, with a selling price of 15 yuan and a buying price of 12 yuan for boiled water. There are still 672 bars remaining for this month. In total, there are nine long parties and five short parties.

Trading in the market was normal. In summary, Fuyu, Chengda, Hengyu, Huixiang, Yuanmao, Yongjin, and Fengyong Tongfu were on the buying side. Chunyuan, Yongzhen, Dayong, Tongtai, Changyong, Dedingkang, and Shunli were on the selling side. Tongfeng, Hengfu, Taiyong, Qingfayong, and Yuanmao first came out and then came in. Yarn and Cotton - Differing Perspectives of Bulls and Bears - Yarn Market in a Hovering State

The yarn market is calm, with mixed increases and decreases, and the trend is uneven. This is because the bulls and bears have different opinions, each with their own perspectives. The buyers are aware that the inventory of existing yarn mills is decreasing and that customer sales are smooth. However, the bears are concerned that the weather is favorable and the cotton production is abundant, so they are bearish on the forward yarn price and tend to sell.

Posted Yarn Prices Show Mixed Increases and Decreases

At the opening of the yarn market in the morning, the prices for each month showed an uneven picture, fluctuating up and down by three or four corners. This was because after the large traders had hedged and sold the previous day, the market sentiment was dispersed. After the second round, rumors spread that customers of existing yarn still had high hopes for large-scale development, and the market atmosphere suddenly tightened. This month suddenly jumped by 1.3 yuan, but the prices for the far-term contract turned loose and fell back by two or three corners. There were very few transactions in the market. British and Indian Cotton Prices Slightly Rebound - Prices of Three Grades of Yarn and Cotton Show Mixed Increases and Decreases

Yesterday, the US cotton market was closed. The spot price of British cotton fell by 9 points, and the futures price fell by 4 to 6 points. The price of Indian cotton initially rose due to short covering and limited transactions. Dealers were generally taking a wait-and-see attitude. Later, the price fell due to reports that Gukila and Kaishawah had received beneficial rain. It is estimated that Pinggul fell by 1.5 rupees, and Omra and Bairoxi fell by 2 rupees. The original telegram is recorded on the left (telegram dated 7th):

Also, according to a telegram from Mumbai, the opening price forecast for the 8th was: Bairoxi at 214.5 rupees, up 0.25 rupees; Omra at 192 rupees, up 0.25 rupees; and Pinggul at 156.5 rupees, up 0.25 rupees.

Three Grades of Yarn and Cotton: According to a telegram from Osaka dated 8th, the price of three grades of yarn futures rose by 0.3 yuan to fell by 0.9 yuan, with the near-term contract at 213.9 yuan and the far-term contract at 201.4 yuan. The price of cotton futures fell by 0.1 yuan to rose by 0.15 yuan, with the near-term contract at 65.25 yuan and the far-term contract at 62.55 yuan.

Large Movement of Piece Goods and Cotton Cloth - Tianjin, Guangdong, Shaanxi, and Henan All Adding Purchases - Domestic Allocations Increase Several Times

Yesterday, the posted cotton and yarn market was flat and weak, while the sales of existing yarn continued to be good, and the market situation was quite good. The Tianjin and Guangdong gangs also made large purchases of cotton cloth. The Tianjin gang purchased more than 400 pieces of 11-pound Three Rabbits coarse cloth, 12-pound Three Rabbits coarse twill, 11-pound Cat Eagle coarse twill, and 16-pound coarse cloth from Shenxin, Xinyu, Qingfeng, and other factories from the British firm Jardine Matheson. They also purchased more than 100 pieces of printed straight tribute, serge, and Meiheng and Dafeng thread, serge, and bleached cloth from Lunchang and Hengfeng factories. The two Guangdong gangs were eager to purchase the current-month and next-month futures of fine twill from local factories, and the transactions reached more than 1,000 pieces. The amount of fine twill was consistently lacking, and the market price also rose slightly by 5 points. White coarse cloth, fine cloth, serge, thread, printed goods were also purchased enthusiastically in serge. The demand for printed and dyed cloth from the Shaanxi and Henan gangs was still good. The autumn sales in the nearby areas were booming, and the customers from various inland routes came to Shanghai to allocate goods. The items were numerous, increasing several times compared to normal times, resulting in the wholesale shops for various grades of silk, straight tribute, serge, printed goods, velvet goods, and colored cloth selling very well in recent days. The patterns and colors of each factory were indeed strong and in short supply. The sales of white fine cloth, fine twill, and coarse cloth to local and inland gangs continued to be strong, and the market was very stable.

This Street's Woolen Fabrics Were Once Extremely Prosperous

The sales of woolen fabrics have recently been brisk from all directions. Imported goods from the West and domestically produced wool products have seen substantial transactions. Feathered wool, "Yuan Chang" serge, "Huate" wool, and "Sanyuan" light floral wool are selling well. Sleeve linings of Western cloth, French "Xi Cun," charcoal linings, and both wide and narrow plain camel wool are also enjoying strong market sales. Hat workshops, overcoat workshops, and tailor shops are all showing interest in purchasing. Financially sound firms are still actively seeking out available goods from foreign firms. The foreign firms are also aware of the progress in the woolen fabric market, with prices increasing, leading most of them to be unwilling to sell easily.

Grains: Tianjin Shipped 40,000 to 50,000 Bags of Flour Yesterday; Prices Rose but Remained Weak

Yesterday's flour market showed an initial stability followed by weakness after the opening bell. With no quotations for imported wheat, market sentiment lacked support. However, during the opening, Tianjin shipped 40,000 to 50,000 bags of available flour, which were purchased for 1.60 yuan per bag. This transaction was directly between the factory and the buyer, not a market purchase. Nevertheless, this caused a brief surge in the opening price for the current month, rising by 8.5 fen. October and November also saw gains of 1 fen, while subsequent months showed no improvement. As the afternoon session began, the trend weakened again, as the accumulation of available goods outstripped sales. Some factories began selling off their holdings, leading to renewed market weakness. Prices fell by 1 to 2 fen from the morning's high. According to industry insiders, without a large-scale outlet in the future, flour prices are likely to face downward pressure.

Futures Wheat Trading Was Quiet—Following the Flour Market Downward in the Afternoon

Yesterday's futures wheat market opened with relatively stable prices across all months. With no market for imported wheat and mainland clients mostly adopting a wait-and-see approach, it was difficult for the wheat market to rally compared to rice prices. However, the period for new harvests had passed, and most goods were held by grain merchants and hoarders who were unwilling to sell unless absolutely necessary. As a result, trading slowed, with minimal fluctuations. When the afternoon session began, the flour market weakened again, and with few buyers, prices across all months fell by about 2 to 3 fen. Future trends will likely depend on flour sales. The current wheat market sees stable prices for high-quality goods, while mid-range and lower-quality goods are average. "Kaiyang He Yao Wan" wheat is priced at 4.88 yuan, "Bengbu" wheat at 4.82 yuan (second grade at 4.76 yuan), "Gaoyou" wheat at 4.75 yuan (second grade at 4.70 yuan), "Jiangjiaba" wheat at 4.76 yuan, "Shuixikou" wheat at 4.70 yuan, "Suqian" wheat at 4.82 yuan, "Wuhu" wheat at 4.57 yuan (second grade at 4.52 yuan), "Dongge" wheat at 4.67 yuan, "Sizhou" wheat at 4.85 yuan, and "Dongtai" wheat at 4.85 yuan. Fuxin purchased 7,000 bags, and Shenda purchased 1,000 bags.

New Rice Shipments Arrive Daily—Prices Declined Steadily from Yesterday's Opening

(Shanghai South) Yesterday, shipments from various regions totaled seventeen or eighteen, amounting to 3,600 to 3,700 shi. Retail sales remained sluggish, and bulk buyers from Dalian and Qingdao only purchased over 900 bags, making it difficult for the market to rally. Thick early japonica rice prices continued to fall by several fen to 1 jiao, while thin indica rice was stable in bulk purchases and continued to see slight reductions in retail sales. Although Dongxin japonica rice prices stabilized, lower-quality rice from Hebei depreciated by several fen. New "Du Yang Jian" and similar varieties experienced similar price movements. Overall, with new goods arriving daily, prospects are not promising.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, shipments from various regions of Hebei arrived at more than twenty locations. Sales of white japonica and thin indica rice were normal, while aged "Yangfu Jian" rice was average. New "Yang Tuan Jian" rice saw slight price adjustments, while "Bian Yuan Xin Ke Jian" rice was flat. Market prices showed stable prices for white japonica new "Bu Jian" and "Dongxin" japonica rice. Aged "Yang Jian," "Bian Yuan," thin indica, and new "Tuan Jian" rice were weak by several fen. New "Yang Jian" rice prices fell by 1 to 2 jiao, and new "Ke Jian" rice prices fell by nearly 1 jiao. Yesterday, over 10 shi of new Kunshan japonica rice arrived, with excellent quality, and an opening price of 10 yuan.

Early Indica Rice Abundant, Prices Weak—Shanghai Market Down Over 0.2 Yuan Yesterday

Yesterday, shipments of early indica rice continued to flood in from various regions along the Yangtze River. Polished rice arrivals were even more abundant due to active sales to Guangdong in the previous month. Market inventories are gradually filling up, and with recent sales to Guangdong slowing down, purchasing prices are particularly tight. Merchants and owners, noting the abundance of goods and falling prices in producing areas, were keen to reduce prices and sell quickly. As a result, polished rice prices suddenly fell by 0.2 to 0.25 yuan. Mechanically milled rice also fell by 0.05 to 0.1 yuan. Despite the price drop, digestion of stock was still happening. Guangdong buyers made some small purchases of polished rice. Daily transactions included 3,025 bags of Jiangxi rice, 6,300 bags of Hunan rice, 158 bags of Beijing polished rice, and 108 bags of Hanzuo rice. Purchases were mainly from this street, with some participation from Ningbo, Shantou, and northern regions.

New Sesame Seeds Gradually Enter the Market—Hoping Producing Areas Will Not Adulterate with Mud and Ash

This year's new sesame seeds from various regions are entering the market earlier than in previous years. The harvest is also expected to be optimistic, with good quality. However, it is hoped that producing areas will not adulterate the seeds with mud and ash, as this year's sales depend entirely on foreign markets. Therefore, in the international arena, it is essential to maintain the reputation of our country's agricultural products and avoid being despised for greed. Yesterday's transactions included 300 bags of new Shashi sesame at 10.09 yuan, 18 bags of new Guide sesame at 10.055 yuan, 35 bags of new Nanjing sesame at 9.06 yuan, 20 bags of new Suzhou sesame at 9.015 yuan, and 53 bags of new Yangzhou sesame at 9.03 yuan and 9.01 yuan. The current upward trend is due to new goods being traded and the weakness of foreign firms, so the future is likely to suffer. Yesterday, foreign firms dumped 450 tons at 11.082 yuan per original package.

Grain Price Statistics for August (2)

Silk and Tea: Shanghai Silk Market Still Relies on End Users

Yesterday, New York was closed for Labor Day, so there was no market. The Lyon silk market remained stable. In Binjiang, it was learned that this year's autumn cocoons had a poor harvest (a 10% reduction in production compared to last year), so silk prices slightly increased, with spot prices rising by 3 yuan and futures prices by 11 yuan. The Shanghai silk market remained active, driven by end users, but prices showed no improvement. Yesterday, ordinary B-grade silk fell below the 600 yuan mark, but sales remained strong. Yesterday, foreign firms and end users purchased a total of 158 bales.

Red Tea from Hunan and Hubei Plummeted

According to news from Hankou, this year's total red tea production in Hunan and Hubei provinces is 230,000 chests. More than 100,000 chests were previously purchased by British firms Jardine Matheson and Concordia, as well as Soviet tea buying organizations, and the market was in good condition. Recently, the market has been severely impacted by the low-priced competition from Indian and Ceylon tea. Sales have been sluggish for the past two weeks, with inventories piling up to 80,000 chests. Red tea prices have plummeted to 21-22 yuan, and floral-scented teas have fallen to around 10 yuan, making the market situation extremely unfavorable.

According to the Tea Industry Association's report, green tea sales were brisk last week but have been quieter this week. In the past two days, only Longjin and Suizhen have sold over 300 chests at 50 yuan and 51 yuan, respectively. Concordia has made small purchases of Tezhen and Xiaozhen eyebrow tea, and Tongfu and Fushi have also made small transactions for Tezhen. It is also heard that Longjin is negotiating for over 200 chests of Tezhen, which may be concluded within days. Ping Shui tea remains quiet, but Jinlong continues to make transactions of disassembled shipments.

Dried and Preserved Goods: New Red Dates and Longans Have Arrived in Shanghai; One More Longan Company—Bao Da

The first batch of new Jixin red dates was shipped from Zhenjiang by shipping companies yesterday, totaling over 300 bags. Samples have already been shown, and the goods are of good quality. Prices are currently being negotiated, so they have not been released yet. New longans arrived via the Taiyuan steamer yesterday in a second batch, with over 1,300 pieces from Tong'an, Zhangzhou, and Anhai. Samples of the larger pieces will be available tomorrow or the day after. Prices are not expected to fluctuate significantly. Industry sources also report that people from the financial sector and a certain longan company have formed a new Bao Da Longan Company, managed by Mr. Yuan Chunfa. The company has joined the industry association and will begin operations immediately.

Sugar Market: New Dutch Red Sugar Sold Out Yesterday

Yesterday, there was little movement in the sugar market. The exchange set prices, with No. 24 coarse white sugar and No. 489 East White sugar maintaining their original prices. The price of No. 1 refined white sugar from this factory remained at 20.5 yuan. However, the newly arrived No. 89 New Dutch Red sugar, which arrived the day before yesterday, was sold out yesterday at 6.05 yuan. The exchange prices were stable, and few transactions were made. It is rumored that merchants are considering continuing to purchase Chaoqing sugar from Shantou, so the future market is unlikely to ease.
