Spring and Autumn

Snippets

— (Chen Yunsu)

Those who become university professors often yearn for the dignity of a university president; once the title of university president is bestowed upon them, they immediately crave to experience being the Minister of Education; and once they seize the seal of the Minister of Education, they never think of their old lives again. What is this called? The former is called 'wanting more after getting Shu', and the latter is called 'being so happy as to forget Shu'. Both are undesirable!

Friends perched atop towers should look down at the lost sheep below and try to point out their path, so they too may have the possibility of climbing up.

Some say that the current cramming education is not for the sake of students' substantial knowledge, nor for their future prospects, but solely to cope with exams, spot checks, and superiors' praises. This is just like those who feed ducks; their aim is not for the ducks themselves to be plump, but for those gluttons who eat duck meat!

Doing things is like eating snacks. Snacks should be chosen to our liking, and work should be chosen to be close to our nature. Only by eating in this way will it suit our appetite, and only by working in this way will it be meaningful. Otherwise, the body will certainly not be comfortable, and there will be no progress in the career.

Philosophy of Running a School

— Shijiu

The "school" mentioned here is a private school. Running a private school is different from running a provincial school. Different sources of funding and different enrollment methods are the two most obvious differences; therefore, running a private school has its own secrets.

If we compare schools to shops, then students are the customers. There are certainly private schools that treat everyone equally; however, those that recruit students with "big discounts" are also commonly seen. The so-called "big discounts" do not mean reducing tuition fees; rather, it means accepting everyone who comes, regardless of their qualifications, which is a wonderful method for absorbing currency.

After customers enter the door, they cannot be easily let go, so it is important to know how to retain them. What is the method of retaining them? Management may be lenient, and homework need not be taken seriously. An official of a certain school—no, the owner—once expressed his school management policy, saying: "The more students, the better; the fewer students repeating grades, the better." This is indeed a profound understanding of the essence of the matter. As for the school's reputation, it must naturally be taken care of; therefore, the owner of a certain school also successively invented the method of being lenient first and then strict, that is, allowing students to pass the first few semesters carelessly in order to absorb currency, but then suddenly tightening up on students in the last semester, eliminating the dross and retaining the essence. Naturally, they can cope with the exams and everyone will "pass," and the school's reputation will naturally improve day by day.

Inspections by the superintendent of schools are not something to be trifled with; however, they can be dealt with. Usually, plant more flowers and trees in the school, and temporarily whitewash all the walls. Then, order the students to strictly maintain order. Naturally, the superintendent will have a feeling of relaxation and happiness, or perhaps he can win a commendation, and the whole school will smile with joy.

Private school owners who want to keep their jobs also have a secret: when the board of directors invites them three times, instead of being flattered and surprised, it is better to put on a slight show of pride. By putting on a slight show of pride, you can secure a longer contract. With a longer contract, can't you act arbitrarily and treat the school as your private property!

Lovers

— Hualing

In ancient times, it was considered a virtue for women to stay at home and avoid social interaction; in modern times, it is considered fashionable for women to be good at socializing with men. Therefore, in the past, even when men and women walked together, they were always one in front and one behind, with a distance of three to five feet between them. Now, when men and women walk together, they are always arm in arm, leaning on each other, with an air of intimacy, not at all avoiding the eyes of strangers. Moralists regard this modern behavior, which goes against the principle of not allowing men and women to touch each other, as a sign of declining morality. However, modern men and women claim to be "lovers."

During the summer vacation, it is the most active period for lovers. If you happen to step into a park, you will find it filled with pairs of men and women in the woods, by the ponds, and everywhere else. These are the lovers. By the poolsides and on the beaches of swimming pools and seaside resorts, under the colorful parasols, you will find pairs of men and women. These are naturally also lovers. In air-conditioned cinemas, in the last few rows of seats, you will find pairs of men and women, whispering and laughing teasingly in the dark space where the movie is playing. These are the lovers. In high-class dance halls that do not provide dance partners, under the dim green lights, you will find pairs of men and women, their faces close together, their chests touching, their toes touching, dancing to the music. Among them, there are certainly many who are lovers. In the evenings after dinner, on the sidewalks under the tall French parasol trees, in the gentle breeze, you will find even more lovers strolling slowly, talking and laughing, arm in arm. "Lovers" have become the most poetic decoration in big cities.

If marriage is the tomb of love, then I think the lover period should be considered the bud of love. On the faces of pairs of lovers, there is a genuine and innocent smile. The passion in their hearts bursts forth and is revealed on the corners of their lips. Everyone forgets everything else besides love, forgets all the sorrows and pains of the world. What every lover feels is, "In my heart, there is only you; in your heart, there is only me."

However, there is no bud that does not bloom, so most lovers in the world end in marriage. There is also a small portion that is hit and destroyed by the external forces of storms. Marriage is the tomb of love, and a bud that is destroyed by storms is even more likely to end in tragedy. Therefore, I wish the pairs of lovers I see would savor the sweetness of your lover period as much as possible. The lover period is truly the golden period of your lifelong love life. Hold on to it tightly, and don't let it escape lightly.

Monk Beans

— Junmei

In our Jiangzhe area, beans seem to be a popular food. Different methods of stir-frying, stewing, and simmering produce various individual names and flavors, such as loose and crispy sand-fried beans, sweet and fragrant spiced beans, and salty and hard fried salt beans. However, the most popular are the soft, tender, and greasy monk beans.

It is said that monk beans were created by Su Dongpo. The green beans are peeled on one end, soaked in water to plump them up, and then stewed with salty ingredients. They are cooked through in just one mealtime. They can be eaten with wine or as a side dish, melting in your mouth. Like watermelon seeds and peanuts, people can't get enough of them and don't want to stop. Spiced beans and sand-fried beans also have their own unique flavors, but they always have some elasticity and resistance. However, although it can be welcomed by eaters, it is only a weak person who sacrifices himself for people to chew!

If we use a monk bean to symbolize our ancient country and nation, then fried salt beans can be compared to Abyssinia, because it, after all, gives the teeth more resistance. If you are not careful, you will have to break your gums and bite your tongue. Although it is finally swallowed, it also leaves some residue, some burnt skin chips, embedded in the teeth to make trouble, giving the eater a great discomfort. When you want to get your hands on it, your hands will also get greasy. Monk beans are not like that. They are just obedient and docile. Under the power of the tip of the tongue, the skin and flesh have melted, and there are no crumbs left. This is also very sad!

But our beans are already destined to be beans. We only hope that those in charge of cooking will cook more fried salt beans, and don't just cater to people's tastes, soaking them fat and soft, so that people can also feel inconvenient and know what to be wary of.

Phoenixes Replaced in the Nest

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Six: Iron Face Sees Close Hearts, Words Deceive Parrots; Moth Eyebrows Preserve Chivalry, Asks About the Classics of Kunlun

At this time, dinner had already been brought to the table, interrupting the conversation between mother and daughter. Menglan stopped mentioning it, and in order to dispel her mother's suspicion, she cheered up and ate a bowl and a half of rice. After dinner, she sat in her mother's room for half an hour before returning to her room upstairs. It happened to be a Sunday. Although she was very willing to go out for a walk to relieve her boredom, her body was tired and she couldn't muster any energy. Therefore, she just piled a few magazines on the table and casually flipped through them. Just as she was getting interested in reading, suddenly two hands reached out and covered her eyes. Raising her hand to feel those two hands, she only felt that they were soft and there was a ring. So she smiled and said, "I guessed it right away, you are Li Youmei." The person put down her hand and smiled, "How did you know it was me?" Menglan stood up and smiled, "Such a big girl, still so naughty. You look like Xue Baochai, and your personality is like Shi Xiangyun. You are a beauty who combines both perfections." Youmei laughed and said, "You're still talking about people. You don't study the proper books and only secretly read 'Dream of the Red Chamber' at home." Saying that, she took Menglan's hand and sat down on the edge of the bed together. Menglan saw that she was wearing a light red silk jacket, with a long blue lake-colored skirt underneath, and a pair of white cloth shoes were exposed. Her plump skin was exposed in the cuffs, which was really cute. She also had a long, round face, big eyes, and two red blushes on her cheeks, which harmonized beautifully with her black, oily hair. She suddenly laughed and said, "What are you looking at me for?" Menglan said, "Summer is coming soon, you will look even better when you take off your clothes." Youmei smiled and said, "If you like to watch, then watch." I heard Auntie say that you have been very uncomfortable these days, how come you are so happy when you see me?" Menglan couldn't help but sigh when she heard this. Youmei held one of her hands and said, "So, you really have something that is making you unhappy. What is it for?" Menglan said, "There is no way to say." Saying that, she shook her head twice. Youmei said, "We are such good friends, you shouldn't hide anything from me. I am the most nosy person, maybe the thing that you feel is difficult, just happens to be something that I can help with." When Menglan heard this, she couldn't help but suddenly stand up, looked at her face and said, "What, you can help me? How can you help me?" When she said this, her face turned red. The blush rose very fiercely, as if it did not belong to the aspect of shyness. Youmei said, "You haven't said what the difficulty is, how can I say that I can help you." Menglan said, "Because you said that you can just help, I suspect that you know what my difficulty is." Youmei smiled and said, "That's you misunderstanding my meaning. I thought that your matter, maybe you can use me." Menglan stopped mentioning this. She sat down on the chair at the table, supported her head with her hand, and sighed slightly. (72)

The National Army's Broadsword Brigade and the Old Wang Mazi Store in the Former Capital (Part 2)

— Bingyuan

I once heard a military expert say that among the daredevil teams in the various armies of our country, the one affiliated with the Northwest Army led by General Feng Huanzhang was always the most highly regarded. Its training, skills, and combat strength should all be second to none. The team members were all selected from the strong and robust in the army, receiving individual training, and everyone was proficient in martial arts, with profound fighting skills. Even in unarmed combat, they could withstand the strength of more than a dozen strong men, and it was not easy to get close to them. The knives used by the team members were all made of wrought steel, thick on the back, narrow on the face, and thin on the edge. Although they were not necessarily like the treasured swords of chivalrous warriors in novels, which could cut hair blown against them and chop iron and cut nails, using them to chop off heads and unload arms, coupled with the skills displayed by the team members, was indeed like cutting vegetables and breaking melons.

As for the source of the knives, they did not come from the ordnance factories of national institutions, but were made by the old Wang Mazi ironware shop in the former capital. According to the old Wang family store in the former capital, also known as Wang Mazi Iron Shop, it was opened in Dongsi Pailou and has a history of more than 400 years, famous in the martial arts world for manufacturing the eighteen kinds of old weapons, such as knives, guns, swords, and halberds. It is said that the third-generation owner of the store, that is, Wang Mazi, liked to play with knives, guns, sticks, and clubs in his youth, and later inherited the Shaolin Orthodox knife technique from a famous teacher. Wang was taciturn, did not smile easily, and would stand up for injustice. He especially valued righteousness and trustworthiness. Regardless of whether he was in charge or not, if anyone asked for help in an emergency, he would always respond. His ancestor was a survivor of the former Ming Dynasty, and he was not originally a craftsman. He was quite wealthy and opened the store, not for profit, but with other profound intentions. However, because his goods were of high quality and the prices were low, his business was booming and his profits were abundant. Wang Mazi inherited his ancestor's business and followed the old rules in everything, but he devoted extra research to the manufacture of knives, striving for perfection. Whenever extraordinary people and chivalrous warriors came to buy, he would spare no effort to cast and forge them. Sometimes, he would become friends with the customers and would not accept payment. Over time, his wealth gradually dwindled, and he relied solely on business to maintain the store. Otherwise, Wang Mazi would have become a poor man long ago. After a hundred years of the founding of the former Qing Dynasty, few people in the old capital's society did not know the owner Wang of Dongsi. Because of his generosity and disregard for wealth, his reputation spread far and wide. Later, he became a famous expert in skills and had extensive social connections. However, his appearance was gentle and modest, quite unlike a boxer, let alone a blacksmith. Some said that the son of a worker starts as a worker, and his ancestors and fathers were originally scholars. Wang Mazi was a great hermit in the city, and he was not despised because of his occupation. In his later years, Wang suddenly had an epiphany. Whenever he opened the furnace to smelt iron, he would add a certain substance to the ore. After several refining processes, he would take it to make utensils. Among the utensils, the knife was the most famous, because the knife was the most common item used by martial artists, and Wang himself was also good at knife skills. Therefore, every knife he made was extremely hard and extremely sharp, and those who used it could handle it with ease, which was no ordinary product. It is a pity that our country's habits are such that every invention is intended to be kept secret, and absolutely no one is willing to disclose it. If the descendants are virtuous, they can continue it, but if they are unworthy, they will lose the true transmission. Is there anything in the world more regrettable than this? As for Wang Mazi's method of casting knives, its general outline still exists today, and it is not yet completely unrecognizable, but his descendants do not know the value of their ancestor's lifelong hard work, and only know how to turn to commercialization by cutting corners. Over time, his unique secrets will gradually disappear. Some people say that the knives made by Wang Mazi in the past contained some red gold. The gold is very hard, and the statement also makes sense. Therefore, in the past, all products that claimed to be treasured knives had to undergo more than a hundred days of manufacturing, costing more than a thousand strings of cash. The work was complicated, the capital was huge, and the value can be known. It is not an exaggeration to call them treasured knives.

The knives used by the executioners of the former Qing Dynasty's Ministry of Justice to execute prisoners were also made by the Wang family's old store. Since the Republic of China, the broadswords used by the broadsword brigades in the various armies of North China were mostly ordered to be manufactured because of its reputation. At that time, the broadswords cast by the Gongxian and Dezhou arsenals were indeed not as "hard," "skillful," "durable," and "sharp." Recently, the broadsword brigades in the national army included Han Fuju's troops in Shandong Province and Song Zheyuan's troops in Hebei Province. Not only were the entire teams known as brave warriors, but the martial arts skills of each team member were also extraordinary. Examining their history, they still belong to the legacy of the old Northwest Army's succession and replenishment. The Song's army is the 29th Army that fought hard at Xifengkou.

Short Story

Boasting After Decline

— Chen Liang

Little Tang fell, and since his father's speculative business failed, he lost a financial backing. His friends all witnessed him fall from the towering and luxurious peak of enjoyment, buried in a mud-like life, never recovering. This caused a sigh and criticism from his friends. Some said he was too absurd when he had money, and some said he underestimated money too much before. Although those who criticized him were the same people who had assisted his extravagant spending in the past, and who had encouraged him to run on the road to decline, they now turned their faces.

To a third party, one might sigh at the coldness of human relationships, but Little Tang himself didn't care about this at all. He happened to glimpse his "intimate friend" from two years ago by the fence of the night garden, getting out of a car with a woman and walking into the door. He thought with relief: "The friends I made have finally made a fortune, but why doesn't he come to see me? Oh, I'm really confused myself, wasn't my father's residence auctioned off? ... Walking east and west, without a fixed home, how can he find me?" He rushed forward to shout at him, but unexpectedly, a doorman hit him on the head with a stick.

Only then did Little Tang get angry. He retreated to the dark corner by the fence. He glared at the doorman and scolded: "You blind thing, have you forgotten opening the car door for me before? Don't you recognize Tang San Shao? You are familiar with my Studebaker every night, how dare you hit me, insult me? That friend's uncle is a lawyer..." He stopped scolding there. Little Tang had a new understanding: "Luckily I didn't shout at that friend, my appearance is unsightly, he has a woman next to him, that's too embarrassing for him, an intimate friend shouldn't..."

He told another partner that his friends were all so rich.

Picking up a cigarette butt on the street and sticking it to his lips, he recognized what brand it was. He also told his partner that he had a lot of experience with cigarettes. In the past, he had to have two tins of this brand every day, half of which were for treating guests. At that time, he would throw away half of a cigarette after smoking it. Now, now, it is "a dragon in the sand"! One day... However, Little Tang's stomach didn't approve of his boasting, and started to cause trouble and shout. Little Tang couldn't help it, and put on a pitiful look, "Sir, Madam, please have pity on me..." begging people.

Effective Method for Quitting Smoking that Everyone Wants

— Physician Jia Zhizhong

Once nicotine enters the body, it stimulates the blood to produce countless "platelets." These "platelets" can promote the vitality of each cell, so once you stop smoking, the "platelets" in the blood have no way to stimulate, and each cell loses its dependence and cannot function. The body feels very uncomfortable, and even cannot support it, falling into extreme pain. Those who have smoked for too long are more deeply anesthetized, so the weakness of the body is more severe. Even if you try to quit, you will inevitably give up halfway and fail to achieve complete success. Therefore, the safest method of quitting smoking is to use the nourishing and replenishing method of quitting smoking. The nourishing and replenishing method of quitting smoking can not only reduce the nicotine toxins, but also generate a kind of nourishing power. The various parts that were previously damaged by opium immediately return to their original state, so there is absolutely no pain during the process. The following quitter used this method to quit his fourteen-year smoking addiction, taking only a month or so, which can be said to be a safe and effective method.

Patient Zou Laiyi, from Hangzhou, Zhejiang, is now forty years old. He became addicted to smoking at the age of twenty-six. In addition, his body was inherently weak, so his smoking volume increased sharply. He smoked at least six qian of tobacco every day. The inheritance that Mr. Zou possessed in the past gradually declined due to the lack of control over his expenditure for fourteen years. His economy could not afford his smoking. He had tried to quit smoking once in the past year, but because of the hundreds of pathological changes during the quitting process, he resumed smoking halfway through. This spring, he was introduced by a fellow clan member to use the nourishing and replenishing method of quitting smoking, taking "Reproductive Essence" to increase the antitoxins in the blood, and injecting "Yu Wei Ci Baoming" to shorten the quitting period and reduce pain. In the first week of taking "Reproductive Essence," he reduced the amount of smoking by a quarter. In about four weeks, he smoked less than one qian of tobacco. He took "Reproductive Essence" for about a month, and he quit his fourteen-year-old addiction once and for all. His spirit is now strong, his weight has increased, and his complexion has become rosy.

— Wu Dachao, Bachelor of Medicine, University of Hong Kong Medical School

Prostitutes are the main hub of venereal disease transmission, so people who like to frequent brothels are prone to leukorrhea. The reason is that the prostitute's vagina is unclean. Flavin has the effect of penetrating the membrane and killing bacteria, and Vakxin can increase the body's ability to resist toxins. Whether chronic or acute, it is a good medicine for the symptoms.

Patient Lin Shuncai, from Mudu Town, Suzhou, has suffered from leukorrhea for two years. At that time, due to improper treatment, it changed from acute to chronic. Although he took many kinds of medicines in the middle, they were still ineffective. Sometimes, although he felt superficially cured after taking the medicine, it relapsed in less than a few months. Common Sense of Self-Treatment

How to Save Young Men from Nocturnal Emission

— Doctor Zhou Xiaohan

Although masturbation is not a contagious disease, the number of young men suffering from it is constantly increasing. Almost everyone wants to try it around the age of fifteen or sixteen, but less exposure to pornographic pictures can help to avoid it.

The harm of masturbation, as openly discussed today, has been proven to contribute to neurasthenia and incomplete development. Because after masturbation, a certain amount of seminal fluid is bound to be lost. Moreover, after developing this bad habit, although one knows that it will damage the body and destroy the essence, one cannot resist the physiological stimulation and is willing to be a moth flying into the flame without realizing it. How sad is that?

Nocturnal emission mostly occurs due to masturbation, and neurasthenia is caused by nocturnal emission. Therefore, young men with the habit of masturbation will have a weakened seminal gate. In severe cases, they will have wet dreams at least ten times a month. Imagine, for such young men, it is difficult to maintain good health.

There are various types of neurasthenia, including mental fatigue, dizziness, tinnitus, palpitations, insomnia, night sweats, poor memory, and declining recollection. All of these are referred to as neurasthenia.

Recently, pictorial magazines and popular hygiene books have discussed the treatment of this condition, mostly focusing on stopping masturbation as the only solution. Indeed, the treatment of nocturnal emission requires complete abstinence from masturbation. But, after stopping masturbation, can the seminal gate and the body damaged by nocturnal emission automatically recover? Of course not. Therefore, the point of discussion in this article is to provide more advanced contributions, offering practical and effective guidance on the treatment of nocturnal emission and neurasthenia. Therefore, for those who suffer from nocturnal emission, whether due to physical weakness or caused by masturbation, the first step is to strengthen the seminal gate. After the seminal gate is strengthened, the mind will be firm, and nocturnal emission can be avoided. Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

World Peace Congress

— Me

According to a dispatch from Brussels on the 6th, the World Peace Movement Congress continued its meeting yesterday. After speeches by various celebrities, it passed a declaration and concluded its work. The most important statement in the declaration said that the sole purpose of this movement is to ensure that all nations in the world, regardless of their strength or weakness, share the joy of peace under conditions of complete equality. If any country violates international law and engages in aggression, thereby disrupting world peace, then we should treat it as the sole enemy, and so on. These words are so good to look at and so good to hear, especially for small and weak nations, who find them even more appealing and nod in agreement, ready to applaud loudly.

But looking back, there are many so-called things that hope for and guarantee peace, such as the League of Nations, the Nine-Power Treaty, the Locarno Treaties, and the Disarmament Conference. Have these paper talks ever achieved any real effect in guaranteeing peace? These grand and high-sounding clauses have long become waste paper, trampled on and torn up by aggressors. And now they want to hold this Peace Congress?

Let's not dwell on the past, and look at the present. Germany is building tanks on a large scale, currently has three tank divisions, and plans to increase this to eight divisions. It is also constantly thinking about reclaiming its old colonies. The United States has decided to follow Britain's example by retaining 40,000 tons of destroyers and strengthening its merchant fleet. Japan is actively preparing for war and expanding its aviation education; Britain is recruiting 24,000 new soldiers; France is extending its conscription period; Russia is reducing the conscription age. With this state of affairs before our eyes, can they even hear the call for peace?

When a person is seriously ill, they immediately hire a witch, ask someone to interpret characters, or ask a Taibao to perform ghost plays, but in the end, it has no effect at all. Some countries in the world, seeing that the world situation is bad and that a second world war is imminent, immediately launch a peace congress to oppose war. The result is the same as hiring a witch, interpreting characters, or hiring a Taibao. After the Ghost Festival, various places hold Yulan festivals to pray for peace in a village or township and to bless them not to suffer from diseases. The effectiveness of the Peace Congress is the same as that of the Yulan festival. This is truly extremely boring.

We Chinese people are superstitious, and foreigners are no less superstitious. Just look at the current Peace Congress, which is the same as our Chinese welcoming-the-gods festivals. Why is that? It is also a principle of people calling out to heaven when they are in trouble. In fact, the more they call for peace, the less peaceful it becomes, because the current world is a world where the strong prey on the weak. Only guns against guns, cannons against cannons, airplanes against airplanes, killing each other until the ghosts cry and the gods wail, fighting to the death, can stop it. Assuming that they call for peace and pray for peace, the general aggressors will regard it as cowardice, fear of death, and an opportunity to take advantage of. It is truly encouraging the ambitions of others and destroying one's own prestige, and the devil's hand will stretch out even further to snatch it away.

Therefore, in the current world, only war can stop war, only killing can stop killing, only power can stop power. Therefore, if you want to achieve peace through peaceful means, it will not be possible, and it will be even more dangerous. Those in the world who are dedicated to peace as a means and aim to avoid trouble at all costs can also think about its reasons.

The Story of the Landlady (Continued)

— Yi Yi

I told him what I saw, the landlady's sad face, and he opened his mouth, missing three teeth, and laughed loudly. —— How would you know? You... His laughter was swallowed by a violent cough.

—— Probably three years ago, the old cart driver said after calming down. The landlady's husband died, and she was the only one who took care of the store. But a young woman, looking like that, and having just lost her husband... Think about it, there are many businessmen coming and going. As time goes on, everyone has to say a few teasing words to her. Humph, it wasn't long before another cart driver quietly told me about her secret —— she had been hooked up with a peddler selling local silk who lived in the store. He also said something about seeing it with his own eyes. I didn't believe it at first, but later I saw how affectionate she was with that silk peddler.

This is where the problem came in. That young cart driver wasn't a good guy. I don't know what tricks he used, but he got his hands on the landlady too. Of course, there was bound to be jealousy. One night, that bastard cart driver tricked the silk peddler into the valley and beat him to death with stones —— only I know about this so far. So, that cart driver could eat alone, but people's mouths are always too bad. You say one thing, I say another, saying some improper gossip. The landlady could only pretend not to hear it and be done with it. That cart driver couldn't stand it. Many people probably wanted to fight him out of jealousy. Finally, one night, he ran away with a lot of the landlady's money and jewelry!

The landlady fell into the abyss of pain, and has been there ever since...

—— Isn't she still very young? I said:

—— I often joke with her sometimes, she says she hates men, heartless.... That old cart driver laughed again!

I knew why he was laughing.

He turned back and cracked his whip twice, and the carriage passed through a forest. He told me again:

—— After passing through the forest, and crossing a bridge, there is the famous Qilibu. There is a villa there. I will tell you something about that villa when we get there.

He didn't wait for me to ask him any more questions. He then:

"Get up —— Oh Oh!" He whipped the horse and ran away quickly. … (The End)

Lessons from Autumn Mosquitoes

— Yun

There are two most annoying and terrible things in summer: flies and mosquitoes. These two small animals are produced in dirty places and reproduce extremely quickly. In the countryside, watching a ditch of wriggling larvae turn into winged mosquitoes that fly around and bite people in just a few days. Flies are said to lay eggs. I haven't seen their transformation with my own eyes, but they fly around everywhere in groups, and their reproductive power is no less than that of mosquitoes. Country people are the least concerned about hygiene. When students come to the square to promote fly and mosquito catching, although the children will surround them to watch the fun, the old people will grumble:

"What hygiene, no hygiene, we have lived to this age. Reading books will read out these tricks."

At that time, I was just reading textbooks in elementary school, and I also knew a little about the danger of flies and mosquitoes, but since the adults did not believe these ghost stories, our little bit of newly learned common sense was naturally useless.

Now I live in a big city, and my knowledge of hygiene has also progressed with age. Even if I don't go to the countryside to promote hygiene, I won't let those harmful flies and mosquitoes into my house casually. Once summer comes, I have two necessities in my house: fly swatters and mosquito coils.

But these small animals also learn to be smart when they come to the city. Flies don't fly around in groups, they adopt scattered tactics. As long as you don't pay attention, they hover over the dishes like airplanes incubating eggs, disappearing in an instant. Fly swatters are useless. As for mosquitoes, you only hear their buzzing, and after they bite you, you can't see their shadows. Once you light a mosquito coil, you don't even hear the buzzing.

After the beginning of autumn, the situation changes again. In the countryside, these things have already disappeared. They enjoyed a summer season and are now all rigid. There is no need for fly swatters and mosquito coils to exert their power, and they will fall on the table or somewhere else and die by themselves. But in the city, just when malaria is rampant, it is really puzzling.

Last night, I was reading under the lamp when a mosquito flew around my arm, like an eagle circling in the sky. It was searching for its target, so my gaze abandoned the black characters on the book and followed it in circles, wanting to wait for it to land on my arm and immediately send it to its death. It took a long time, and it gradually flew closer to my arm, but in an instant, it had bitten me, and the mosquito had disappeared somewhere. The bitten arm immediately showed a red bump, very itchy. I immediately applied mosquito repellent, and simply stopped reading, quietly waiting for it to fly back a second time, but it disappointed me until I couldn't keep my eyelids open. When I woke up this morning, I found four or five red bumps on my thighs, which were naturally its attacks again.

This gave me a big lesson: "Hygiene" cannot only be done when you see a lot of flies and mosquitoes. We must be hygienic anytime and anywhere until they have disappeared, so that we may suffer less next year. To put it more clearly, we are not afraid of them flying in groups, but we must pay attention to their sneaky attacks.

Page 20

Snake and the Poor Man

— Rural Dweller

Old Zhang the Fourth loved talking about snakes the most, it seemed he had especially vast knowledge of snakes. As long as he had free time, once he started talking, he could go on for two or three hours, talking about green grass snakes, red rat snakes, black wind snakes, and even two-headed ones, four-legged ones, all vividly brought to life in his words.

I am most afraid of snakes, yet I really enjoy listening to people tell snake stories, and even more so, I often wanted to see the faces of strange and bizarre snakes. For example, the two-headed snake, I have never seen one. A slender snake body with two heads growing out of it, four small round eyeballs emitting light, two mouths with venomous fangs, two blood-red forked tongues, what a terrifying shape that would be. How can a snake grow two heads? I once heard Old Zhang the Fourth talk about it, extremely mysterious.

That autumn, I was staying at my uncle's oil mill in a small inland town. Old Zhang the Fourth was the town's messenger, making two rounds a day, having to get up early and work late. The afternoon was his freest time, when he would either 'lie like a corpse' (sleep) or 'sell words' (talk a lot). There were many letters coming and going at the oil mill, so he often stopped there, leaning his body against the stacks of soybean bags, crossing his right leg, and speaking animatedly. One day he talked about two-headed snakes—"After cutting a snake in half, you must bury it, otherwise, if two head sections happen to be picked up by crows and joined together, they will connect and become a two-headed snake, and they will take revenge."…

This saying was obviously too mystical; I didn't believe it, but I did believe that he had seen a lot of snakes. He had to travel forty or fifty miles of rural roads every day and cross mountain slopes overgrown with weeds. After the Awakening of Insects, snakes appeared on the roads. "One night!" he would often exclaim in alarm: "The moonlight was very bright, and I didn't bring a mast lamp. When it was almost time to rest my head, I was afraid of seeing the desolate graves beside the local temple, so I walked with my head down. Suddenly, there it was, lying across the road like a thick rope made of bundled meat. I kicked it unintentionally, and with a 'whoosh' sound, what do you think it was?…"

"It was a snake, right? How could it make a 'whoosh' sound?" I asked with a look of surprise and doubt.

"…What else could it be but a snake? A black wind snake, it darted away with a 'whoosh' sound, its body pitch black. I was barefoot, and if it had bitten me, my life would certainly not be guaranteed. The teeth of a black wind snake are more poisonous than arsenic. I would have died halfway, and even the ghosts wouldn't have known."

"Why don't you wear shoes? You must guard against snake bites when walking at night!"

"Young master: Poor people, where do they get so many shoes? It's like always owing road debts; even iron shoes would be worn through. I was born with a barefoot fate, and sooner or later, I'll be bitten to death by a venomous snake on the road." He glanced with his bloodshot eyes, then stretched his right hand behind his head, using it as a soft pillow. He yawned and said: "Alas, poor people are destined to walk the road!" This aroused teasing from several oil mill clerks!

"Old Zhang, doesn't your wife know how to make shoes? She can even make embroidered slippers... hehe…"

"Alright, alright, don't embarrass me. One day, when I, Zhang the Fourth, strike it rich, will she, that slut, have the face to see me? Unless I'm bitten to death by a snake in the dark, am I never going to amount to anything!" Then, without saying another word, his eyes drooped, and he fell asleep…

—Counting it, this was already five or six years ago.

This time, I stayed at my uncle's oil mill in the town for a few days again, but I didn't see Old Zhang the Fourth. According to the oil mill clerks, he had suffered from snakehead boils two years ago, and he had never recovered. He became as thin as a living ghost. Later, when the automobile road opened, the town no longer needed him to run errands. He couldn't stand on his feet, so he opened a pier. Thus, in the lonely afternoons, there was no one to talk about snakes anymore. As for myself, I am not as afraid of snakes as I used to be. After wandering around in the city for five or six years, running around for a living every day, on the bustling streets, I saw beggars holding live snakes and begging for money, some even shoving small snakes into their noses and letting them swim out of their mouths, doing all sorts of terrible things to get people to give them money quickly. In the city, poor people actually use snakes to earn a living.

I silently pray; may Old Zhang the Fourth not have sacrificed himself to the venomous fangs of snakes. Perhaps, if I have the chance, I will hear him tell stories again… However, this will probably only be a dream, right?

The Child Without Milk

— Already

The country woman who came from the back room suddenly disappeared, leaving only the child she brought with her crying. She arrived here before lunch. As soon as she entered the door, she put the child down and went out with the sister-in-law's husband and another man, in a hurried manner. She came back for a while at some point, alone. But after a while, her whereabouts were vague again.

Without knowing each other, she was completely a stranger in our family, except for the sister-in-law. Therefore, her movements did not attract anyone else's attention at all. If it weren't for the child's crying, which made us annoyed, everyone would have really forgotten her.

The child cried all night.

The next day, I saw my sister-in-law was very busy: cooking milk cakes, feeding tofu paste, washing diapers, carrying the child in and out, and sometimes humming out-of-tune lullabies, as if she had become a mother herself. At this time, we had discussions: "Who exactly is that country woman from the back room?" "Why did she disappear as soon as she came?" "How can a child who is breastfeeding be separated from its mother?" "I heard that the child was only a little over a month old when it was born."

That night—the second night, the child cried even more fiercely, with hardly a moment of rest. "Waa! Waa waa waa!" The sound was so mournful, like it was hungry and uncomfortable, and like it was sad for not being able to find its mother. My sister-in-law's out-of-tune lullaby hummed again. The more she sang "rock-a-bye," the more the child cried "waa waa."

After being disturbed by them for two nights, I couldn't bear it any longer.

"Sister-in-law! Why does your child keep crying like this? It cried last night, and it's crying again tonight." I tapped on the partition wall with my hand.

"Sir! I'm really sorry. The child doesn't have any milk to eat, so it's been disturbing you for two nights in a row." The back room responded.

"Why doesn't it have any milk to eat? Her mother…"

"The mother went to be a wet nurse."

"Oh!" I was a little stunned: "Then what about her own child?"

"The child? We originally wanted to give it away, but the child's grandmother refused, so we plan to hire someone else to raise it."

"Waa waa waa" "…My little baby" rang out for a while.

"Why is it so troublesome? The mother is a wet nurse for someone else, and the child eats someone else's milk." I didn't quite believe her words.

"It's troublesome, but the family is poor, and there's no other way. This way, we can earn a little money to help with household expenses." She continued: "She is my younger sister."

"Earn money? Doesn't your own child still need a wet nurse?"

"Of course. But wages are high in Shanghai, ten dollars a month, while in the countryside it's only two and a half dollars, much cheaper."

"This way, you can earn seven or eight dollars more a month."

"More than that. Here, there is food and clothing, but in the countryside, it is sent to the wet nurse's home, so there is no need to provide meals."

"Then the child doesn't need to be brought here."

"That's because we're afraid the employer won't be satisfied. Who can guarantee it will be successful in one try?"

I understood everything: ten dollars took away this child's milk, and two and a half dollars occupied another child's milk.

The third night was even more crying. But because it was so tired from crying, it seemed to have fallen asleep for a while.

As soon as it dawned, someone from the countryside came to take the child back. The mother didn't even come to see her once. The sister-in-law gave her a bottle of tofu paste, which was prepared for the child to eat on the way. They left.

Then I thought of another question: Who will raise the child of the mother in the countryside who is being a wet nurse for this child?

The Mute

— Li Xuan

Two farmers were hoeing in the cornfield on the river slope. It was an extraordinarily hot day in June around noon. Although there was a bit of river breeze, the tall sorghum stalks at the edge of the field blocked the wind for those who were hoeing half-bent and stepping backward. The younger one pulled the hoe to the end of this plot, then thrust it into the soft soil, pushed the large reed-woven hat to the back of his head, wiped the sweat from his forehead with his arm, and walked towards the sorghum field. The older one continued hoeing without stopping. He raised his head, saw that the young man had left the field again, and shouted with great displeasure:

"Little Pi, you're resting again?"

"Drinking some water."

Under a small mulberry tree, there was a red earthenware jar. Just as the young man was about to squat down, he:

"Hey, you you... what are you doing?"

Under the sorghum roots in the soybean sprout bush, a person was crawling, with terrifyingly long hair, a tangled mess covering his face, with a lot of grass clippings and dust stuck to it. Underneath the hair was a bare body, and at this moment, he was holding the jar with both hands and drinking water. The young man panicked a little. He was afraid that the person sleeping in the field was dead. This was a human life! He would have to report it to the authorities, pay for the coffin, and give gifts to the village chief... He scurried away in a panic, walked to the sweating old man: (To be continued)

Movie

Postscript of the First Screening of "Carnival Night"

Famous Director's Famous Saying on Lun, Many Stars Devour

The satirical book drama "Carnival Night," directed by the famous director Mr. Shi Dongshan, has been edited and completed. It was screened at the Jincheng Grand Theater on Tuesday morning last week at ten o'clock. Most of the viewers were Xinhua staff and related actors. After a full two hours of silence, seriousness, and suffocation, everyone stood up and stretched wearily, with joyful smiles on their faces. They all admitted that their efforts over the past few months had not been wasted! However, Director Shi was a dozing Kongo, propping his right hand on his forehead, sitting motionless in his seat. Everyone shouted: "Mr. Shi, Mr. Shi: Dongshan, what's wrong? What's wrong?" He then stood up lazily, without a trace of a smile on his face, which showed that he still felt dissatisfied with this film. Sure enough, his first sentence was: "Mr. Lu, I think we'll go to Suzhou tomorrow to reshoot some outdoor scenes!" But after the negotiations, he also revealed a happy expression, greeting everyone and saying: "Thank you for your hard work, ladies and gentlemen. These are just minor dissatisfactions. For the most part, it's still considered a success! It's getting late, let's go to Da Dong for lunch! Let's have a gathering." On the way to Da Dong, he pulled the reporter and made the following remarks; he said: "A film, from the beginning of filming to completion, is painstakingly done by the director; whether it sells well after it's shown is another question that can be set aside. Basically, the business eye and the artistic eye, in present-day China, seem far from reaching a proportional period! As for the criticisms of others, they can also be set aside. Basically, others have their own subjective views, so-called the wise see wisdom, the benevolent see benevolence. But at least before the official premiere, as far as I'm concerned, I must feel very satisfied, this is always worthy of my months or years of hard work, worthy of the audience who have come enthusiastically and paid a considerable price. Therefore, this has become my unwavering proposition, and especially this "Carnival Night," which I adapted from the work of the famous writer Gogol, I hope that in the final screening, there will not be a single shot that makes 'me' feel disgusted." His words reached this point, and the feet of the crowd moved to the second floor of Da Dong: A messy arrangement of tables, after moving chairs, I only answered him with a few simple words: "The current audience, for film knowledge, is indeed a lot of , on your film use more effort, the viewers will certainly also more effort to be identified it! Do not believe it, but watch the film after the premiere everyone's criticisms it's." At this time the clock reported a little: everyone's belly, has been singing empty city plan; So but wait for came, laid upon wolf swallow tiger eat, butchery door big swallow, as you are winter melon cup it, oyster oil beef it, put down a table, only a few seconds, it has wind roll left cloud, under empty dish empty bowl. Indeed, the people who participated this time, nineteen were all "Carnival Night" in the fellow sufferers of the same fate, basically without the need for courtesy and restraint, now let the reporter introduce to make this end: counting the director Shi Dongshan, recording Lu Yuanliang photography Yu Shengsan, starring Hu Ping, Zhou Xuan, Gu Eryi, Jinshan, and Wang Weiyi Shi Chao Yin Xiucen, etc.
